āvasathāt mūtram dūrāt pāda avasecanam ucchiṣṭa utsarjanam ca eva dūre kāryam hita eṣiṇā na atikalpam na atisāyam na ca madhyaṃdine sthite na ajñātaiḥ saha gaccheta na ekaḥ na vṛṣalaiḥ saha pradakṣiṇam ca kurvīta parijñātān vanaspatīn catuṣpathān prakurvīta sarvān eva pradakṣiṇān madhyaṃdine niśā kāle madhyarātre ca sarvadā brahmacārī ca nityam syāt pādam pādena na ākramet amāvāsyām paurṇamāsyām caturdaśyām ca sarvaśas aṣṭamyām sarva pakṣāṇām brahmacārī sadā bhavet vṛthā māṃsam na khādeta pṛṣṭha māṃsam tathā eva ca ākrośam parivādam ca paiśunyam ca vivarjayet nāruṃtudaḥ syāt na nṛśaṃsa vādī na hīnataḥ param abhyādadīta yayā asya vācā paraḥ udvijeta na tām vadet ruśatīm pāpa lokyām vāc sāyakāḥ vadanāt niṣpatanti yaiḥ āhataḥ śocati rātri ahāni vācā duruktam bībhatsam na saṃrohati vākkṣatam hīna aṅgān atirikta aṅgān vidyā hīnān vayaḥ adhikān rūpa draviṇa hīnān ca sattva hīnān ca na ākṣipet nāstikyam veda nindām ca devatānām ca kutsanam dveṣa stambha abhimānān ca taikṣṇyam ca parivarjayet anyatra putrāt śiṣyāt vā śikṣā artham tāḍanam smṛtam na brāhmaṇān parivadet nakṣatrāṇi na nirdiśet tithim pakṣasya na brūyāt tathā asya āyuḥ na riṣyate kṛtvā mūtra purīṣe tu rathyām ākramya vā punar pāda prakṣālanam kuryāt svādhyāye bhojane tathā trīṇi devāḥ pavitrāṇi brāhmaṇānām akalpayan adṛṣṭam adbhiḥ nirṇiktam yat ca vācā praśasyate saṃyāvam kṛsaram māṃsam śaṣkulī pāyasam tathā vāgyataḥ dantakāṣṭham ca nityam eva samācaret na ca abhyudita śāyī syāt prāyaścittī tathā bhavet mātā pitaram utthāya pūrvam eva abhivādayet varjayet dantakāṣṭhāni varjanīyāni nityaśas udak mukhaḥ ca satatam śaucam kuryāt samāhitaḥ a kṛtvā devatā pūjām na anyam gacchet kadā cana anyatra tu gurum vṛddham dhārmikam vā vicakṣaṇam na ca ajñātām striyam gacchet garbhiṇīm vā kadā cana prāc śirāḥ tu svapet vidvān atha vā dakṣiṇā śirāḥ na nagnaḥ karhi cit snāyāt na niśāyām kadā cana snātvā ca na avamṛjyeta gātrāṇi su vicakṣaṇaḥ na ca anulimpet a snātvā snātvā vāsaḥ na nirdhunet ārdraḥ eva tu vāsāṃsi nityam seveta mānavaḥ rakta mālyam na dhāryam syāt śuklam dhāryam tu paṇḍitaiḥ raktam śirasi dhāryam tu tathā vāneyam iti api kāñcanī ca eva yā mālā na sā duṣyati karhi cit snātasya varṇakam nityam ārdram dadyāt viśām pate tathā na anya dhṛtam dhāryam na ca apadaśam eva ca upavāsam ca kurvīta snātaḥ śuciḥ alaṃkṛtaḥ parva kāleṣu sarveṣu brahmacārī sadā bhavet na ālīḍhayā parihatam bhakṣayīta kadā cana tathā na uddhṛta sārāṇi prekṣatām na a pradāya ca na saṃnikṛṣṭaḥ medhāvī na aśuciḥ na ca satsu ca pratiṣiddhān na dharmeṣu bhakṣān bhuñjīta pṛṣṭhatas pippalam ca vaṭam ca eva śaṇa śākam tathā eva ca udumbaram na khādet ca bhava arthī puruṣa uttamaḥ ājam gavyam ca yat māṃsam māyūram ca eva varjayet varjayet śuṣka māṃsam ca tathā paryuṣitam ca yat na pāṇau lavaṇam vidvān prāśnīyāt na ca rātriṣu dadhi saktūn na bhuñjīta vṛthāmāṃsam ca varjayet vālena tu na bhuñjīta para śrāddham tathā eva ca sāyam prātar ca bhuñjīta na antarāle samāhitaḥ vāgyataḥ na eka vastraḥ ca na a saṃviṣṭaḥ kadā cana bhūmau sadā eva na aśnīyāt na an āsīnaḥ na śabdavat toya pūrvam pradāya annam atithibhyaḥ viśām pate paścāt bhuñjīta medhāvī na ca api anya manāḥ naraḥ viṣam hālāhalam bhuṅkte yaḥ a pradāya suhṛd jane pānīyam pāyasam sarpiḥ dadhi saktu madhūni api nirasya śeṣam eteṣām na pradeyam tu kasya cit bhuñjānaḥ manuja vyāghra nā eva śaṅkām samācaret aṅguṣṭham caraṇasya atha dakṣiṇasya avasecayet pāṇim mūrdhni samādhāya spṛṣṭvā ca agnim samāhitaḥ jñāti śraiṣṭhyam avāpnoti prayoga kuśalaḥ naraḥ adbhiḥ prāṇān samālabhya nābhim pāṇi talena ca spṛśan ca eva pratiṣṭheta na ca api ārdreṇa pāṇinā aṅguṣṭhasya antarāle ca brāhmam tīrtham udāhṛtam kaniṣṭhikāyāḥ paścāt tu deva tīrtham iha ucyate aṅguṣṭhasya ca yat madhyam pradeśinyāḥ ca bhārata tena pitryāṇi kurvīta spṛṣṭvā apaḥ nyāyataḥ tathā para apavādam na brūyāt na apriyam ca kadā cana na manyuḥ kaḥ cit utpādyaḥ puruṣeṇa bhava arthinā tris pītvā apaḥ dvis pramṛjya kṛta śaucaḥ bhavet naraḥ indriyāṇi sakṛt spṛśya tris abhyukṣya ca mānavaḥ kurvīta pitryam daivam ca veda dṛṣṭena karmaṇā brāhmaṇa arthe ca yat śaucam tat ca me śṛṇu kaurava sarva śauceṣu brāhmeṇa tīrthena samupaspṛśet niṣṭhīvya tu tathā kṣutvā spṛśya apaḥ hi śuciḥ bhavet gṛhe pārāvatāḥ dhanyāḥ śukāḥ ca saha sārikāḥ gṛheṣu ete na pāpāya tathā vai tailapāyikāḥ uddīpakāḥ ca gṛdhrāḥ ca kapotāḥ bhramarāḥ tathā amaṅgalyāni ca etāni tathā ākrośaḥ mahātmanām agamyāḥ ca na gaccheta rāja patnīḥ sakhīḥ tathā vaidyānām bāla vṛddhānām bhṛtyānām ca yudhiṣṭhira bandhūnām brāhmaṇānām ca tathā śāraṇikasya ca tat āvaset sadā prājñaḥ bhava arthī manuja īśvara saṃdhyāyām na svapet rājan vidyām na ca samācaret pānīyasya kriyā naktam na kāryā bhūtim icchatā varjanīyāḥ ca vai nityam saktavaḥ niśi bhārata śeṣāṇi ca avadātāni pānīyam ca eva bhojane mahā kula prasūtām ca praśastām lakṣaṇaiḥ tathā vayaḥsthām ca mahā prājña kanyām āvoḍhum arhati apatyam utpādya tatas pratiṣṭhāpya kulam tathā putrāḥ pradeyāḥ jñāneṣu kula dharmeṣu bhārata kanyā ca utpādya dātavyā kula putrāya dhīmate putrāḥ niveśyāḥ ca kulāt bhṛtyāḥ labhyāḥ ca bhārata na proṣṭhapadayoḥ kāryam tathā āgneye ca bhārata jyotiṣe yāni ca uktāni tāni sarvāṇi varjayet prāc mukhaḥ śmaśrukarmāṇi kārayeta samāhitaḥ parivādam na ca brūyāt pareṣām ātmanaḥ tathā varjayet vyaṅginīm nārīm tathā kanyām narottama sama ārṣām vyaṅgitām ca eva mātuḥ sva kula jām tathā tathā ati kṛṣṇa varṇām ca varṇa utkṛṣṭām ca varjayet piṅgalām kuṣṭhinīm nārīm na tvam āvoḍhum arhasi apasmāri kule jātām nihīnām ca eva varjayet śvitriṇām ca kule jātām trayāṇām manuja īśvara lakṣaṇaiḥ anvitā yā ca praśastā yā ca lakṣaṇaiḥ manojñā darśanīyā ca tām bhavān voḍhum arhati mahā kule niveṣṭavyam sadṛśe vā yudhiṣṭhira avarā patitā ca eva na grāhyā bhūtim icchatā agnīn utpādya yatnena kriyāḥ su vihitāḥ ca yāḥ vedeṣu brāhmaṇaiḥ proktāḥ tāḥ ca sarvāḥ samācaret na ca īrṣyā strīṣu kartavyā dārāḥ rakṣyāḥ ca sarvaśas anāyuṣyā bhavet īrṣyā tasmāt īrṣyām vivarjayet anāyuṣyaḥ divāsvapnaḥ tathā abhyudita śāyi tā prātar niśāyām ca tathā ye ca ucchiṣṭāḥ svapanti vai pāradāryam anāyuṣyam nāpita ucchiṣṭa tā tathā saṃdhyām na bhuñjet na snāyāt na purīṣam samutsṛjet brāhmaṇān pūjayet ca api tathā snātvā narādhipa devān ca praṇamet snātaḥ gurūn ca api abhivādayet anāgatāyām saṃdhyāyām paścimāyām gṛhe vaset mātuḥ pituḥ gurūṇām ca kāryam eva anuśāsanam hitam vā api ahitam vā api na vicāryam nara ṛṣabha hasti pṛṣṭhe aśva pṛṣṭhe ca ratha caryāsu ca eva ha apradhṛṣyaḥ ca śatrūṇām bhṛtyānām sva janasya ca yukti śāstram ca te jñeyam śabda śāstram ca bhārata gandharva śāstram ca kalāḥ parijñeyāḥ narādhipa purāṇam itihāsāḥ ca tathā ākhyānāni yāni ca mahātmanām ca caritam śrotavyam nityam eva te snātām caturthe divase rātrau gacchet vicakṣaṇaḥ pañcame divase nārī ṣaṣṭhe ahani pumān bhavet jñāti saṃbandhi mitrāṇi pūjanīyāni nityaśas yaṣṭavyam ca yathāśakti yajñaiḥ vividha dakṣiṇaiḥ eṣa te lakṣaṇa uddeśaḥ āyuṣyāṇām prakīrtitaḥ śeṣaḥ traividya vṛddhebhyaḥ pratyāhāryaḥ yudhiṣṭhira ācāraḥ bhūti jananaḥ ācāraḥ kīrti vardhanaḥ ācārāt vardhate hi āyuḥ ācāraḥ hanti alakṣaṇam āgamānām hi sarveṣām ācāraḥ śreṣṭhaḥ ucyate anukampatā sarva varṇān brahmaṇā samudāhṛtam yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca yathā jyeṣṭhaḥ kaniṣṭheṣu vartate bharata ṛṣabha kaniṣṭhāḥ ca yathā jyeṣṭhe varteran tat bravīhi me bhīṣmaḥ uvāca jyeṣṭha vat tāta vartasva jyeṣṭhaḥ hi satatam bhavān guroḥ garīyasī vṛttiḥ yā ced śiṣyasya bhārata na gurau a kṛtaprajñe śakyam śiṣyeṇa vartitum andhaḥ syāt andha velāyām jaḍaḥ syāt api vā budhaḥ parihāreṇa tat brūyāt yaḥ teṣām syāt vyatikramaḥ pratyakṣam bhinna hṛdayāḥ bhedayeyuḥ kṛtam narāḥ śriyā abhitaptāḥ kaunteya bheda kāmāḥ tathā arayaḥ jyeṣṭhaḥ kulam vardhayati vināśayati vā punar hanti sarvam api jyeṣṭhaḥ kulam yatra avajāyate atha yaḥ vinikurvīta jyeṣṭhaḥ bhrātā yavīyasaḥ a jyeṣṭhaḥ syāt a bhāgaḥ ca niyamyaḥ rājabhiḥ ca saḥ nikṛtī hi naraḥ lokān pāpān gacchati asaṃśayam sarva anarthaḥ kule yatra jāyate pāpa pūruṣaḥ sarve ca api vikarma sthāḥ bhāgam na arhanti sodarāḥ na a pradāya kaniṣṭhebhyaḥ jyeṣṭhaḥ kurvīta yautakam anujam hi pituḥ dāyaḥ jaṅghā śrama phalaḥ adhvagaḥ bhrātṝṇām avibhaktānām utthānam api ced saha na putra bhāgam viṣamam pitā dadyāt katham cana na jyeṣṭhān avamanyeta duṣkṛtaḥ su kṛtaḥ api vā daśa ācāryān upādhyāya upādhyāyān pitā daśa daśa ca eva pitṝn mātā sarvām vā pṛthivīm api gauraveṇa abhibhavati nā asti mātṛ samaḥ guruḥ mātā garīyasī yat ca tena etām manyate janaḥ jyeṣṭhaḥ bhrātā pitṛ samaḥ mṛte pitari bhārata sa hi eṣām vṛtti dātā syāt sa ca etān paripālayet śarīram etau sṛjataḥ pitā mātā ca bhārata ācārya śāstā yā jātiḥ sā satyā sā ajarā amarā jyeṣṭhā mātṛ samā ca api bhaginī bharata ṛṣabha bhrātuḥ bhāryā ca tadvat syāt yasyāḥ bālye stanam pibet yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca sarveṣām eva varṇānām mlecchānām ca pitāmaha brahma kṣatreṇa niyamāḥ cartavyāḥ iti naḥ śrutam upavāse katham teṣām kṛtyam asti pitāmaha niyamam ca upavāsānām sarveṣām brūhi pārthiva avāpnoti gatim kām ca upavāsa parāyaṇaḥ upavāsaḥ param puṇyam upavāsaḥ parāyaṇam upoṣya iha nara śreṣṭha kim phalam pratipadyate upoṣya ca api kim tena pradeyam syāt narādhipa vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ uvāca evam bruvāṇam kaunteyam dharma jñam dharma tattva vid dharmaputram idam vākyam bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavaḥ abravīt idam khalu mahā rāja śrutam āsīt purātanam upavāsa vidhau śreṣṭhāḥ ye guṇāḥ bharata ṛṣabha prājāpatyam hi aṅgirasam pṛṣṭavān asmi bhārata yathā mām tvam tathā eva aham pṛṣṭavān tam tapodhanam praśnam etam mayā pṛṣṭaḥ bhagavān agni saṃbhavaḥ upavāsa vidhim puṇyam ācaṣṭa bharata ṛṣabha aṅgirāḥ uvāca dvis tri rātram atha eva atra nirdiṣṭam puruṣa ṛṣabha vaiśya śūdrau tu yau mohāt upavāsam prakurvate tri rātram dvis tri rātram vā tayoḥ puṣṭiḥ na vidyate caturtha bhakta kṣapaṇam vaiśya śūdre vidhīyate pañcamyām ca eva ṣaṣṭhyām ca paurṇamāsyām ca bhārata kṣamāvān rūpa saṃpannaḥ śrutavān ca eva jāyate yajiṣṇuḥ pañcamīm ṣaṣṭhīm kṣapet yaḥ bhojayet dvijān aṣṭamīm atha kaunteya śuklapakṣe caturdaśīm mārgaśīrṣam tu yaḥ māsam eka bhaktena saṃkṣipet sarva kalyāṇa saṃpūrṇaḥ sarva oṣadhi samanvitaḥ kṛṣi bhāgī bahu dhanaḥ bahu putraḥ ca jāyate subhagaḥ darśanīyaḥ ca yaśaḥ bhāgī ca jāyate strīṣu vallabha tām yāti vaśyāḥ ca asya bhavanti tāḥ naraḥ vā yadi vā nārī jñātīnām śreṣṭha tām vrajet jyeṣṭhā mūlam tu yaḥ māsam eka bhaktena saṃkṣapet aiśvaryam atulam śreṣṭham pumān strī vā abhijāyate āṣāḍham eka bhaktena sthitvā māsam atandritaḥ śrāvaṇam niyataḥ māsam eka bhaktena yaḥ kṣapet yatra tatra abhiṣekeṇa yujyate jñāti vardhanaḥ prauṣṭhapadam tu yaḥ māsam ekāhāraḥ bhavet naraḥ prajāvān vāhana āḍhyaḥ ca bahu putraḥ ca jāyate kārttikam tu naraḥ māsam yaḥ kuryāt eka bhojanam śūraḥ ca bahu bhāryaḥ ca kīrtimān ca eva jāyate iti māsāḥ nara vyāghra kṣapatām parikīrtitāḥ tithīnām niyamāḥ ye tu śṛṇu tān api pārthiva gavāḍhyaḥ bahu putraḥ ca dīrgha āyuḥ ca sa jāyate māsi māsi trirātrāṇi kṛtvā varṣāṇi dvādaśa gaṇa ādhipatyam prāpnoti niḥsapatnam anāvilam ete tu niyamāḥ sarve kartavyāḥ śaradaḥ daśa yaḥ tu prātar tathā sāyam bhuñjānaḥ na antarā pibet ṣaḍbhiḥ sa varṣaiḥ nṛpate sidhyate na atra saṃśayaḥ agniṣṭomasya yajñasya phalam prāpnoti mānavaḥ adhivāse saḥ apsarasām nṛtya gīta vinādite tapta kāñcana varṇa ābham vimānam adhirohati pūrṇam varṣa sahasram tu brahma loke mahīyate tad kṣayāt iha ca āgamya māhātmyam pratipadyate yaḥ tu saṃvatsaram pūrṇam ekāhāraḥ bhavet naraḥ tad kṣayāt iha ca āgamya māhātmyam pratipadyate yaḥ tu saṃvatsaram pūrṇam caturtham bhaktam aśnute ahiṃsā nirataḥ nityam satya vāc niyata indriyaḥ triṃśat varṣa sahasrāṇi svarge ca sa mahīyate ṣaṣṭhe kāle tu kaunteya naraḥ saṃvatsaram kṣapet catvāriṃśat sahasrāṇi varṣāṇām divi modate aṣṭamena tu bhaktena jīvan saṃvatsaram nṛpa gavāmayasya yajñasya phalam prāpnoti mānavaḥ pañcāśatam sahasrāṇi varṣāṇām divi modate pakṣe pakṣe gate rājan yaḥ aśnīyāt varṣam eva tu ṣaṣ māsa anaśanam tasya bhagavān aṅgirāḥ bravīt ṣaṣṭim varṣa sahasrāṇi divam āvasate ca saḥ vīṇānām vallakīnām ca veṇūnām ca viśām pate saptatim ca sahasrāṇi varṣāṇām divi modate māsāt ūrdhvam nara vyāghra na upavāsaḥ vidhīyate vidhim tu anaśanasya āhuḥ pārtha dharma vidaḥ janāḥ pade pade yajña phalam sa prāpnoti na saṃśayaḥ śatam ca apsarasaḥ kanyāḥ ramayanti api tam naram ārtaḥ vā vyādhitaḥ vā api gacchet anaśanam tu yaḥ śatam varṣa sahasrāṇām modate divi sa prabho kāñcī nūpura śabdena suptaḥ ca eva prabodhyate sa gatvā strī śata ākīrṇe ramate bharata ṛṣabha kṣīṇasya āpyāyanam dṛṣṭam kṣatasya kṣata rohaṇam duḥkhitasya artha mānābhyām dravyāṇām pratipādanam ramate strī śata ākīrṇe puruṣaḥ alaṃkṛtaḥ śubhe an aśnan deham utsṛjya phalam prāpnoti mānavaḥ bāla sūrya pratīkāśe vimāne hema varcasi vaiḍūrya muktā khacite vīṇā muraja nādite patākā dīpikā ākīrṇe divya ghaṇṭā ninādite yāvanti romakūpāṇi tasya gātreṣu pāṇḍava tāvanti eva sahasrāṇi varṣāṇām divi modate na asti vedāt param śāstram na asti mātṛ samaḥ guruḥ brāhmaṇebhyaḥ param nā asti pāvanam divi ca iha ca ṛṣayaḥ ca parām siddhim upavāsaiḥ avāpnuvan divyam varṣa sahasram hi viśvāmitreṇa dhīmatā sarve eva divam prāptāḥ kṣamāvantaḥ mahā ṛṣayaḥ idam aṅgirasā pūrvam mahā ṛṣibhyaḥ pradarśitam imam tu kaunteya yathākramam vidhim pravartitam hi aṅgirasā mahā ṛṣiṇā viyoni jānām ca vijānate rutam dhruvām ca kīrtim labhate nara uttamaḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca pitāmahena vidhivat yajñāḥ proktāḥ mahātmanā guṇāḥ ca eṣām yathātattvam pretya ca iha ca sarvaśas na te śakyāḥ daridreṇa yajñāḥ prāptum pitāmaha bahu upakaraṇāḥ yajñāḥ nānā saṃbhāra vistarāḥ pārthivaiḥ rāja putraiḥ vā śakyāḥ prāptum pitāmaha bhīṣmaḥ uvāca yaḥ tu kalyam tathā sāyam bhuñjānaḥ na antarā pibet ṣaḍbhiḥ eva tu varṣaiḥ sa sidhyate na atra saṃśayaḥ tapta kāñcana varṇam ca vimānam labhate naraḥ deva strīṇām adhīvāse nṛtya gīta ninādite prājāpatye vaset padmam varṣāṇām agni saṃnibhe trīṇi varṣāṇi yaḥ prāśet satatam tu eka bhojanam sadā dvādaśa māsān tu juhvānaḥ jātavedasam yajñam bahu suvarṇam vā vāsava priyam āharet satya vāc dāna śīlaḥ ca brahmaṇyaḥ ca anasūyakaḥ pāṇḍura abhra pratīkāśe vimāne haṃsa lakṣaṇe tṛtīye divase yaḥ tu prāśnīyāt eka bhojanam sadā dvādaśa māsān tu juhvānaḥ jātavedasam mayūra haṃsa saṃyuktam vimānam labhate naraḥ saptarṣīṇām sadā loke saḥ apsarobhiḥ vaset saha nivartanam ca tatra asya trīṇi padmāni vai viduḥ sadā dvādaśa māsān vai juhvānaḥ jātavedasam indra kanyā abhirūḍham ca vimānam labhate naraḥ devarājasya ca krīḍām nityakālam avekṣate sadā dvādaśa māsān tu juhvānaḥ jātavedasam alubdhaḥ satya vādī ca brahmaṇyaḥ ca avihiṃsakaḥ anasūyuḥ a pāpa sthaḥ dvādaśa aha phalam labhet jāmbūnada mayam divyam vimānam haṃsa lakṣaṇam sūrya mālā sama ābhāsam ārohet pāṇḍuram gṛham āvartanāni catvāri tathā padmāni dvādaśa śara agni parimāṇam ca tatra asau vasate sukham divase yaḥ tu ṣaṣṭhe vai muniḥ prāśeta bhojanam sadā dvādaśa māsān vai juhvānaḥ jātavedasam sadā triṣavaṇa snāyī brahmacārī anasūyakaḥ agni jvālā sama ābhāsam haṃsa barhiṇa sevitam nūpurāṇām ninādena mekhalānām ca nisvanaiḥ koṭī sahasram varṣāṇām trīṇi koṭi śatāni ca padmāni aṣṭādaśa tathā patāke dve tathā eva ca ayutāni ca pañcāśat ṛkṣa carma śatasya ca lomnām pramāṇena samam brahma loke mahīyate sadā dvādaśa māsān vai juhvānaḥ jātavedasam saṃkhyām atiguṇām ca api teṣu lokeṣu modate yaḥ tu saṃvatsaram kṣāntaḥ bhuṅkte ahani aṣṭame naraḥ kṛṣṇāḥ kanaka gauryaḥ ca nāryaḥ śyāmāḥ tathā aparāḥ vayaḥ rūpa vilāsinyaḥ labhate na atra saṃśayaḥ sadā dvādaśa māsān vai juhvānaḥ jātavedasam puṇḍarīka prakāśam ca vimānam labhate naraḥ nīyate rudra kanyābhiḥ saḥ antarikṣam sanātanam aṣṭādaśa sahasrāṇi varṣāṇām kalpam eva ca koṭī śata sahasram ca teṣu lokeṣu modate sadā dvādaśa māsān vai juhvānaḥ jātavedasam vimānam maṇḍala āvartam āvarta gahana āvṛtam sāgara ūrmi pratīkāśam sādhayet yānam uttamam vicitra maṇi mālābhiḥ nāditam śaṅkha puṣkaraiḥ ārohati mahat yānam haṃsa sārasa vāhanam ekādaśe tu divase yaḥ prāpte prāśate haviḥ sadā dvādaśa māsān vai juhvānaḥ jātavedasam para striyaḥ nā abhilaṣet vācā atha manasā api vā anṛtam ca na bhāṣeta mātā pitroḥ kṛte api vā kumāryaḥ kāñcana ābhāsāḥ rūpavatyaḥ nayanti tam rudrāṇām tam adhīvāsam divi divyam manoharam varṣāṇi aparimeyāni yuga antam api ca āvaset koṭī śata sahasram ca daśa koṭi śatāni ca divase dvādaśe yaḥ tu prāpte vai prāśate haviḥ ādityaiḥ dvādaśaiḥ tasya vimānam saṃvidhīyate maṇi muktā pravālaiḥ ca mahārhaiḥ upaśobhitam haṃsa mālā parikṣiptam nāga vīthī samākulam aṭṭaiḥ mahadbhiḥ saṃyuktam brahma loke pratiṣṭhitam nityam āvasate rājan nara nārī samāvṛtam ṛṣiḥ evam mahābhāgaḥ tu aṅgirāḥ prāha dharma vid trayodaśe tu divase yaḥ prāpte prāśate haviḥ sadā dvādaśa māsān vai deva satra phalam labhet jātarūpa prayuktam ca ratna saṃcaya bhūṣitam deva kanyābhiḥ ākīrṇam divya ābharaṇa bhūṣitam tatra śaṅku patākam ca yuga antam kalpam eva ca caturdaśe tu divase yaḥ pūrṇe prāśate haviḥ sadā dvādaśa māsān vai mahā medha phalam labhet anirdeśya vayaḥ rūpāḥ deva kanyāḥ su alaṃkṛtāḥ mṛṣṭa tapta aṅgada dharāḥ vimānaiḥ anuyānti tam kalahaṃsa vinirghoṣaiḥ nūpurāṇām ca nisvanaiḥ jāhnavī vālukā ākīrṇe pūrṇam saṃvatsaram naraḥ sadā dādaśa māsān tu juhvānaḥ jātavedasam maṇi maṇḍalakaiḥ citram jātarūpa samāvṛtam divya ābharaṇa śobhābhiḥ vara strībhiḥ alaṃkṛtam maṇi muktā pravālaiḥ ca bhūṣitam vaidyuta prabham ṣoḍaśe divase yaḥ tu saṃprāpte prāśate haviḥ sadā dvādaśa māsān vai soma yajña phalam labhet phalam padma śata prakhyam mahā kalpam daśa adhikam āvartanāni catvāri sāgare yāti asau naraḥ divase saptadaśame yaḥ prāpte prāśate haviḥ sadā dvādaśa māsān vai juhvānaḥ jātavedasam sthānam vāruṇam aindram ca raudram ca eva adhigacchati bhūḥ bhuvam ca api devarṣim viśvarūpam avekṣate dvātriṃśat rūpa dhāriṇyaḥ madhurāḥ samalaṃkṛtāḥ tāvat carati asau vīraḥ sudhā amṛta rasa aśanaḥ aṣṭādaśe tu divase prāśnīyāt eka bhojanam sadā dvādaśa māsān vai sapta lokān sa paśyati rathaiḥ sa nandi ghoṣaiḥ ca pṛṣṭhatas saḥ anugamyate deva kanyā adhirūḍhaiḥ tu bhrājamānaiḥ su alaṃkṛtaiḥ sadā dvādaśa māsān vai sapta lokān sa paśyati divya ambara dharaḥ śrīmān ayutānām śatam samāḥ sadā dvādaśa māsān tu satya vādī dhṛta vrataḥ a māṃsa āśī brahmacārī sarva bhūta hite rataḥ sa lokān vipulān divyān ādityānām upāśnute vimānaiḥ kāñcanaiḥ divyaiḥ pṛṣṭhatas ca anugamyate sadā dvādaśa māsān vai juhvānaḥ jātavedasam aśvinoḥ marutām ca eva sukheṣu abhirataḥ sadā anabhijñaḥ ca duḥkhānām vimāna varam āsthitaḥ sadā dvādaśa māsān vai juhvānaḥ jātavedasam dhṛtimān ahiṃsā nirataḥ satya vāc anasūyakaḥ lokān vasūnām āpnoti divākara sama prabhaḥ kāma cārī sudhā āhāraḥ vimāna varam āsthitaḥ ramate deva kanyābhiḥ divya ābharaṇa bhūṣitaḥ sadā dvādaśa māsān tu mita āhāraḥ jita indriyaḥ kāma cārī kāma gamaḥ pūjyamānaḥ apsaraḥ gaṇaiḥ ramate deva kanyābhiḥ divya ābharaṇa bhūṣitaḥ sadā dvādaśa māsān vai juhvānaḥ jātavedasam ādityānām adhīvāse modamānaḥ vaset ciram pañcaviṃśe tu divase yaḥ prāśet eka bhojanam sadā dvādaśa māsān tu puṣkalam yānam āruhet rathaiḥ sa nandi ghoṣaiḥ ca pṛṣṭhatas saḥ anugamyate deva kanyā samārūḍhaiḥ rājataiḥ vimalaiḥ śubhaiḥ ṣaḍviṃśe divase yaḥ tu prāśnīyāt eka bhojanam sadā dvādaśa māsān tu niyataḥ niyata aśanaḥ sa prāpnoti mahābhāgaḥ pūjyamānaḥ apsaraḥ gaṇaiḥ saptānām marutām lokān vasūnām ca api saḥ aśnute sadā dvādaśa māsān tu juhvānaḥ jātavedasam amṛta āśī vasan tatra sa vitṛptaḥ pramodate devarṣi caritam rājan rājarṣibhiḥ adhiṣṭhitam adhyāvasati divya ātmā vimāna varam āsthitaḥ strībhiḥ manobhirāmābhiḥ ramamāṇaḥ mada utkaṭaḥ yaḥ aṣṭāviṃśe tu divase prāśnīyāt eka bhojanam sadā dvādaśa māsān tu jita ātmā vijita indriyaḥ phalam devarṣi caritam vipulam samupāśnute bhogavān tejasā bhāti sahasrāṃśuḥ iva amalaḥ sukumāryaḥ ca nāryaḥ tam ramamāṇāḥ su varcasaḥ pīna stana ūru jaghanāḥ divya ābharaṇa bhūṣitāḥ ramayanti manaḥ kāntāḥ vimāne sūrya saṃnibhe sarva kāma game divye kalpa ayuta śatam samāḥ sadā dvādaśa māsān vai satya vrata parāyaṇaḥ tasya lokāḥ śubhāḥ divyāḥ deva rāja ṛṣi pūjitāḥ jātarūpa mayam yuktam sarva ratna vibhūṣitam tatra ca enam śubhāḥ nāryaḥ divya ābharaṇa bhūṣitāḥ manobhirāmāḥ madhurāḥ ramayanti mada utkaṭāḥ divyaḥ divyena vapuṣā bhrājamānaḥ iva amaraḥ vasūnām marutām ca eva sādhyānām aśvinoḥ tathā rudrāṇām ca tathā lokān brahma lokam ca gacchati yaḥ tu māse gate bhuṅkte eka bhaktam śama ātmakaḥ sadā dvādaśa māsān vai brahma lokam avāpnuyāt tejasā vapuṣā lakṣmyā bhrājate raśmivān iva sukheṣu abhirataḥ yogī duḥkhānām a vijānakaḥ rudra deva ṛṣi kanyābhiḥ satatam ca abhipūjyate nānāvidha surūpābhiḥ nānā rāgābhiḥ eva ca nānā madhura bhāṣābhiḥ nānā ratibhiḥ eva ca vimāne nagara ākāre sūrya vat sūrya saṃnibhe pṛṣṭhatas soma saṃkāśe udak ca eva abhra saṃnibhe dakṣiṇāyām tu rakta ābhe adhastāt nīla maṇḍale ūrdhvam citra abhisaṃkāśe na ekaḥ vasati pūjitaḥ yāvat varṣa sahasram tu jambūdvīpe pravarṣati tāvat saṃvatsarāḥ proktāḥ brahma lokasya dhīmataḥ juhvan agnīn ca niyataḥ saṃdhyā upāsana sevitā bahubhiḥ niyamaiḥ evam māsān aśnāti yaḥ naraḥ abhra avakāśa śīlaḥ ca tasya vāsaḥ nirucyate divam gatvā śarīreṇa svena rājan yathā amaraḥ svargam puṇyam yathākāmam upabhuṅkte yathāvidhi eṣa te bharata śreṣṭha yajñānām vidhiḥ uttamaḥ vyākhyātaḥ hi ānupūrvyeṇa upavāsa phala ātmakaḥ daridraiḥ manujaiḥ pārtha prāpyam yajña phalam yathā upavāsam imam kṛtvā gacchet ca paramām gatim acaleṣu aprakampeṣu mā te bhūt atra saṃśayaḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca yat varam sarva tīrthānām tat bravīhi pitāmaha bhīṣmaḥ uvāca sarvāṇi khalu tīrthāni guṇavanti manīṣiṇām yat tu tīrtham ca śaucam ca tat me śṛṇu samāhitaḥ snātavyam mānase tīrthe sattvam ālambya śāśvatam ahiṃsā sarva bhūtānām ānṛśaṃsyam damaḥ śamaḥ nirmamāḥ nirahaṃkārāḥ nirdvaṃdvāḥ niṣparigrahāḥ śauca aśauce na te saktāḥ sva kārya parimārgiṇaḥ sarva tyāgeṣu abhiratāḥ sarvajñāḥ sarva darśinaḥ śaucena vṛtta śauca arthāḥ te tīrthāḥ śucayaḥ ca te sa snātaḥ yaḥ dama snātaḥ sa bāhya abhyantaraḥ śuciḥ atīteṣu anapekṣāḥ ye prāpteṣu artheṣu nirmamāḥ śaucam eva param teṣām yeṣām nā utpadyate spṛhā prajñānam śaucam eva iha śarīrasya viśeṣataḥ tathā niṣkiṃcana tvam ca manasaḥ ca prasanna tā vṛtta śaucam manaḥ śaucam tīrtha śaucam param hitam snātāḥ ye mānase tīrthe tad jñāḥ kṣetrajña darśinaḥ kevalam guṇa saṃpannaḥ śuciḥ eva naraḥ sadā śarīra sthāni tīrthāni proktāni etāni bhārata pṛthivyām yāni tīrthāni puṇyāni śṛṇu tāni api yathā śarīrasya uddeśāḥ śucayaḥ parinirmitāḥ tathā pṛthivyāḥ bhāgāḥ ca puṇyāni salilāni ca prārthanāt ca eva tīrthasya snānāt ca pitṛ tarpaṇāt dhunanti pāpam tīrtheṣu pūtāḥ yānti divam sukham parigrahāt ca sādhūnām pṛthivyāḥ ca eva tejasā atīva puṇyāḥ te bhāgāḥ salilasya ca tejasā manasaḥ ca pṛthivyāḥ ca puṇya tīrthāḥ tathā apare ubhayoḥ eva yaḥ snātaḥ sa siddhim śīghram āpnuyāt yathā balam kriyā hīnam kriyā vā bala varjitā evam śarīra śaucena tīrtha śaucena ca anvitaḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca pitāmaha mahā bāho sarva śāstra viśārada śrotum icchāmi martyānām saṃsāra vidhim uttamam mṛtam śarīram utsṛjya kāṣṭha loṣṭa samam janāḥ bhīṣmaḥ uvāca asau āyāti bhagavān bṛhaspatiḥ udāra dhīḥ vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ uvāca tayoḥ saṃvadatoḥ evam pārtha gāṅgeyayoḥ tadā ājagāma viśuddha ātmā bhagavān sa bṛhaspatiḥ tatas rājā samutthāya dhṛtarāṣṭra purogamaḥ pūjām anupamām cakre sarve te ca sabhāsadaḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca martyasya kaḥ sahāyaḥ vai pitā mātā sutaḥ guruḥ mṛtam śarīram utsṛjya kāṣṭha loṣṭa samam janāḥ asahāyaḥ pitā mātā tathā bhrātā sutaḥ guruḥ mṛtam śarīram utsṛjya kāṣṭha loṣṭa samam janāḥ muhūrtam upatiṣṭhanti tatas yānti parāc mukhāḥ tasmāt dharmaḥ sahāya arthe sevitavyaḥ sadā nṛbhiḥ tasmāt nyāya āgataiḥ arthaiḥ dharmam seveta paṇḍitaḥ dharmaḥ ekaḥ manuṣyāṇām sahāyaḥ pāralaukikaḥ lobhāt mohāt anukrośāt bhayāt vā api a bahu śrutaḥ naraḥ karoti akāryāṇi para arthe lobha mohitaḥ dharmaḥ ca arthaḥ ca kāmaḥ ca tritayam jīvite phalam yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca śarīra vicayam jñātum buddhiḥ tu mama jāyate mṛtam śarīra rahitam sūkṣmam avyakta tām gatam pṛthivī vāyuḥ ākāśam āpaḥ jyotiḥ ca pañcamam prāṇinām iha sarveṣām sākṣi bhūtāni ca aniśam tvak asthi māṃsam śukram ca śoṇitam ca mahāmate yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca annam aśnanti ye devāḥ śarīra sthāḥ nareśvara pṛthivī vāyuḥ ākāśam āpaḥ jyotiḥ manaḥ tathā tatas tṛpteṣu rāja indra teṣu bhūteṣu pañcasu manaḥ ṣaṣṭheṣu śuddha ātman retaḥ saṃpadyate mahat tatas garbhaḥ saṃbhavati strī puṃsoḥ pārtha saṃgame etat te sarvam ākhyātam kim bhūyas śrotum icchasi yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca ākhyātam etat bhavatā garbhaḥ saṃjāyate yathā tatas asya karma paśyanti śubham vā yadi vā aśubham devatāḥ pañcabhūta sthāḥ kim bhūyas śrotum icchasi yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca jīvaḥ dharma samāyuktaḥ śīghram retaḥ tvam āgataḥ strīṇām puṣpam samāsādya sūte kālena bhārata duḥkham saṃsāra cakram ca naraḥ kleśam ca vindati jīvaḥ moha samāyuktaḥ tat me nigadataḥ śṛṇu kharaḥ jīvati varṣāṇi daśa pañca ca bhārata kharaḥ mṛtaḥ balīvardaḥ sapta varṣāṇi jīvati balīvardaḥ mṛtaḥ ca api jāyate brahmarākṣasaḥ brahmarakṣaḥ tu trīn māsān tatas jāyati brāhmaṇaḥ tatra jīvati varṣāṇi daśa pañca ca bhārata gardabhaḥ pañca varṣāṇi pañca varṣāṇi sūkaraḥ śvā varṣam ekam bhavati tatas jāyati mānavaḥ upādhyāyasya yaḥ pāpam śiṣyaḥ kuryāt abuddhimān sa jīvaḥ iha saṃsārān trīn āpnoti na saṃśayaḥ prāk śvā bhavati rāja indra tatas kravyād tatas kharaḥ tatas pretaḥ parikliṣṭaḥ paścāt jāyati brāhmaṇaḥ manasā api guroḥ bhāryām yaḥ śiṣyaḥ yāti pāpa kṛt saḥ adhamān yāti saṃsārān adharmeṇa iha cetasā śva yonau tu sa saṃbhūtaḥ trīṇi varṣāṇi jīvati tatra api nidhanam prāptaḥ kṛmi yonau prajāyate kṛmi bhāvam anuprāptaḥ varṣam ekam sa jīvati yadi putra samam śiṣyam guruḥ hanyāt akāraṇe ātmanaḥ kāmakāreṇa saḥ api haṃsaḥ prajāyate saḥ api rājan mṛtaḥ jantuḥ pūrvam jāyati gardabhaḥ kharaḥ jīvati māsān tu daśa śvā ca caturdaśa biḍālaḥ sapta māsān tu tatas jāyati mānavaḥ mātā pitaram ākruśya sārikaḥ saṃprajāyate tāḍayitvā tu tau eva jāyate kacchapaḥ nṛpa kacchapaḥ daśa varṣāṇi trīṇi varṣāṇi śalyakaḥ vyālaḥ bhūtvā tu ṣaṭ māsān tatas jāyati mānuṣaḥ bhartṛ piṇḍam upāśnan yaḥ rāja dviṣṭāni sevate vānaraḥ daśa varṣāṇi trīṇi varṣāṇi mūṣakaḥ śvā bhūtvā ca atha ṣaṭ māsān tatas jāyati mānuṣaḥ nyāsa apahartā tu naraḥ yamasya viṣayam gataḥ saṃsārāṇām śatam gatvā kṛmi yonau prajāyate tatra jīvati varṣāṇi daśa pañca ca bhārata duṣkṛtasya kṣayam gatvā tatas jāyati mānuṣaḥ asūyakaḥ naraḥ ca api mṛtaḥ jāyati śārṅgakaḥ viśvāsa hartā tu naraḥ mīnaḥ jāyati durmatiḥ bhūtvā mīnaḥ aṣṭa varṣāṇi mṛgaḥ jāyati bhārata mṛgaḥ tu caturaḥ māsān tatas chāgaḥ prajāyate chāgaḥ tu nidhanam prāpya pūrṇe saṃvatsare tatas kīṭaḥ saṃjāyate jantuḥ tatas jāyati mānuṣaḥ dhānyān yavān tilān māṣān kulatthān sarṣapān caṇān kalāyān atha mudgān ca godhūmān atasīḥ tathā sa jāyate mahā rāja mūṣakaḥ nirapatrapaḥ tatas pretya mahā rāja punar jāyati sūkaraḥ śvā tatas jāyate mūḍhaḥ karmaṇā tena pārthiva śvā bhūtvā pañca varṣāṇi tatas jāyati mānuṣaḥ para dāra abhimarśam tu kṛtvā jāyati vai vṛkaḥ śvā sṛgālaḥ tatas gṛdhraḥ vyālaḥ kaṅkaḥ bakaḥ tathā sakhi bhāryām guroḥ bhāryām rāja bhāryām tathā eva ca pradharṣayitvā kāmāt yaḥ mṛtaḥ jāyati sūkaraḥ sūkaraḥ pañca varṣāṇi pañca varṣāṇi śvāvidhaḥ pipīlakaḥ tu ṣaṭ māsān kīṭaḥ syāt māsam eva ca etān āsādya saṃsārān kṛmi yonau prajāyate tatra jīvati māsān tu kṛmi yonau trayodaśa tatas adharma kṣayam kṛtvā punar jāyati mānuṣaḥ mohāt karoti yaḥ vighnam sa mṛtaḥ jāyate kṛmiḥ kṛmiḥ jīvati varṣāṇi daśa pañca ca bhārata adharmasya kṣayam kṛtvā tatas jāyati mānuṣaḥ pūrvam dattvā tu yaḥ kanyām dvitīye saṃprayacchati tatra jīvati varṣāṇi trayodaśa yudhiṣṭhira adharma saṃkṣaye yuktaḥ tatas jāyati mānuṣaḥ deva kāryam upākṛtya pitṛ kāryam atha api ca vāyasaḥ daśa varṣāṇi tatas jāyati kukkuṭaḥ jāyate lavakaḥ ca api māsam tasmāt tu mānuṣaḥ jyeṣṭham pitṛ samam ca api bhrātaram yaḥ avamanyate krauñcaḥ jīvati māsān tu daśa dvau sapta pañca ca vṛṣalaḥ brāhmaṇīm gatvā kṛmi yonau prajāyate tatra apatyam samutpādya tatas jāyati mūṣakaḥ kṛtaghnaḥ tu mṛtaḥ rājan yamasya viṣayam gataḥ paṭṭisam mudgaram śūlam agni kumbham ca dāruṇam asipatravanam ghoram vālukām kūṭaśālmalīm etāḥ ca anyāḥ ca bahvīḥ sa yamasya viṣayam gataḥ saṃsāra cakram āsādya kṛmi yonau prajāyate kṛmiḥ bhavati varṣāṇi daśa pañca ca bhārata tatas garbham samāsādya tatra eva mriyate śiśuḥ saṃsārān ca bahūn gatvā tatas tiryak prajāyate mṛtaḥ duḥkham anuprāpya bahu varṣa gaṇān iha a punarbhāva saṃyuktaḥ tatas kūrmaḥ prajāyate aśastram puruṣam hatvā sa śastraḥ puruṣa adhamaḥ artha arthī yadi vā vairī sa mṛtaḥ jāyate kharaḥ māse caturthe saṃprāpte śvāpadaḥ saṃprajāyate śvāpadaḥ daśa varṣāṇi dvīpī varṣāṇi pañca ca tatas tu nidhanam prāptaḥ kāla paryāya coditaḥ adharmasya kṣayam kṛtvā tatas jāyati mānuṣaḥ bahūn kleśān samāsādya saṃsārān ca eva viṃśatim tatas paścāt mahā rāja kṛmi yonau prajāyate kṛmiḥ viṃśati varṣāṇi bhūtvā jāyati mānuṣaḥ bhojanam corayitvā tu makṣikā jāyate naraḥ makṣikā saṃgha vaśagaḥ bahūn māsān bhavati uta tatas pāpa kṣayam kṛtvā mānuṣa tvam avāpnute vādyam hṛtvā tu puruṣaḥ maśakaḥ saṃprajāyate tathā piṇyāka saṃmiśram aśanam corayet naraḥ sa jāyate babhru samaḥ dāruṇaḥ mūṣakaḥ naraḥ lavaṇam corayitvā tu cīrīvākaḥ prajāyate dadhi hṛtvā bakaḥ ca api plavaḥ matsyān a saṃskṛtān corayitvā payaḥ ca api balākā saṃprajāyate hṛtvā paiṣṭam apūpam ca kumbholūkaḥ prajāyate phalam vā mūlakam hṛtvā apūpam vā pipīlikaḥ kāṃsyam hṛtvā tu durbuddhiḥ hārītaḥ jāyate naraḥ rājatam bhājanam hṛtvā kapotaḥ saṃprajāyate hṛtvā tu kāñcanam bhāṇḍam kṛmi yonau prajāyate krauñcaḥ kārpāsikam hṛtvā mṛtaḥ jāyati mānavaḥ corayitvā naraḥ paṭṭam tu āvikam vā api bhārata kṣaumam ca vastram ādāya śaśaḥ jantuḥ prajāyate varṇān hṛtvā tu puruṣaḥ mṛtaḥ jāyati barhiṇaḥ hṛtvā raktāni vastrāṇi jāyate jīvajīvakaḥ varṇaka ādīn tathā gandhān corayitvā tu mānavaḥ viśvāsena tu nikṣiptam yaḥ nihnavati mānavaḥ matsya yonim anuprāpya mṛtaḥ jāyati mānuṣaḥ mānuṣa tvam anuprāpya kṣīṇa āyuḥ upapadyate pāpāni tu naraḥ kṛtvā tiryak jāyati bhārata na ca ātmanaḥ pramāṇam te dharmam jānanti kim cana ye pāpāni narāḥ kṛtvā nirasyanti vrataiḥ sadā a saṃvāsāḥ prajāyante mlecchāḥ ca api na saṃśayaḥ narāḥ pāpa samācārāḥ lobha moha samanvitāḥ eteṣām eva jantūnām patnī tvam upayānti tāḥ para sva haraṇe doṣāḥ sarve eva prakīrtitāḥ aparasmin kathā yoge bhūyas śroṣyasi bhārata etat mayā mahā rāja brahmaṇaḥ vadataḥ purā sura ṛṣīṇām śrutam madhye pṛṣṭaḥ ca api yathātatham yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca kṛtvā karmāṇi pāpāni katham yānti śubhām gatim kṛtvā pāpāni karmāṇi adharma vaśam āgataḥ mohāt adharmam yaḥ kṛtvā punar samanutapyate a dattvā api pradānāni vividhāni samāhitaḥ pradānāni tu vakṣyāmi yāni dattvā yudhiṣṭhira naraḥ kṛtvā api akāryāṇi tadā dharmeṇa yujyate sarveṣām eva dānānām annam śreṣṭham udāhṛtam prāṇāḥ hi annam manuṣyāṇām tasmāt jantuḥ ca jāyate anne pratiṣṭhitāḥ lokāḥ tasmāt annam prakāśate annam eva praśaṃsanti deva ṛṣi pitṛ mānavāḥ svādhyāya samupetebhyaḥ prahṛṣṭena antarātmanā yasya hi annam upāśnanti brāhmaṇānām śatāḥ daśa brāhmaṇānām sahasrāṇi daśa bhojya nara ṛṣabha bhaikṣeṇa annam samāhṛtya vipraḥ veda puraskṛtaḥ a hiṃsan brāhmaṇam nityam nyāyena paripālya ca tena apohati dharma ātmā duṣkṛtam karma pāṇḍava ṣaṣ bhāga pariśuddham ca kṛṣeḥ bhāgam upārjitam avāpya prāṇa saṃdeham kārkaśyena samārjitam annam dattvā dvijātibhyaḥ śūdraḥ pāpāt pramucyate satām panthānam āśritya sarva pāpāt pramucyate dāna kṛdbhiḥ kṛtaḥ panthāḥ yena yānti manīṣiṇaḥ te sma prāṇasya dātāraḥ tebhyaḥ dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ sarva avastham manuṣyeṇa nyāyena annam upārjitam kāryam pātra gatam nityam annam hi paramā gatiḥ yatet brāhmaṇa pūrvam hi bhoktum annam gṛhī sadā avandhyam divasam kuryāt anna dānena mānavaḥ bhojayitvā daśa śatam naraḥ veda vidām nṛpa nyāya vid dharma viduṣām itihāsa vidām tathā na yāti narakam ghoram saṃsārān ca na sevate rūpavān kīrtimān ca eva dhanavān ca upapadyate mūlam etat hi dharmāṇām pradānasya ca bhārata yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca tapaḥ atha guru śuśrūṣā kim śreyaḥ puruṣam prati sarvāṇi etāni dharmasya pṛthak dvārāṇi sarvaśas śṛṇu saṃkīrtyamānāni ṣaḍ eva bharata ṛṣabha ahiṃsā apāśrayam dharmam yaḥ sādhayati vai naraḥ trīn doṣān sarva bhūteṣu nidhāya puruṣaḥ sadā ahiṃsakāni bhūtāni daṇḍena vinihanti yaḥ ātma upamaḥ ca bhūteṣu yaḥ vai bhavati pūruṣaḥ sarva bhūta ātma bhūtasya sarva bhūtāni paśyataḥ eṣa saṃkṣepataḥ dharmaḥ kāmāt anyaḥ pravartate eṣā eva te astu upamā jīva loke yathā dharmaḥ naipuṇena upadiṣṭaḥ vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ uvāca divam ācakrame dhīmān paśyatām eva naḥ tadā vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ uvāca tatas yudhiṣṭhiraḥ rājā śara talpe pitāmaham ṛṣayaḥ brāhmaṇāḥ devāḥ praśaṃsanti mahāmate ahiṃsā lakṣaṇam dharmam veda prāmāṇya darśanāt karmaṇā manujaḥ kurvan hiṃsām pārthiva sattama vācā ca manasā ca eva katham duḥkhāt pramucyate bhīṣmaḥ uvāca caturvidhā iyam nirdiṣṭā ahiṃsā brahma vādibhiḥ yathā sarvaḥ catuṣpādaḥ tribhiḥ pādaiḥ na tiṣṭhati yathā nāga pade anyāni padāni pada gāminām sarvāṇi eva apidhīyante pada jātāni kauñjare evam lokeṣu ahiṃsā tu nirdiṣṭā dharmataḥ parā pūrvam tu manasā tyaktvā tathā vācā atha karmaṇā tri kāraṇam tu nirdiṣṭam śrūyate brahma vādibhiḥ manaḥ vāci tathā āsvāde doṣāḥ hi eṣu pratiṣṭhitāḥ na bhakṣayanti atas māṃsam tapaḥ yuktāḥ manīṣiṇaḥ doṣān tu bhakṣaṇe rājan māṃsasya iha nibodha me putra māṃsa upamam jānan khādate yaḥ vicetanaḥ mātā pitṛ samāyoge putra tvam jāyate yathā rasam ca prati jihvāyāḥ prajñānam jāyate tathā tathā śāstreṣu niyatam rāgaḥ hi āsvāditāt bhavet a saṃskṛtāḥ saṃskṛtāḥ ca lavaṇa a lavaṇāḥ tathā prajñāyante yathā bhāvāḥ tathā cittam nirudhyate bherī śaṅkha mṛdaṅga ādyān tantrī śabdān ca puṣkalān niṣeviṣyanti vai mandāḥ māṃsa bhakṣāḥ katham narāḥ rasam gṛddhyā abhibhūtāḥ vai praśaṃsanti phala arthinaḥ praśaṃsā hi eva māṃsasya doṣa karma phala anvitā jīvitam hi parityajya bahavaḥ sādhavaḥ janāḥ sva māṃsaiḥ para māṃsāni paripālya divam gatāḥ evam eṣā mahā rāja caturbhiḥ kāraṇaiḥ vṛtā ahiṃsā tava nirdiṣṭā sarva dharma artha saṃhitā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca śrāddheṣu ca bhavān āha pitṝn āmiṣa kāṅkṣiṇaḥ māṃsaiḥ bahuvidhaiḥ proktaḥ tvayā śrāddha vidhiḥ purā jātaḥ naḥ saṃśayaḥ dharme māṃsasya parivarjane doṣaḥ bhakṣayataḥ kaḥ syāt kaḥ ca a bhakṣayataḥ guṇaḥ hatvā bhakṣayataḥ vā api pareṇa upahṛtasya vā hanyāt vā yaḥ parasya arthe krītvā vā bhakṣayet naraḥ niścayena cikīrṣāmi dharmam etam sanātanam bhīṣmaḥ uvāca māṃsasya bhakṣaṇe rājan yaḥ adharmaḥ kuru puṃgava tam me śṛṇu yathātattvam yaḥ ca asya vidhiḥ uttamaḥ rūpam avyaṅga tām āyuḥ buddhim sattvam balam smṛtim prāptu kāmaiḥ naraiḥ hiṃsā varjitā vai kṛtātmabhiḥ ṛṣīṇām atra saṃvādaḥ bahuśas kuru puṃgava babhūva teṣām tu matam yat tat śṛṇu yudhiṣṭhira saptarṣayaḥ vālakhilyāḥ tathā eva ca marīcipāḥ a māṃsa bhakṣaṇam rājan praśaṃsanti manīṣiṇaḥ na bhakṣayati yaḥ māṃsam na hanyāt na ca ghātayet tam mitram sarva bhūtānām manuḥ svāyaṃbhuvaḥ abravīt adhṛṣyaḥ sarva bhūtānām viśvāsyaḥ sarva jantuṣu sādhūnām saṃmataḥ nityam bhavet māṃsasya varjanāt nāradaḥ prāha dharma ātmā niyatam saḥ avasīdati madhu māṃsa nivṛttyā iti prāha evam sa bṛhaspatiḥ māsi māsi aśvamedhena yaḥ yajeta śatam samāḥ sarve vedāḥ na tat kuryuḥ sarva yajñāḥ ca bhārata yaḥ bhakṣayitvā māṃsāni paścāt api nivartate cartum vratam idam śreṣṭham sarva prāṇi abhaya pradam sarva bhūteṣu yaḥ vidvān dadāti abhaya dakṣiṇām dātā bhavati loke sa prāṇānām na atra saṃśayaḥ evam vai paramam dharmam praśaṃsanti manīṣiṇaḥ prāṇāḥ yathā ātmanaḥ abhīṣṭāḥ bhūtānām api te tathā mṛtyutaḥ bhayam asti iti viduṣām bhūtim icchatām kim punar hanyamānānām tarasā jīvita arthinām arogāṇām apāpānām pāpaiḥ māṃsa upajīvibhiḥ ahiṃsā paramaḥ dharmaḥ tathā ahiṃsā param tapaḥ na hi māṃsam tṛṇāt kāṣṭhāt upalāt vā api jāyate hatvā jantum tatas māṃsam tasmāt doṣaḥ asya bhakṣaṇe svāhā svadhā amṛta bhujaḥ devāḥ satya ārjava priyāḥ kravyādān rākṣasān viddhi jihma anṛta parāyaṇān kāntāreṣu atha ghoreṣu durgeṣu gahaneṣu ca rātrau ahani saṃdhyāsu catvareṣu sabhāsu ca ghātakaḥ khādaka arthāya tam ghātayati vai naraḥ khādaka artham atas hiṃsā mṛga ādīnām pravartate yasmāt grasati ca eva āyuḥ hiṃsakānām mahā dyute tasmāt vivarjayet māṃsam yaḥ icchet bhūtim ātmanaḥ trātāram na adhigacchanti raudrāḥ prāṇi vihiṃsakāḥ udvejanīyāḥ bhūtānām yathā vyāla mṛgāḥ tathā lobhāt vā buddhi mohāt vā bala vīrya artham eva ca saṃsargāt vā atha pāpānām adharma ruci tā nṛṇām māṃsasya a bhakṣaṇam prāhuḥ niyatāḥ parama ṛṣayaḥ idam tu khalu kaunteya śrutam āsīt purā mayā mārkaṇḍeyasya vadataḥ ye doṣāḥ māṃsa bhakṣaṇe yaḥ hi khādati māṃsāni prāṇinām jīvita arthinām hatānām vā mṛtānām vā yathā hantā tathā eva saḥ a khādan anumodan ca bhāva doṣeṇa mānavaḥ adhṛṣyaḥ sarva bhūtānām āyuṣmān nīrujaḥ sukhī bhavati a bhakṣayan māṃsam dayāvān prāṇinām iha hiraṇya dānaiḥ go dānaiḥ bhūmi dānaiḥ ca sarvaśas māṃsasya a bhakṣaṇe dharmaḥ viśiṣṭaḥ syāt iti śrutiḥ a prokṣitam vṛthāmāṃsam vidhi hīnam na bhakṣayet bhakṣayan nirayam yāti naraḥ nā asti atra saṃśayaḥ prokṣita abhyukṣitam māṃsam tathā brāhmaṇa kāmyayā khādakasya kṛte jantum yaḥ hanyāt puruṣa adhamaḥ ijyā yajña śruti kṛtaiḥ yaḥ mārgaiḥ abudhaḥ janaḥ hanyāt jantum sa vai naraka bhāj naraḥ bhakṣayitvā tu yaḥ māṃsam paścāt api nivartate āhartā ca anumantā ca viśastā kraya vikrayī saṃskartā ca upabhoktā ca ghātakāḥ sarve eva te purāṇam ṛṣibhiḥ juṣṭam vedeṣu pariniścitam yathā uktam rāja śārdūla na tu tat mokṣa kāṅkṣiṇām haviḥ yat saṃskṛtam mantraiḥ prokṣita abhyukṣitam śuci veda uktena pramāṇena pitṝṇām prakriyāsu ca atas anyathā vṛthāmāṃsam abhakṣyam manuḥ abravīt vidhinā hi narāḥ pūrvam māṃsam rājan a bhakṣayan sa varjayeta māṃsāni prāṇinām iha sarvaśas śrūyate hi purākalpe nṛṇām vrīhi mayaḥ paśuḥ yena ayajanta yajvānaḥ puṇya loka parāyaṇāḥ ṛṣibhiḥ saṃśayam pṛṣṭaḥ vasuḥ cedi patiḥ purā ākāśāt medinīm prāptaḥ tatas sa pṛthivīpatiḥ prajānām hita kāmena tu agastyena mahātmanā āraṇyāḥ sarva daivatyāḥ prokṣitāḥ tapasā mṛgāḥ kriyāḥ hi evam na hīyante pitṛ daivata saṃśritāḥ prīyante pitaraḥ ca eva nyāyataḥ māṃsa tarpitāḥ idam tu śṛṇu rāja indra kīrtyamānam mayā anagha a bhakṣaṇe sarva sukham māṃsasya manuja adhipa yaḥ tu varṣa śatam pūrṇam tapaḥ tapyet su dāruṇam kaumude tu viśeṣeṇa śukla pakṣe narādhipa caturaḥ vārṣikān māsān yaḥ māṃsam parivarjayet catvāri bhadrāṇi āpnoti kīrtim āyuḥ yaśaḥ balam atha vā māsam api ekam sarva māṃsāni a bhakṣayan atītya sarva duḥkhāni sukhī jīvet nirāmayaḥ ye varjayanti māṃsāni māsaśas pakṣaśas api vā teṣām hiṃsā nivṛttānām brahma lokaḥ vidhīyate māṃsam tu kaumudam pakṣam varjitam pārtha rājabhiḥ sarva bhūta ātma bhūtaiḥ taiḥ vijñāta artha parāvaraiḥ nābhāgena ambarīṣeṇa gayena ca mahātmanā āyuṣā ca anaraṇyena dilīpa raghu pūrubhiḥ kārtavīrya aniruddhābhyām nahuṣeṇa yayātinā nṛgeṇa viṣvagaśvena tathā eva śaśabindunā yuvanāśvena ca tathā śibinā auśīnareṇa ca duḥṣantena karūṣeṇa rāma alarka nalaiḥ tathā virūpāśvena niminā janakena ca dhīmatā ikṣvākuṇā śaṃbhunā ca śvetena sagareṇa ca etaiḥ ca anyaiḥ ca rāja indra purā māṃsam na bhakṣitam śāradam kaumudam māsam tatas te svargam āpnuvan brahma loke ca tiṣṭhanti jvalamānāḥ śriyā anvitāḥ upāsyamānāḥ gandharvaiḥ strī sahasra samanvitāḥ tat etat uttamam dharmam ahiṃsā lakṣaṇam śubham ye caranti mahātmānaḥ nāka pṛṣṭhe vasanti te madhu māṃsam ca ye nityam varjayanti iha dhārmikāḥ viśiṣṭa tām jñātiṣu ca labhante na atra saṃśayaḥ buddhimān vai kuruśreṣṭha prāpnuyāt ca mahat yaśaḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca ime vai mānavāḥ loke bhṛśam māṃsasya gṛddhinaḥ visṛjya bhakṣān vividhān yathā rakṣaḥ gaṇāḥ tathā na apūpān vividha ākārān śākāni vividhāni ca ṣāḍavān rasayogān ca tathā icchanti yathā āmiṣam na manye rasataḥ kim cit māṃsataḥ asti iha kim cana tat icchāmi guṇān śrotum māṃsasya a bhakṣaṇe api vā bhakṣaṇe ca eva ye doṣāḥ tān ca eva puruṣa ṛṣabha bhīṣmaḥ uvāca kṣata kṣīṇa abhitaptānām grāmyadharma ratāḥ ca ye adhvanā karśitānām ca na māṃsāt vidyate param sadyas vardhayati prāṇān puṣṭim agryām dadāti ca na bhakṣaḥ abhyadhikaḥ kaḥ cit māṃsāt asti paraṃtapa ye bhavanti manuṣyāṇām tān me nigadataḥ śṛṇu na asti kṣudrataraḥ tasmāt na nṛśaṃsataraḥ naraḥ tasmāt dayām naraḥ kuryāt yathā ātmani tathā pare śukrāt ca tāta saṃbhūtiḥ māṃsasya iha na saṃśayaḥ yajña arthe paśavaḥ sṛṣṭāḥ iti api śrūyate śrutiḥ atas anyathā pravṛttānām rākṣasaḥ vidhiḥ ucyate kṣatriyāṇām tu yaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ vidhiḥ tam api me śṛṇu vīryeṇa upārjitam māṃsam yathā khādan na duṣyati āraṇyāḥ sarva daivatyāḥ prokṣitāḥ sarvaśas mṛgāḥ sama tām upasaṃgamya rūpam hanyāt na vā nṛpa atas rājarṣayaḥ sarve mṛgayām yānti bhārata dayāvatām ime lokāḥ pare ca api tapasvinām abhayam tasya bhūtāni dadati iti anuśuśrumaḥ kṣatam ca skhalitam ca eva patitam kliṣṭam āhatam sarva bhūtāni rakṣanti sameṣu viṣameṣu ca na enam vyāla mṛgāḥ ghnanti na piśācāḥ na rākṣasāḥ prāṇa dānāt param dānam na bhūtam na bhaviṣyati aniṣṭam sarva bhūtānām maraṇam nāma bhārata mṛtyu kāle hi bhūtānām sadyas jāyati vepathuḥ jāti janma jarā duḥkhe nityam saṃsāra sāgare garbha vāseṣu pacyante kṣāra amla kaṭukaiḥ rasaiḥ mūtra śleṣma purīṣāṇām sparśaiḥ ca bhṛśa dāruṇaiḥ jātāḥ ca api avaśāḥ tatra bhidyamānāḥ punar punar pāṭyamānāḥ ca dṛśyante vivaśāḥ māṃsa gṛddhinaḥ kumbhīpāke ca pacyante tām tām yonim upāgatāḥ ākramya māryamāṇāḥ ca bhrāmyante vai punar punar tasmāt prāṇiṣu sarveṣu dayāvān ātmavān bhavet sarva māṃsāni yaḥ rājan yāvajjīvam na bhakṣayet svarge sa vipulam sthānam prāpnuyāt na atra saṃśayaḥ ye bhakṣayanti māṃsāni bhūtānām jīvita eṣiṇām ākroṣṭā ākruśyate rājan dveṣṭā dveṣya tvam āpnute ahiṃsā paramaḥ dharmaḥ tathā ahiṃsā paraḥ damaḥ ahiṃsā paramam dānam ahiṃsā paramam tapaḥ ahiṃsā paramaḥ yajñaḥ tathā ahiṃsā param balam ahiṃsā paramam mitram ahiṃsā paramam sukham ahiṃsā paramam satyam ahiṃsā paramam śrutam sarva yajñeṣu vā dānam sarva tīrtheṣu ca āplutam ahiṃsraḥ sarva bhūtānām yathā mātā yathā pitā etat phalam ahiṃsāyāḥ bhūyas ca kuru puṃgava na hi śakyāḥ guṇāḥ vaktum iha varṣa śataiḥ api yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca akāmāḥ ca sa kāmāḥ ca hatāḥ ye asmin mahā āhave kām yonim pratipannāḥ te tat me brūhi pitāmaha duḥkham prāṇa parityāgaḥ puruṣāṇām mahā mṛdhe jānāmi tattvam dharma jña prāṇatyāgam su duṣkaram samṛddhe vā a samṛddhe vā śubhe vā yadi vā aśubhe kāraṇam tatra me brūhi sarvajñaḥ hi asi me mataḥ bhīṣmaḥ uvāca samṛddhe vā a samṛddhe vā śubhe vā yadi vā aśubhe saṃsāre asmin samājātāḥ prāṇinaḥ pṛthivīpate niratāḥ yena bhāvena tatra me śṛṇu kāraṇam atra te vartayiṣyāmi purāvṛttam idam nṛpa dvaipāyanasya saṃvādam kīṭasya ca yudhiṣṭhira brahma bhūtaḥ caran vipraḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ purā dadarśa kīṭam dhāvantam śīghram śakaṭa vartmani gati jñaḥ sarva bhūtānām ruta jñaḥ ca śarīriṇām sarvajñaḥ sarvatas dṛṣṭvā kīṭam vacanam abravīt kīṭa saṃtrasta rūpaḥ asi tvaritaḥ ca eva lakṣyase kīṭaḥ uvāca śakaṭasya asya mahataḥ ghoṣam śrutvā bhayam mama āgatam vai mahābuddhe svanaḥ eṣa hi dāruṇaḥ śrūyate na sa mām hanyāt iti tasmāt apākrame śvasatām ca śṛṇomi evam go putrāṇām pracodyatām vahatām su mahā bhāram saṃnikarṣe svanam prabho nṛṇām ca saṃvāhayatām śrūyate vividhaḥ svanaḥ soḍhum asmadvidhena eṣa na śakyaḥ kīṭa yoninā tasmāt apakramāmi eṣa bhayāt asmāt su dāruṇāt duḥkham hi mṛtyuḥ bhūtānām jīvitam ca su durlabham atas bhītaḥ palāyāmi gaccheyam na asukham sukhāt bhīṣmaḥ uvāca iti uktaḥ sa tu tam prāha kutas kīṭa sukham tava śabdam sparśam rasam gandham bhogān ca uccāvacān bahūn na abhijānāsi kīṭa tvam śreyaḥ maraṇam eva te kīṭaḥ uvāca cetayāmi mahā prājña tasmāt icchāmi jīvitum iha api viṣayaḥ sarvaḥ yathādeham pravartitaḥ mānuṣāḥ tiryagāḥ ca eva pṛthak bhogāḥ viśeṣataḥ aham āsam manuṣyaḥ vai śūdraḥ bahu dhanaḥ purā a brahmaṇyaḥ nṛśaṃsaḥ ca kadaryaḥ vṛddhi jīvanaḥ vāc tīkṣṇaḥ nikṛti prajñaḥ moṣṭā viśvasya sarvaśas bhṛtya atithi janaḥ ca api gṛhe paryuṣitaḥ mayā mātsaryāt svādu kāmena nṛśaṃsena bubhūṣatā deva artham pitṛ yajña artham annam śraddhā kṛtam mayā guptam śaraṇam āśritya bhayeṣu śaraṇa āgatāḥ akasmāt naḥ bhayāt tyaktāḥ na ca trātā abhaya eṣiṇaḥ dhanam dhānyam priyān dārān yānam vāsaḥ tathā adbhutam śriyam dṛṣṭvā manuṣyāṇām asūyāmi nirarthakam īrṣyuḥ para sukham dṛṣṭvā ātatāyī a bubhūṣakaḥ trivarga hantā ca anyeṣām ātma kāma anuvartakaḥ nṛśaṃsa guṇa bhūyiṣṭham purā karma kṛtam mayā śubhānām api jānāmi kṛtānām karmaṇām phalam mātā ca pūjitā vṛddhā brāhmaṇaḥ ca arcitaḥ mayā sakṛt jāti guṇa upetaḥ saṃgatyā gṛham āgataḥ atithiḥ pūjitaḥ brahman tena mām na ajahāt smṛtiḥ karmaṇā tena ca eva aham sukha āśām iha lakṣaye vyāsaḥ uvāca aham hi darśanāt eva tārayāmi tapaḥ balāt jānāmi pāpaiḥ sva kṛtaiḥ gatam tvām kīṭa kīṭa tām karma bhūmi kṛtam devāḥ bhuñjate tiryagāḥ ca ye dharmāt api manuṣyeṣu kāmaḥ arthaḥ ca yathā guṇaiḥ vāc buddhi pāṇi pādaiḥ ca api upetasya vipaścitaḥ kim hīyate manuṣyasya mandasya api hi jīvataḥ jīvan hi kurute pūjām vipra agryaḥ śaśi sūryayoḥ bruvan api kathām puṇyām tatra kīṭa tvam eṣyasi guṇa bhūtāni bhūtāni tatra tvam upabhokṣyase tam ṛṣim draṣṭum agamat sarvāsu anyāsu yoniṣu śvāvidh godhā varāhāṇām tathā eva mṛga pakṣiṇām śvapāka vaiśya śūdrāṇām kṣatriyāṇām ca yoniṣu sa kīṭa iti evam ābhāṣya ṛṣiṇā satya vādinā pratismṛtya atha jagrāha pādau mūrdhnā kṛtāñjaliḥ kīṭaḥ uvāca idam tat atulam sthānam īpsitam daśabhiḥ guṇaiḥ yat aham prāpya kīṭa tvam āgataḥ rāja putra tām vahanti mām atibalāḥ kuñjarāḥ hema mālinaḥ syandaneṣu ca kāmbojāḥ yuktāḥ parama vājinaḥ uṣṭra aśvatara yuktāni yānāni ca vahanti mām sa bāndhavaḥ saha amātyaḥ ca aśnāmi piśita odanam gṛheṣu su nivāseṣu sukheṣu śayaneṣu ca parārdhyeṣu mahābhāga svapāmi iha su pūjitaḥ sarveṣu apararātreṣu sūta māgadha bandinaḥ stuvanti mām yathā devam mahā indram priya vādinaḥ yat aham kīṭa tām prāpya saṃprāptaḥ rāja putra tām namaḥ te astu mahā prājña kim karomi praśādhi mām vyāsaḥ uvāca arcitaḥ aham tvayā rājan vāgbhiḥ adya yadṛcchayā adya te kīṭa tām prāpya smṛtiḥ jātā a jugupsitā śūdreṇa artha pradhānena nṛśaṃsena ātatāyinā mama te darśanam prāptam tat ca eva su kṛtam purā itas tvam rāja putra tvāt brāhmaṇyam samavāpsyasi go brāhmaṇa kṛte prāṇān hutvā ātmīyān raṇa ajire rāja putra sukham prāpya ṛtūn ca eva āpta dakṣiṇān tiryagyonyāḥ śūdra tām abhyupaiti śūdraḥ vaiśya tvam kṣatriya tvam ca vaiśyaḥ vṛtta ślāghī kṣatriyaḥ brāhmaṇa tvam svargam puṇyam brāhmaṇaḥ sādhu vṛttaḥ bhīṣmaḥ uvāca tyaktvā sa kīṭa tām rājan cacāra vipulam tapaḥ tasya dharma artha viduṣaḥ dṛṣṭvā tat vipulam tapaḥ ājagāma dvijaśreṣṭhaḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ tadā vyāsaḥ uvāca kṣātram ca eva vratam kīṭa bhūtānām paripālanam kṣātram ca eva vratam dhyāyan tatas vipra tvam eṣyasi pāhi sarvāḥ prajāḥ samyak śubha aśubha vid ātmavān śubhaiḥ saṃvibhajan kāmaiḥ aśubhānām ca pāvanaiḥ ātmavān bhava su prītaḥ svadharma caraṇe rataḥ kṣātrīm tanum samutsṛjya tatas vipra tvam eṣyasi bhīṣmaḥ uvāca mahā ṛṣeḥ vacanam śrutvā prajāḥ dharmeṇa pālya ca acireṇa eva kālena kīṭaḥ pārthiva sattama tatas tam brāhmaṇam dṛṣṭvā punar eva mahā yaśāḥ ājagāma mahā prājñaḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ tadā vyāsaḥ uvāca bho bho vipra ṛṣabha śrīmat mā vyathiṣṭhāḥ katham cana śubha kṛt śubha yonīṣu pāpa kṛt pāpa yoniṣu tasmāt mṛtyu bhayāt kīṭa mā vyathiṣṭhāḥ katham cana kīṭaḥ uvāca dharma mūlām śriyam prāpya pāpmā naṣṭaḥ iha adya me bhīṣmaḥ uvāca bhagavat vacanāt kīṭaḥ brāhmaṇyam prāpya durlabham akarot pṛthivīm rājan yajña yūpa śata aṅkitām avāpa ca param kīṭaḥ pārtha brahma sanātanam te api yasmāt svabhāvena hatāḥ kṣatriya puṃgavāḥ saṃprāptāḥ te gatim puṇyām tasmāt mā śoca putraka yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca vidyā tapaḥ ca dānam ca kim eteṣām viśiṣyate pṛcchāmi tvā satām śreṣṭha tat me brūhi pitāmaha bhīṣmaḥ uvāca atrā api udāharanti imam itihāsam purātanam maitreyasya ca saṃvādam kṛṣṇadvaipāyanasya ca kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ rājan ajñāta caritam caran vārāṇasyām upātiṣṭhat maitreyam svairiṇī kule tam upasthitam āsīnam jñātvā sa muni sattamam pratiṣṭhamānaḥ asmayata prītaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ mahā manāḥ tam utsmayantam saṃprekṣya maitreyaḥ kṛṣṇam abravīt kāraṇam brūhi dharma ātman yaḥ asmayiṣṭhāḥ kutas ca te ātmanaḥ ca tapaḥ bhāgyam mahā bhāgyam tathā eva ca pṛthak ācarataḥ tāta pṛthak ātmani ca ātmanoḥ alpa antaram aham manye viśiṣṭam api vā tvayā vyāsaḥ uvāca aticcheda ativādābhyām smayaḥ ayam samupāgataḥ trīṇi eva tu padāni āhuḥ puruṣasya uttamam vratam idānīm ca eva naḥ kṛtyam purastāt ca param smṛtam alpaḥ api tādṛśaḥ dāyaḥ bhavati uta mahā phalaḥ tṛṣitāya ca yat dattam hṛdayena anasūyatā tṛṣitaḥ tṛṣitāya tvam dattvā etat aśanam mama ajaiṣīḥ mahataḥ lokān mahā yajñaiḥ iva abhibho adhikam mārjanāt tāta tathā evā api anulepanāt yāni imāni uttamāni iha veda uktāni praśaṃsasi teṣām śreṣṭhatamam dānam iti me na asti saṃśayaḥ dāna kṛdbhiḥ kṛtaḥ panthāḥ yena yānti manīṣiṇaḥ te hi prāṇasya dātāraḥ teṣu dharmaḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ yathā vedāḥ su adhītāḥ ca yathā ca indriya saṃyamaḥ śrīmantam āpnuvanti arthāḥ dānam yajñaḥ tathā sukham sukhāt eva param duḥkham duḥkhāt anyat param sukham dṛśyate hi mahā prājña niyatam vai svabhāvataḥ trividhāni iha vṛttāni narasya āhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ bhīṣmaḥ uvāca atyantam śrīmati kule jātaḥ prājñaḥ bahu śrutaḥ asaṃśayam mahā prājña yathā evā āttha tathā eva tat anujñātaḥ tu bhavatā kim cit brūyām aham vibho vyāsaḥ uvāca brūhi tāvat mahā prājña śuśrūṣe vacanam tava nirdoṣam nirmalam ca eva vacanam dāna saṃhitam vidyā tapobhyām hi bhavān bhāvitātmā na saṃśayaḥ bhavataḥ bhāvitātma tvāt dāyaḥ ayam su mahān mama bhūyas buddhyā anupaśyāmi su samṛddha tapāḥ iva tapaḥ śrutam ca yoniḥ ca api etat brāhmaṇya kāraṇam na hi śrutavatām kim cit adhikam brāhmaṇāt ṛte yathā hi su kṛte kṣetre phalam vindati mānavaḥ evam dattvā śrutavati phalam dātā samaśnute brāhmaṇaḥ ced na vidyeta śruta vṛtta upasaṃhitaḥ pratigrahītā dānasya mogham syāt dhaninām dhanam sa ca annāt jāyate tasmāt sūkṣmaḥ eva vyatikramaḥ yat eva dadataḥ puṇyam tat eva pratigṛhṇataḥ yatra vai brāhmaṇāḥ santi śruta vṛtta upasaṃhitāḥ tatra dāna phalam puṇyam iha ca amutra ca aśnute ye yoni śuddhāḥ satatam tapasi abhiratāḥ bhṛśam dāna adhyayana saṃpannāḥ te vai pūjyatamāḥ sadā te hi svargasya netāraḥ yajña vāhāḥ sanātanāḥ bhīṣmaḥ uvāca diṣṭyā evam tvam vijānāsi diṣṭyā te buddhiḥ īdṛśī lokaḥ hi ayam guṇān eva bhūyiṣṭham sma praśaṃsati rūpa māna vayaḥ māna śrī mānāḥ ca api asaṃśayam diṣṭyā na abhibhavanti tvām daivaḥ te ayam anugrahaḥ yat te bhṛśataram dānāt vartayiṣyāmi tat śṛṇu yāni iha āgama śāstrāṇi yāḥ ca kāḥ cit pravṛttayaḥ tāni vedam puraskṛtya pravṛttāni yathākramam aham dānam praśaṃsāmi bhavān api tapaḥ śrute duranvayam duṣpradhṛṣyam durāpam duratikramam surāpaḥ a saṃmata ādāyī bhrūṇa hā guru talpa gaḥ sarva vidyaḥ tu cakṣuṣmān api yādṛśa tādṛśaḥ tapasvinau ca tau āhuḥ tābhyām kāryam sadā namaḥ dāna pradāḥ sukham pretya prāpnuvanti iha ca śriyam anna dānaiḥ sukṛtinaḥ pratipadyanti laukikāḥ pūjitāḥ pūjayanti etān mānitāḥ mānayanti ca prāpsyase tu anna pānāni yāni dāsyasi kāni cit medhāvī asi kule jātaḥ śrutavān a nṛśaṃsavān etat gṛhāṇa prathamam praśastam gṛhamedhinām yaḥ bhartā vāsitā tuṣṭaḥ bhartuḥ tuṣṭā ca vāsitā tam praṇamya atha maitreyaḥ kṛtvā ca abhipradakṣiṇam svasti prāpnotu bhagavān iti uvāca kṛtāñjaliḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca sat strīṇām samudācāram sarva dharma bhṛtām vara bhīṣmaḥ uvāca sarvajñām sarva dharma jñām deva loke manasvinīm kaikeyī sumanā nāma śāṇḍilīm paryapṛcchata kena vṛttena kalyāṇi samācāreṇa kena vā vidhūya sarva pāpāni deva lokam tvam āgatā hutāśana śikhā iva tvam jvalamānā sva tejasā sutā tārādhipasya iva prabhayā divam āgatā arajāṃsi ca vastrāṇi dhārayantī gata klamā vimāna sthā śubhe bhāsi sahasraguṇam ojasā iti pṛṣṭā sumanayā madhuram cāru hāsinī śāṇḍilī nibhṛtam vākyam sumanām idam abravīt na aham kāṣāya vasanā na api valkala dhāriṇī na ca muṇḍā na jaṭilā bhūtvā deva tvam āgatā ahitāni ca vākyāni sarvāṇi paruṣāṇi ca devatānām pitṝṇām ca brāhmaṇānām ca pūjane apramattā sadā yuktā śvaśrū śvaśura vartinī advāre na ca tiṣṭhāmi ciram na kathayāmi ca asat vā hasitam kim cit ahitam vā api karmaṇā kārya arthe nirgatam ca api bhartāram gṛham āgatam āsanena upasaṃyojya pūjayāmi samāhitā bhakṣyam vā api atha vā lehyam tat sarvam varjayāmi aham kuṭumba arthe samānītam yat kim cit kāryam eva tu pravāsam yadi me bhartā yāti kāryeṇa kena cit añjanam rocanām ca eva snānam mālya anulepanam na utthāpayāmi bhartāram sukha suptam aham sadā ātureṣu api kāryeṣu tena tuṣyati me manaḥ na āyāsayāmi bhartāram kuṭumba arthe ca sarvadā gupta guhyā sadā ca asmi su saṃmṛṣṭa niveśanā imam dharma patham nārī pālayantī samāhitā arundhatī iva nārīṇām svarga loke mahīyate bhīṣmaḥ uvāca etat ākhyāya sā devī sumanāyai tapasvinī pati dharmam mahābhāgā jagāma adarśanam tadā yaḥ ca idam pāṇḍava ākhyānam paṭhet parvaṇi parvaṇi yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca sāmnā vā api pradāne vā jyāyaḥ kim bhavataḥ matam bhīṣmaḥ uvāca sāmnā prasādyate kaḥ cit dānena ca tathā aparaḥ puruṣaḥ prakṛtim jñātvā tayoḥ ekataram bhajet guṇān tu śṛṇu me rājan sāntvasya bharata ṛṣabha dāruṇāni api bhūtāni sāntvena ārādhayet yathā atrā api udāharanti imam itihāsam purātanam gṛhītvā rakṣasā muktaḥ dvijātiḥ kānane yathā gṛhītaḥ kṛcchram āpannaḥ rakṣasā bhakṣayiṣyatā sa buddhi śruta saṃpannaḥ tam dṛṣṭvā atīva bhīṣaṇam rakṣaḥ tu vācā saṃpūjya praśnam papraccha tam dvijam mokṣyase brūhi me praśnam kena asmi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ ābhiḥ gāthābhiḥ avyagraḥ praśnam pratijagāda ha videśa sthaḥ viloka sthaḥ vinā nūnam suhṛd janaiḥ viṣayān atulān bhuṅkṣe tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ nūnam mitrāṇi te rakṣaḥ sādhu upacaritāni api sva doṣāt aparajyante tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ dhana aiśvarya adhikāḥ stabdhāḥ tvad guṇaiḥ parama avarāḥ avajānanti nūnam tvām tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ guṇavān viguṇān anyān nūnam paśyasi satkṛtān prājñaḥ aprājñān vinīta ātmā tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ avṛttyā kliśyamānaḥ api vṛtti upāyān vigarhayan māhātmyāt vyathase nūnam tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ saṃpīḍya ātmānam ārya tvāt tvayā kaḥ cit upaskṛtaḥ jitam tvām manyate sādho tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ kliśyamānān vimārgeṣu kāma krodha āvṛta ātmanaḥ manye nu dhyāyasi janān tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ prājñaiḥ saṃbhāvitaḥ nūnam na prājñaiḥ upasaṃhitaḥ hrīmān amarṣī durvṛttaiḥ tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ nūnam mitra mukhaḥ śatruḥ kaḥ cit ārya vat ācaran vañcayitvā gataḥ tvām vai tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ prakāśa artha gatiḥ nūnam rahasya kuśalaḥ kṛtī tad jñaiḥ na pūjyase nūnam tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ guṇāḥ te na virājante tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ mahat prārthayase nūnam tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ tapaḥ praṇihita ātmānam manye tvā araṇya kāṅkṣiṇam bandhu vargaḥ na gṛhṇāti tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ na bhāti kāle abhihitam tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ dṛḍha pūrva śrutam mūrkham kupitam hṛdaya priyam anunetum na śaknoṣi tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ nūnam āsaṃjayitvā te kṛtye kasmin cit īpsite kaḥ cit arthayate atyartham tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ nūnam tvā sva guṇa apekṣam pūjayānam suhṛd dhruvam mayā arthaḥ iti jānāti tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ vivaktum prāpti śaithilyāt tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ nānā buddhi rucīn loke manuṣyān nūnam icchasi grahītum sva guṇaiḥ sarvān tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ yaśaḥ prārthayase nūnam tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ kṛtam anyaiḥ apahṛtam tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ nūnam ātma kṛtam doṣam a paśyan kim cit ātmani akāraṇe abhiśastaḥ asi tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ suhṛdām apramattānām a pramokṣya artha hāni jam duḥkham artha guṇaiḥ hīnam tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ sādhūn gṛhasthān dṛṣṭvā ca tathā asādhūn vanecarān muktān ca āvasathe saktān tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ na pratiṣṭhati te nūnam tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ dattān akuśalaiḥ arthān manīṣī saṃjijīviṣuḥ prāpya vartayase nūnam tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ pāpān vivardhataḥ dṛṣṭvā kalyāṇān ca avasīdataḥ dhruvam mṛgayase yogyam tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ paraspara viruddhānām priyam nūnam cikīrṣasi suhṛdām avirodhena tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ śrotriyān ca vikarma sthān prājñān ca api ajita indriyān manye anudhyāyasi janān tena asi hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ evam saṃpūjitam rakṣaḥ vipram tam pratyapūjayat yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca pitāmaha mahā prājña sarva śāstra viśārada āścarya bhūtam lokasya śrotum icchāmi ariṃdama ayam ca kālaḥ saṃprāptaḥ durlabha jñāti bāndhavaḥ śāstā ca na hi naḥ kaḥ cit tvām ṛte bharata ṛṣabha vaktum arhasi naḥ praśnam yat tvām pṛcchāmi pārthiva ayam nārāyaṇaḥ śrīmān sarva pārthiva saṃmataḥ asya ca eva samakṣam tvam pārthivānām ca sarvaśas bhrātṝṇām ca priya artham me snehāt bhāṣitum arhasi vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ uvāca tasya tat vacanam śrutvā snehāt āgata saṃbhramaḥ bhīṣmaḥ bhāgīrathī putraḥ idam vacanam abravīt asya viṣṇoḥ purā rājan prabhāvaḥ ayam mayā śrutaḥ yaḥ ca go vṛṣabhāṅkasya prabhāvaḥ tam ca me śṛṇu rudrāṇyāḥ saṃśayaḥ yaḥ ca daṃpatyoḥ tam ca me śṛṇu vratam cacāra dharma ātmā kṛṣṇaḥ dvādaśa vārṣikam dīkṣitam ca āgatau draṣṭum ubhau nārada parvatau kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ ca eva dhaumyaḥ ca japatām varaḥ devalaḥ kāśyapaḥ ca eva hastikāśyapaḥ eva ca apare ṛṣayaḥ santaḥ dīkṣā dama samanvitāḥ hariteṣu suvarṇeṣu barhiṣkeṣu naveṣu ca upopaviviśuḥ prītāḥ viṣṭareṣu mahā ṛṣayaḥ rājarṣīṇām surāṇām ca ye vasanti tapodhanāḥ vaktrāt niḥsṛtya kṛṣṇasya vahniḥ adbhuta karmaṇaḥ saḥ agniḥ dadāha tam śailam sa drumam sa latā kṣupam sa pakṣi mṛga saṃghātam sa śvāpada sarīsṛpam mṛgaiḥ ca vividha ākāraiḥ hāhā bhūtam acetanam sa tu vahniḥ mahā jvālaḥ dagdhvā sarvam aśeṣatas viṣṇoḥ samīpam āgamya pādau śiṣya vat aspṛśat tatas viṣṇuḥ vanam dṛṣṭvā nirdagdham ari karśanaḥ saumyaiḥ dṛṣṭi nipātaiḥ tat punar prakṛtim ānayat sa pakṣi gaṇa saṃghuṣṭaḥ sa śvāpada sarīsṛpaḥ tat adbhutam acintyam ca dṛṣṭvā muni gaṇaḥ tadā vismitaḥ hṛṣṭa lomā ca babhūva asra āvila īkṣaṇaḥ tatas nārāyaṇaḥ dṛṣṭvā tān ṛṣīn vismaya anvitān praśritam madhuram snigdham papraccha vadatām varaḥ kim asya ṛṣi pūgasya tyakta saṅgasya nityaśas etam me saṃśayam sarvam yāthātathyam aninditāḥ ṛṣayaḥ vaktum arhanti niścita artham tapodhanāḥ ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ bhavān visṛjate lokān bhavān saṃharate punar bhavān śītam bhavān uṣṇam bhavān eva pravarṣati pṛthivyām yāni bhūtāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca teṣām pitā tvam mātā ca prabhuḥ prabhavaḥ eva ca yat śrutam yat ca dṛṣṭam naḥ tat pravakṣyāmahe hare vāsudevaḥ uvāca kṛṣṇavartmā yuga anta ābhaḥ yena ayam mathitaḥ giriḥ ṛṣayaḥ ca ārtim āpannāḥ jita krodhāḥ jita indriyāḥ putram ca ātma samam vīrye tapasā sraṣṭum āgataḥ tatas mama ātmā yaḥ dehe saḥ agniḥ bhūtvā viniḥsṛtaḥ gataḥ ca vara dam draṣṭum sarva loka pitāmaham tena ca ātmā anuśiṣṭaḥ me putra tve muni sattamāḥ śiṣya vat paricarya atha śāntaḥ prakṛtim āgataḥ mayā premṇā samākhyātam na bhīḥ kāryā tapodhanāḥ sarvatra gatiḥ avyagrā bhavatām dīrgha darśanāḥ tapasvi vrata saṃdīptāḥ jñāna vijñāna śobhitāḥ yat śrutam yat ca vaḥ dṛṣṭam divi vā yadi vā bhuvi tasya amṛta nikāśasya vāc madhoḥ asti me spṛhā divi vā bhuvi vā kim cit paśyāmi amala darśanāḥ śraddheyaḥ kathitaḥ hi arthaḥ sat jana śravaṇam gataḥ ciram tiṣṭhati medinyām śaile lekhyam iva arpitam tat aham sat jana mukhāt niḥsṛtam tad samāgame kathayiṣyāmi aharahar buddhi dīpa karam nṛṇām tatas muni gaṇāḥ sarve praśritāḥ kṛṣṇa saṃnidhau vāgbhiḥ ṛc bhūṣita arthābhiḥ stuvantaḥ madhusūdanam tatas muni gaṇāḥ sarve nāradam devadarśanam anubhūtam muni gaṇaiḥ tīrtha yātrā parāyaṇaiḥ tat bhavān ṛṣi saṃghasya hita artham sarva coditaḥ yathādṛṣṭam hṛṣīkeśe sarvam ākhyātum arhati evam uktaḥ sa munibhiḥ nāradaḥ bhagavān ṛṣiḥ kathayām āsa deva ṛṣiḥ pūrva vṛttām kathām śubhām bhīṣmaḥ uvāca tatas nārāyaṇa suhṛd nāradaḥ bhagavān ṛṣiḥ śaṃkarasya umayā sārdham saṃvādam pratyabhāṣata tapaḥ cacāra dharma ātmā vṛṣabhāṅkaḥ sureśvaraḥ nānā oṣadhi yute ramye nānā puṣpa samākule apsaraḥ gaṇa saṃkīrṇe bhūta saṃgha niṣevite tatra devaḥ mudā yuktaḥ bhūta saṃgha śataiḥ vṛtaḥ nānā rūpaiḥ virūpaiḥ ca divyaiḥ adbhuta darśanaiḥ kroṣṭuka dvīpi vadanaiḥ ṛkṣa ṛṣabha mukhaiḥ tathā nānā varṇa mṛga prakhyaiḥ sarva jāti samanvayaiḥ divya puṣpa samākīrṇam divya mālā vibhūṣitam tat sadaḥ vṛṣabhāṅkasya divya vāditra nāditam mṛdaṅga paṇava udghuṣṭam śaṅkha bherī nināditam nṛtyadbhiḥ bhūta saṃghaiḥ ca barhiṇaiḥ ca samantataḥ dṛṣṭi kāntam anirdeśyam divyam adbhuta darśanam ṣaṭpadaiḥ upagītaiḥ ca mādhava apratimaḥ giriḥ tam mahā utsava saṃkāśam bhīma rūpa dharam punar dṛṣṭvā muni gaṇasya āsīt parā prītiḥ janārdana munayaḥ ca mahābhāgāḥ siddhāḥ ca eva ūrdhvaretasaḥ marutaḥ vasavaḥ sādhyāḥ viśvedevāḥ sanātanāḥ yakṣāḥ nāgāḥ piśācāḥ ca lokapālāḥ hutāśanāḥ bhāvāḥ ca sarve nyagbhūtāḥ tatra eva āsan samāgatāḥ vihagāḥ ca mudā yuktāḥ prānṛtyan vyanadan ca ha giri pṛṣṭheṣu ramyeṣu vyāharantaḥ jana priyāḥ paryaṅke iva vibhrājan upaviṣṭaḥ mahā manāḥ vyāla yajña upavītī ca lohita aṅgada bhūṣaṇaḥ hari śmaśruḥ jaṭī bhīmaḥ bhaya kartā suradviṣām abhayaḥ sarva bhūtānām bhaktānām vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ dṛṣṭvā tam ṛṣayaḥ sarve śirobhiḥ avanīm gatāḥ vimuktāḥ sarva pāpebhyaḥ kṣāntāḥ vigata kalmaṣāḥ tasya bhūtapateḥ sthānam bhīma rūpa dharam babhau tat sadaḥ vṛṣabhāṅkasya bhīma rūpa dharam babhau tam abhyayāt śailasutā bhūta strī gaṇa saṃvṛtā hara tulya ambara dharā samāna vrata cāriṇī giri sravābhiḥ puṇyābhiḥ sarvatas anugatā śubhā puṣpa vṛṣṭyā abhivarṣantī gandhaiḥ bahuvidhaiḥ tathā sevantī himavat pārśvam hara pārśvam upāgamat tatas smayantī pāṇibhyām narma artham cāru darśanā hara netre śubhe devī sahasā sā samāvṛṇot saṃvṛtābhyām tu netrābhyām tamaḥ bhūtam acetanam nirhomam nirvaṣaṭkāram tat sadaḥ sahasā bhavat nimīlite bhūtapatau naṣṭa sūryaḥ iva abhavat jvālā ca mahatī dīptā lalāṭāt tasya niḥsṛtā tṛtīyam ca asya saṃbhūtam netram āditya saṃnibham yuga anta sadṛśam dīptam yena asau mathitaḥ giriḥ tatas girisutā dṛṣṭvā dīpta agni sadṛśa īkṣaṇam haram praṇamya śirasā dadarśa āyata locanā mṛga yūthaiḥ drutaiḥ bhītaiḥ hara pārśvam upāgataiḥ śaraṇam ca api a vindadbhiḥ tat sadaḥ saṃkulam babhau dvādaśa āditya sadṛśaḥ yuga anta agniḥ iva aparaḥ tam dṛṣṭvā mathitam śailam śailarājasutā tatas bhagavantam prapannā sā sa añjali pragrahā sthitā umām śarvaḥ tadā dṛṣṭvā strī bhāva āgata mārdavām prahṛṣṭa vihagaḥ ca eva prapuṣpita vana drumaḥ prakṛti stham girim dṛṣṭvā prītā devī maheśvaram uvāca sarva bhūtānām patim patim aninditā bhagavan sarva bhūta īśa śūlapāṇe mahāvrata saṃśayaḥ me mahān jātaḥ tam me vyākhyātum arhasi kimartham ca punar deva prakṛti sthaḥ kṣaṇāt kṛtaḥ naṣṭa ālokaḥ tatas lokaḥ kṣaṇena samapadyata naṣṭa āditye tathā loke tamaḥ bhūte nagātmaje tṛtīyam locanam dīptam sṛṣṭam te rakṣatā prajāḥ tasya ca akṣṇaḥ mahat tejaḥ yena ayam mathitaḥ giriḥ tvad priya artham ca me devi prakṛti sthaḥ kṣaṇāt kṛtaḥ pūrvam tathā eva śrī kāntam uttaram paścimam tathā dakṣiṇam ca mukham raudram kena ūrdhvam kapilāḥ jaṭāḥ kena kaṇṭhaḥ ca te nīlaḥ barhi barha nibhaḥ kṛtaḥ etam me saṃśayam sarvam vada bhūtapate anagha sa dharma cāriṇī ca aham bhaktā ca iti vṛṣadhvaja evam uktaḥ sa bhagavān śailaputryā pinākadhṛk tasyāḥ vṛttyā ca buddhyā ca prītimān abhavat prabhuḥ tatas tām abravīt devaḥ subhage śrūyatām iti tilottamā nāma purā brahmaṇā yoṣit uttamā tilam tilam samuddhṛtya ratnānām nirmitā śubhā sā abhyagacchata mām devi rūpeṇa apratimā bhuvi pradakṣiṇam lobhayantī mām śubhe rucira ānanā yatas yatas sā sudatī mām upādhāvat antike tām didṛkṣuḥ aham yogāt catur mūrti tvam āgataḥ paścimam me mukham saumyam sarva prāṇi sukha āvaham dakṣiṇam bhīma saṃkāśam raudram saṃharati prajāḥ jaṭilaḥ brahmacārī ca lokānām hita kāmyayā indreṇa ca purā vajram kṣiptam śrī kāṅkṣiṇā mama dagdhvā kaṇṭham tu tat yātam tena śrīkaṇṭha tā mama vāhaneṣu prabhūteṣu śrīmatsu anyeṣu satsu te katham go vṛṣabhaḥ deva vāhana tvam upāgataḥ surabhīm sasṛje brahma amṛta dhenum payaḥ mucam sā sṛṣṭā bahudhā jātā kṣaramāṇā payaḥ amṛtam tasyāḥ vatsa mukha utsṛṣṭaḥ phenaḥ mad gātram āgataḥ tatas dagdhāḥ mayāḥ gāvaḥ nānā varṇa tvam āgatāḥ tatas aham lokaguruṇā śamam nītaḥ artha vedinā vṛṣam ca imam dhvaja artham me dadau vāhanam eva ca nivāsāḥ bahu rūpāḥ te viśva rūpa guṇa anvitāḥ tān ca saṃtyajya bhagavan śmaśāne ramase katham keśa asthi kalile bhīme kapāla ghaṭa saṃkule aśucau māṃsa kalile vasā śoṇita kardame vinikīrṇa āmiṣa caye śivā nāda vinādite medhya anveṣī mahīm kṛtsnām vicarāmi niśāsu aham tena me sarva vāsānām śmaśāne ramate manaḥ tatra ca eva ramante me bhūta saṃghāḥ śubha ānane pinākapāṇe vara da saṃśayaḥ me mahān ayam dharmaḥ kiṃlakṣaṇaḥ proktaḥ katham vā ācaritum naraiḥ nāradaḥ uvāca tatas muni gaṇaḥ sarvaḥ tām devīm pratyapūjayat vāgbhiḥ ṛc bhūṣita arthābhiḥ stavaiḥ ca artha vidām vara śamaḥ dānam yathāśakti gārhasthyaḥ dharmaḥ uttamaḥ para dāreṣu a saṃkalpaḥ nyāsa strī parirakṣaṇam eṣa pañcavidhaḥ dharmaḥ bahu śākhaḥ sukha udayaḥ bhagavan saṃśayam pṛṣṭaḥ tam me vyākhyātum arhasi cāturvarṇyasya yaḥ dharmaḥ sve sve varṇe guṇa āvahaḥ brāhmaṇe kīdṛśaḥ dharmaḥ kṣatriye kīdṛśaḥ bhavet vaiśye kiṃlakṣaṇaḥ dharmaḥ śūdre kiṃlakṣaṇaḥ bhavet nyāyataḥ te mahābhāge saṃśayaḥ samudīritaḥ bhūmi devāḥ mahābhāgāḥ sadā loke dvijātayaḥ upavāsaḥ sadā dharmaḥ brāhmaṇasya na saṃśayaḥ guru daivata pūjā artham svādhyāya abhyasana ātmakaḥ guruṇā tu abhyanujñātaḥ samāvarteta vai dvijaḥ vindeta anantaram bhāryām anurūpām yathāvidhi āhitāgniḥ adhīyānaḥ juhvānaḥ saṃyata indriyaḥ vighasa āśī yata āhāraḥ gṛhasthaḥ satya vāc śuciḥ iṣṭīḥ ca paśubandhān ca vidhi pūrvam samācaret yajñaḥ ca paramaḥ dharmaḥ tathā ahiṃsā ca dehiṣu brāhmaṇasya gṛhasthasya śrotriyasya viśeṣataḥ daṃpatyoḥ sama śīla tvam dharmaḥ ca gṛhamedhinām gṛhyāṇām ca eva devānām nityam puṣpa bali kriyā su saṃmṛṣṭa upalipte ca sa ājya dhūma udgame gṛhe dvijātīnām satām nityam sadā eva eṣa pravartate tam aham te pravakṣyāmi tam me śṛṇu samāhitā kṣatriyasya smṛtaḥ dharmaḥ prajā pālanam āditas nirdiṣṭa phala bhoktā hi rājā dharmeṇa yujyate prajāḥ pālayate yaḥ hi dharmeṇa manuja adhipaḥ tasya dharma arjitāḥ lokāḥ prajā pālana saṃcitāḥ tatra rājñaḥ paraḥ dharmaḥ damaḥ svādhyāyaḥ eva ca yajñopavīta dhāraṇam yajñaḥ dharma kriyāḥ tathā bhṛtyānām bharaṇam dharmaḥ kṛte karmaṇi amogha tā go brāhmaṇa arthe vikrāntaḥ saṃgrāme nidhanam gataḥ aśvamedha jitān lokān prāpnoti tridiva ālaye vaiśyasya satatam dharmaḥ pāśupālyam kṛṣiḥ tathā vāṇijyam sat patha sthānam ātithyam praśamaḥ damaḥ viprāṇām svāgatam tyāgaḥ vaiśya dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ tilān gandhān rasān ca eva na vikrīṇīta vai kva cit vaṇikpatham upāsīnaḥ vaiśyaḥ sat patham āśritaḥ śūdra dharmaḥ paraḥ nityam śuśrūṣā ca dvijātiṣu sa śūdraḥ saṃśita tapāḥ satya saṃdhaḥ jita indriyaḥ śuśrūṣan atithim prāptam tapaḥ saṃcinute mahat śūdraḥ dharma phalaiḥ iṣṭaiḥ saṃprayujyeta buddhimān uktāḥ tvayā pṛthak dharmāḥ cāturvarṇya hitāḥ śubhāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ loka sāreṇa sṛṣṭāḥ dhātrā guṇa arthinā lokān tārayitum kṛtsnān martyeṣu kṣitidevatāḥ ime tu loka dharma artham trayaḥ sṛṣṭāḥ svayaṃbhuvā pṛthivyāḥ sarjane nityam sṛṣṭāḥ tān api me śṛṇu śiṣṭa ācīrṇaḥ paraḥ proktaḥ trayaḥ dharmāḥ sanātanāḥ ṣaḍ imāni tu karmāṇi provāca bhuvaneśvaraḥ vṛtti artham brāhmaṇānām vai śṛṇu tāni samāhitā adhyāpanam adhītam ca ṣaṣ karmā dharma bhāj dvijaḥ nitya svādhyāya tā dharmaḥ dharmaḥ yajñaḥ sanātanaḥ dānam praśasyate ca asya yathāśakti yathāvidhi gṛhastha tā viśuddhānām dharmasya nicayaḥ mahān pañcayajña viśuddha ātmā satya vāc anasūyakaḥ a mānī ca sadā a jihmaḥ snigdha vāṇī pradaḥ tathā pādyam arghyam yathānyāyam āsanam śayanam tathā dīpam pratiśrayam ca api yaḥ dadāti sa dhārmikaḥ śūdra dharmaḥ samākhyātaḥ tri varṇa paricāraṇam pravṛtti lakṣaṇaḥ dharmaḥ gṛhastheṣu vidhīyate tam aham kīrtayiṣyāmi sarva bhūta hitam śubham dātavyam asakṛt śaktyā yaṣṭavyam asakṛt tathā puṣṭi karma vidhānam ca kartavyam bhūtim icchatā ekena aṃśena dharma arthaḥ cartavyaḥ bhūtim icchatā ekena aṃśena kāma arthe ekam aṃśam vivardhayet tasya vṛttim pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu me devi tattvataḥ āśā pāśa vimokṣaḥ ca śasyate mokṣa kāṅkṣiṇām na kuṇḍyām na udake saṅgaḥ na vāsasi na ca āsane na tridaṇḍe na śayane na agnau na śaraṇa ālaye vṛkṣa mūla śayaḥ nityam śūnya āgāra niveśanaḥ nadī pulina śāyī ca nadī tīra ratiḥ ca yaḥ ātmani eva ātmanaḥ bhāvam samāsajya aṭati dvijaḥ sthāṇu bhūtaḥ nirāhāraḥ mokṣa dṛṣṭena karmaṇā eṣa mokṣa vidām dharmaḥ veda uktaḥ sat pathaḥ satām caturvidhāḥ bhikṣavaḥ te kuṭī cara kṛta udakaḥ haṃsaḥ paramahaṃsaḥ ca yaḥ yaḥ paścāt saḥ uttamaḥ atas parataram na asti na adharam na tiras agratas tam dṛṣṭvā me manaḥ prītam maheśvara sadā bhavet etam me saṃśayam deva muni dharma kṛtam vibho nikhilena mayā pṛṣṭam mahādeva yathātatham yam kṛtvā munayaḥ yānti siddhim sva tapasā śubhe phenapānām ṛṣīṇām yaḥ dharmaḥ dharma vidām sadā tam me śṛṇu mahābhāge dharma jñe dharmam āditas amṛtam brahmaṇā pītam madhuram prasṛtam divi eṣa teṣām viśuddhānām phenapānām tapodhane dharma caryā kṛtaḥ mārgaḥ vālakhilya gaṇe śṛṇu vālakhilyāḥ tapaḥ siddhāḥ munayaḥ sūrya maṇḍale uñcham uñchanti dharma jñāḥ śākunīm vṛttim āsthitāḥ mṛga nirmoka vasanāḥ cīra valkala vāsasaḥ nirdvaṃdvāḥ sat patham prāptāḥ vālakhilyāḥ tapodhanāḥ aṅguṣṭha parva mātrāḥ te sveṣu aṅgeṣu vyavasthitāḥ tapaḥ caraṇam īhante teṣām dharma phalam mahat dyotayantaḥ diśaḥ sarvāḥ tapasā dagdha kilbiṣāḥ ye tu anye śuddha manasaḥ dayā dharma parāyaṇāḥ santaḥ cakracarāḥ puṇyāḥ soma loka carāḥ ca ye saṃprakṣāla aśmakuṭṭāḥ ca dantolūkhalinaḥ tathā somapānām ca devānām ūṣmapāṇām tathā eva ca uñchanti ye samīpa sthāḥ svabhāva niyata indriyāḥ teṣām agni pariṣyandaḥ pitṛ deva arcanam tathā yajñānām ca api pañcānām yajanam dharmaḥ ucyate ṛṣi dharmaḥ sadā cīrṇaḥ yaḥ anyaḥ tam api me śṛṇu sarveṣu eva ṛṣi dharmeṣu jeyaḥ ātmā jita indriyaḥ kāma krodhau tatas paścāt jetavyau iti me matiḥ soma yajña abhyanujñānam pañcamī yajña dakṣiṇā nityam yajña kriyā dharmaḥ pitṛ deva arcane ratiḥ sthaṇḍile śayanam yogaḥ śāka parṇa niṣevaṇam phala mūla aśanam vāyuḥ āpaḥ śaivala bhakṣaṇam ṛṣīṇām niyamāḥ hi ete yaiḥ jayanti ajitām gatim atīta pātrasaṃcāre kāle vigata bhaikṣake atithim kāṅkṣamāṇaḥ vai śeṣa anna kṛta bhojanaḥ deśeṣu ramaṇīyeṣu girīṇām nirjhareṣu ca sravantīnām ca kuñjeṣu parvata upavaneṣu ca deśeṣu ca vicitreṣu phalavatsu samāhitāḥ teṣām api vidhim puṇyam śrotum icchāmi śaṃkara vānaprastheṣu deveśa sva śarīra upajīviṣu vānaprastheṣu yaḥ dharmaḥ tam me śṛṇu samāhitā vānaprasthaiḥ idam karma kartavyam śṛṇu yādṛśam tri kālam abhiṣeka arthaḥ pitṛ deva arcanam kriyā nīvāra grahaṇam ca eva phala mūla niṣevaṇam iṅgudaiḥ aṇḍa tailānām sneha artham ca niṣevaṇam vīraśayyām upāsadbhiḥ vīrasthāna upasevibhiḥ maṇḍūkayoga niyataiḥ yathā nyāya niṣevibhiḥ vīrāsana gataiḥ nityam sthaṇḍile śayanaiḥ tathā abbhakṣaiḥ vāyubhakṣaiḥ ca śaivāla uttara bhojanaiḥ aśmakuṭṭaiḥ tathā dāntaiḥ saṃprakṣālaiḥ tathā aparaiḥ cīra valkala saṃvītaiḥ mṛga carma nivāsibhiḥ kāryā yātrā yathākālam yathādharmam yathāvidhi vanam gurum iva āsādya vastavyam vana jīvibhiḥ teṣām homa kriyā dharmaḥ pañcayajña niṣevaṇam aṣṭamī yajña para tā cāturmāsya niṣevaṇam vimuktāḥ dāra saṃyogaiḥ vimuktāḥ sarva saṃkaraiḥ sruc bhāṇḍa paramāḥ nityam tretāgni śaraṇāḥ sadā brahma lokam mahā puṇyam soma lokam ca śāśvatam gacchanti munayaḥ siddhāḥ ṛṣi dharma vyapāśrayāt eṣa dharmaḥ mayā devi vānaprastha āśritaḥ śubhaḥ vistareṇa artha saṃpannaḥ yathāsthūlam udāhṛtaḥ siddhi vādeṣu saṃsiddhāḥ tathā vana nivāsinaḥ svairiṇaḥ dāra saṃyuktāḥ teṣām dharmaḥ katham smṛtaḥ svairiṇaḥ tāpasāḥ devi sarve dāra vihāriṇaḥ teṣām mauṇḍyam kaṣāyaḥ ca vāsa rātriḥ ca kāraṇam tri kālam abhiṣekaḥ ca hotram tu ṛṣi kṛtam mahat ye ca daṃpati dharmāṇaḥ sva dāra niyata indriyāḥ caranti vidhi dṛṣṭam tat ṛtu kāla abhigāminaḥ teṣām ṛṣi kṛtaḥ dharmaḥ dharmiṇām upapadyate na kāmakārāt kāmaḥ anyaḥ saṃsevyaḥ dharma darśibhiḥ sarva bhūteṣu yaḥ samyak dadāti abhaya dakṣiṇām hiṃsā roṣa vimukta ātmā sa vai dharmeṇa yujyate sarva bhūta anukampī yaḥ sarva bhūta ārjava vrataḥ sarva vedeṣu vā snānam sarva bhūteṣu ca ārjavam ubhe ete same syātām ārjavam vā viśiṣyate vyapeta tandraḥ dharma ātmā śakyā sat patham āśritaḥ āśrama abhiratāḥ deva tāpasāḥ ye tapodhanāḥ rājānaḥ rāja putrāḥ ca nirdhanāḥ vā mahā dhanāḥ nityam sthānam upāgamya divya candana rūṣitāḥ etam me saṃśayam deva tapaḥ caryā gatam śubham śaṃsa sarvam aśeṣeṇa tryakṣa tripura nāśana upavāsa vrataiḥ dāntāḥ ahiṃsrāḥ satya vādinaḥ saṃsiddhāḥ pretya gandharvaiḥ saha modanti anāmayāḥ maṇḍūkayoga śayanaḥ yathāsthānam yathāvidhi dīkṣām carati dharma ātmā sa nāgaiḥ saha modate śaṣpam mṛga mukha utsṛṣṭam yaḥ mṛgaiḥ saha sevate dīkṣitaḥ vai mudā yuktaḥ sa gacchati amarāvatīm śaivālam śīrṇa parṇam vā tat vrataḥ yaḥ niṣevate vāyubhakṣaḥ ambu bhakṣaḥ vā phala mūla aśanaḥ api vā yakṣeṣu aiśvaryam ādhāya modate apsarasām gaṇaiḥ agni yoga vahaḥ grīṣme vidhi dṛṣṭena karmaṇā cīrtvā dvādaśa varṣāṇi rājā bhavati pārthivaḥ āhāra niyamam kṛtvā muniḥ dvādaśa vārṣikam marum saṃsādhya yatnena rājā bhavati pārthivaḥ sthaṇḍile śuddham ākāśam parigṛhya samantataḥ praviśya ca mudā yuktaḥ dīkṣām dvādaśa vārṣikīm sthaṇḍilasya phalāni āhuḥ yānāni śayanāni ca gṛhāṇi ca mahārhāṇi candra śubhrāṇi bhāmini ātmānam upajīvan yaḥ niyataḥ niyata aśanaḥ deham vā anaśane tyaktvā sa svargam samupāśnute ātmānam upajīvan yaḥ dīkṣām dvādaśa vārṣikīm tyaktvā mahā arṇave deham vāruṇam lokam aśnute ātmānam upajīvan yaḥ dīkṣām dvādaśa vārṣikīm sādhayitvā ātmanā ātmānam nirdvaṃdvaḥ niṣparigrahaḥ cīrtvā dvādaśa varṣāṇi dīkṣām ekām manaḥ gatām ātmānam upajīvan yaḥ dīkṣām dvādaśa vārṣikīm yaḥ tu devi yathānyāyam dīkṣitaḥ niyataḥ dvijaḥ ātmani ātmānam ādhāya nirdvaṃdvaḥ niṣparigrahaḥ cīrtvā dvādaśa varṣāṇi dīkṣām ekām manaḥ gatām araṇī sahitam skandhe baddhvā gacchati anāvṛtaḥ vīrādhvānam anāḥ nityam vīrāsana rataḥ tathā vīra sthāyī ca satatam sa vīragatim āpnuyāt divya puṣpa samākīrṇaḥ divya candana bhūṣitaḥ vīra loka gataḥ vīraḥ vīra yoga vahaḥ sadā sattva sthaḥ sarvam utsṛjya dīkṣitaḥ niyataḥ śuciḥ vīrādhvānam prapadyet yaḥ tasya lokāḥ sanātanāḥ śakra loka gataḥ śrīmān modate ca nirāmayaḥ cāturvarṇyam bhagavatā pūrvam sṛṣṭam svayaṃbhuvā kena vā karmaṇā vipraḥ śūdra yonau prajāyate kṣatriyaḥ śūdra tām eti kena vā karmaṇā vibho trayaḥ varṇāḥ prakṛtyā iha katham brāhmaṇyam āpnuyuḥ brāhmaṇyam devi duṣprāpam nisargāt brāhmaṇaḥ śubhe kṣatriyaḥ vaiśya śūdrau vā nisargāt iti me matiḥ karmaṇā duṣkṛtena iha sthānāt bhraśyati vai dvijaḥ jyeṣṭham varṇam anuprāpya tasmāt rakṣeta vai dvijaḥ brāhmaṇyāt sa paribhraṣṭaḥ kṣatra yonau prajāyate brāhmaṇyam durlabham prāpya karoti alpa matiḥ sadā sa dvijaḥ vaiśya tām eti vaiśyaḥ vā śūdra tām iyāt tatra asau nirayam prāptaḥ varṇa bhraṣṭaḥ bahiṣkṛtaḥ brahma loka paribhraṣṭaḥ śūdraḥ samupajāyate kṣatriyaḥ vā mahābhāge vaiśyaḥ vā dharma cāriṇi svāni karmāṇi apāhāya śūdra karmāṇi sevate sva sthānāt sa paribhraṣṭaḥ varṇa saṃkara tām gataḥ brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyaḥ vaiśyaḥ śūdra tvam yāti tādṛśaḥ yaḥ tu śuddhaḥ svadharmeṇa jñāna vijñānavān śuciḥ idam ca eva aparam devi brahmaṇā samudīritam ugra annam garhitam devi gaṇānnam śrāddha sūtakam ghuṣṭānnam nā eva bhoktavyam śūdra annam nā eva karhi cit śūdra annam garhitam devi deva devaiḥ mahātmabhiḥ pitāmaha mukha utsṛṣṭam pramāṇam iti me matiḥ śūdra annena avaśeṣeṇa jaṭhare yaḥ mriyeta vai āhitāgniḥ tathā yajvā sa śūdra gati bhāj bhavet tena śūdra anna śeṣeṇa brahma sthānāt apākṛtaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ śūdra tām eti na asti tatra vicāraṇā yasya annena avaśeṣeṇa jaṭhare yaḥ mriyeta vai tām tām yonim vrajet vipraḥ yasya annam upajīvati brāhmaṇa tvam śubham prāpya durlabham yaḥ avamanyate abhojya annāni ca aśnāti sa dvija tvāt pateta vai svādhyāya varjitaḥ pāpaḥ lubdhaḥ naikṛtikaḥ śaṭhaḥ avratī vṛṣalī bhartā kuṇḍāśī soma vikrayī gurutalpī guru dveṣī guru kutsā ratiḥ ca yaḥ śūdraḥ brāhmaṇa tām gacchet vaiśyaḥ kṣatriya tām vrajet śūdra karmāṇi sarvāṇi yathānyāyam yathāvidhi śuśrūṣām paricaryām ca jyeṣṭhe varṇe prayatnataḥ kuryāt avimanāḥ śūdraḥ satatam sat pathe sthitaḥ ṛtu kāla abhigāmī ca niyataḥ niyata aśanaḥ caukṣaḥ caukṣa jana anveṣī śeṣa anna kṛta bhojanaḥ vṛthāmāṃsāni a bhuñjānaḥ śūdraḥ vaiśya tvam ṛcchati ṛta vāc an ahaṃvādī nirdvaṃdvaḥ śama kovidaḥ yajate nitya yajñaiḥ ca svādhyāya paramaḥ śuciḥ gṛhastha vratam ātiṣṭhan dvi kāla kṛta bhojanaḥ śeṣa āśī vijita āhāraḥ niṣkāmaḥ nirahaṃvadaḥ agnihotram upāsan ca juhvānaḥ ca yathāvidhi sarva ātithyam upātiṣṭhan śeṣa anna kṛta bhojanaḥ sa vaiśyaḥ kṣatriyaḥ jātaḥ janma prabhṛti saṃskṛtaḥ dadāti yajate yajñaiḥ saṃskṛtaiḥ āpta dakṣiṇaiḥ adhīte svargam anvicchan tretāgni śaraṇaḥ sadā dharma daṇḍaḥ na nirdaṇḍaḥ dharma kārya anuśāsakaḥ yantritaḥ kārya karaṇe ṣaḍbhāga kṛta lakṣaṇaḥ ṛtu kāle tu dharma ātmā patnīm seveta nityadā sarva upavāsī niyataḥ svādhyāya paramaḥ śuciḥ barhiṣka antarite nityam śayānaḥ agni gṛhe sadā sarva ātithyam trivargasya kurvāṇaḥ su manāḥ sadā śūdrāṇām ca anna kāmānām nityam siddham iti bruvan sva arthāt vā yadi vā kāmāt na kim cit upalakṣayet pitṛ deva atithi kṛte sādhanam kurute ca yaḥ go brāhmaṇa hita arthāya raṇe ca abhimukhaḥ hataḥ jñāna vijñāna saṃpannaḥ saṃskṛtaḥ vedapāragaḥ śūdraḥ api āgama saṃpannaḥ dvijaḥ bhavati saṃskṛtaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ vā api asat vṛttaḥ sarva saṃkara bhojanaḥ brāhmaṇyam puṇyam utsṛjya śūdraḥ bhavati tādṛśaḥ svabhāva karma ca śubham yatra śūdre api tiṣṭhati na yoniḥ nā api saṃskāraḥ na śrutam na ca saṃnatiḥ kāraṇāni dvija tvasya vṛttam eva tu kāraṇam vṛtte sthitaḥ ca suśroṇi brāhmaṇa tvam nigacchati brāhmaḥ svabhāvaḥ kalyāṇi samaḥ sarvatra me matiḥ ete yoni phalāḥ devi sthāna bhāga nidarśakāḥ svayam ca vara dena uktāḥ brahmaṇā sṛjatā prajāḥ yat tatra bījam vapati sā kṛṣiḥ pāralaukikī mita āśinā sadā bhāvyam sat patha ālambinā sadā saṃhitā dhyāyinā bhāvyam gṛhe vai gṛhamedhinā nityam svādhyāya yuktena dāna adhyayana jīvinā āhitāgniḥ adhīyānaḥ brahma bhūyāya kalpate brāhmaṇyam eva saṃprāpya rakṣitavyam yata ātmabhiḥ etat te sarvam ākhyātam yathā śūdraḥ bhavet dvijaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ vā cyutaḥ dharmāt yathā śūdra tvam āpnute dharma adharme nṛṇām deva brūhi me saṃśayam vibho karmaṇā manasā vācā trividham hi naraḥ sadā kena śīlena vā deva karmaṇā kīdṛśena vā samācāraiḥ guṇaiḥ vākyaiḥ svargam yānti iha mānavāḥ sarva prāṇi hitaḥ praśnaḥ śrūyatām buddhi vardhanaḥ na adharmeṇa na dharmeṇa badhyante chinna saṃśayāḥ pralaya utpatti tattva jñāḥ sarva jñāḥ sama darśinaḥ vīta rāgāḥ vimucyante puruṣāḥ sarva bandhanaiḥ karmaṇā manasā vācā ye na hiṃsanti kim cana prāṇa atipātāt viratāḥ śīlavantaḥ dayā anvitāḥ sarva bhūta dayāvantaḥ viśvāsyāḥ sarva jantuṣu tyakta hiṃsā samācārāḥ te narāḥ svarga gāminaḥ para dāreṣu vartante te narāḥ svarga gāminaḥ stainyāt nivṛttāḥ satatam saṃtuṣṭāḥ sva dhanena ca svabhāgyāni upajīvanti te narāḥ svarga gāminaḥ sva dāra niratāḥ ye ca ṛtu kāla abhigāminaḥ a grāmya sukha bhogāḥ ca te narāḥ svarga gāminaḥ para dāreṣu ye nityam cāritra āvṛta locanāḥ yata indriyāḥ śīla parāḥ te narāḥ svarga gāminaḥ eṣa deva kṛtaḥ mārgaḥ sevitavyaḥ sadā naraiḥ a kaṣāya kṛtaḥ ca eva mārgaḥ sevyaḥ sadā budhaiḥ dāna dharma tapaḥ yuktaḥ śīla śauca dayā ātmakaḥ ātma hetoḥ para arthe vā narma hāsya āśrayāt tathā ye mṛṣā na vadanti iha te narāḥ svarga gāminaḥ anṛtam ye na bhāṣante te narāḥ svarga gāminaḥ ślakṣṇām vāṇīm nirābādhām madhurām pāpa varjitām svāgatena abhibhāṣante te narāḥ svarga gāminaḥ kaṭukām ye na bhāṣante paruṣām niṣṭhurām giram a paiśunya ratāḥ santaḥ te narāḥ svarga gāminaḥ piśunām ye na bhāṣante mitra bheda karīm giram ṛtām maitrīm prabhāṣante te narāḥ svarga gāminaḥ varjayanti sadā sūcyam para droham ca mānavāḥ sarva bhūta samāḥ dāntāḥ te narāḥ svarga gāminaḥ śaṭha pralāpāt viratāḥ viruddha parivarjakāḥ na kopāt vyāharante ye vācam hṛdaya dāraṇīm sāntvam vadanti kruddhāḥ api te narāḥ svarga gāminaḥ eṣa vāṇī kṛtaḥ devi dharmaḥ sevyaḥ sadā naraiḥ śubhaḥ satya guṇaḥ nityam varjanīyāḥ mṛṣā budhaiḥ manasā badhyate yena karmaṇā puruṣaḥ sadā mānasena iha dharmeṇa saṃyuktāḥ puruṣāḥ sadā svargam gacchanti kalyāṇi tat me kīrtayataḥ śṛṇu duṣpraṇītena manasā duṣpraṇītatara ākṛtiḥ badhyate mānavaḥ yena śṛṇu ca anyat śubha ānane araṇye vijane nyastam para svam vīkṣya ye narāḥ manasā api na hiṃsanti te narāḥ svarga gāminaḥ tathā eva para dārān ye kāma vṛttān rahaḥ gatān manasā api na hiṃsanti te narāḥ svarga gāminaḥ śatrum mitram ca ye nityam tulyena manasā narāḥ bhajanti maitrāḥ saṃgamya te narāḥ svarga gāminaḥ śrutavantaḥ dayāvantaḥ śucayaḥ satya saṃgarāḥ svaiḥ arthaiḥ parisaṃtuṣṭāḥ te narāḥ svarga gāminaḥ a vairāḥ ye tu anāyāsāḥ maitra citta parāḥ sadā sarva bhūta dayāvantaḥ te narāḥ svarga gāminaḥ śraddhāvantaḥ dayāvantaḥ cokṣāḥ cokṣa jana priyāḥ śubhānām aśubhānām ca karmaṇām phala saṃcaye vipāka jñāḥ ca ye devi te narāḥ svarga gāminaḥ nyāya upetāḥ guṇa upetāḥ deva dvija parāḥ sadā samatām samanuprāptāḥ te narāḥ svarga gāminaḥ mahān me saṃśayaḥ kaḥ cit martyān prati maheśvara tasmāt tam naipuṇena adya mama ākhyātum tvam arhasi kena āyuḥ labhate dīrgham karmaṇā puruṣaḥ prabho kṣīṇa āyuḥ kena bhavati karmaṇā bhuvi mānavaḥ akulīnāḥ tathā ca anye kulīnāḥ ca tathā apare durdarśāḥ ke cit ābhānti narāḥ kāṣṭha mayāḥ iva priya darśāḥ tathā ca anye darśanāt eva mānavāḥ duṣprajñāḥ ke cit ābhānti ke cit ābhānti paṇḍitāḥ mahā prajñāḥ tathā eva anye jñāna vijñāna darśinaḥ alpa ābādhāḥ tathā ke cit mahā bādhāḥ tathā apare dṛśyante puruṣāḥ deva tat me śaṃsitum arhasi prāṇa atipātī yaḥ raudraḥ daṇḍa hasta udyataḥ tathā nityam udyata daṇḍaḥ ca hanti bhūta gaṇān naraḥ nirdayaḥ sarva bhūtānām nityam udvega kārakaḥ api kīṭa pipīlānām aśaraṇyaḥ su nirghṛṇaḥ viparītaḥ tu dharma ātmā rūpavān abhijāyate nirayam yāti hiṃsā ātmā yāti svargam ahiṃsakaḥ yātanām niraye raudrām sa kṛcchrām labhate naraḥ mānuṣyam labhate ca api hīna āyuḥ tatra jāyate pāpena karmaṇā devi baddhaḥ hiṃsā ratiḥ naraḥ apriyaḥ sarva bhūtānām hīna āyuḥ upajāyate yaḥ tu śukla abhijātīyaḥ prāṇi ghāta vivarjakaḥ nikṣipta daṇḍaḥ nirdaṇḍaḥ na hinasti kadā cana īdṛśaḥ puruṣa utkarṣaḥ devi deva tvam aśnute upapannān sukhān bhogān upāśnāti mudā yutaḥ evam dīrgha āyuṣām mārgaḥ su vṛttānām su karmaṇām prāṇi hiṃsā vimokṣeṇa brahmaṇā samudīritaḥ kiṃśīlāḥ kiṃsamācārāḥ puruṣāḥ kaiḥ ca karmabhiḥ dātā brāhmaṇa satkartā dīna andha kṛpaṇa ādiṣu bhakṣya bhojya anna pānānām vāsasām ca pradāyakaḥ pratiśrayān sabhāḥ kūpān prapāḥ puṣkariṇīḥ tathā āsanam śayanam yānam dhanam ratnam gṛhān tathā sasya jātāni sarvāṇi gāḥ kṣetrāṇi atha yoṣitaḥ su
