pratīta manāḥ nityam yaḥ prayacchati mānavaḥ tatra uṣya su ciram kālam bhuktvā bhogān anuttamān tasmāt svargāt cyutaḥ lokāt mānuṣeṣu upajāyate tatra kāma guṇaiḥ sarvaiḥ samupetaḥ mudā yutaḥ mahā bhogaḥ mahā kośaḥ dhanī bhavati mānavaḥ ete devi mahā bhogāḥ prāṇinaḥ dāna śīlinaḥ brahmaṇā vai purā proktāḥ sarvasya priya darśanāḥ apare mānavāḥ devi pradāna kṛpaṇāḥ dvijaiḥ dīna andha kṛpaṇān dṛṣṭvā bhikṣukān atithīn api yācyamānāḥ nivartante jihvā lobha samanvitāḥ na dhanāni na vāsāṃsi na bhogān na ca kāñcanam apravṛttāḥ tu ye lubdhāḥ nāstikāḥ dāna varjitāḥ evaṃbhūtāḥ narāḥ devi nirayam yānti abuddhayaḥ te ced manuṣya tām yānti yadā kālasya paryayāt kṣudh pipāsā parītāḥ ca sarva bhoga bahiṣkṛtāḥ nirāśāḥ sarva bhogebhyaḥ jīvanti adhama jīvikām apare stambhinaḥ nityam māninaḥ pāpataḥ ratāḥ gurum ca abhigatam premṇā guru vat na bubhūṣate saṃmānyān ca avamanyante vṛddhān paribhavanti ca śvapāka pulkasa ādīnām kutsitānām acetasām kuleṣu teṣu jāyante guru vṛddha apacāyinaḥ na stambhī na ca mānī yaḥ devatā dvija pūjakaḥ a dveṣī su mukhaḥ ślakṣṇaḥ snigdha vāṇī pradaḥ sadā svāgatena eva sarveṣām bhūtānām avihiṃsakaḥ mārga arhāya dadan mārgam gurum guru vat arcayan tatas mānuṣa tām prāpya viśiṣṭa kula jaḥ bhavet yathā arha dātā ca arheṣu dharma caryā paraḥ bhavet saṃmataḥ sarva bhūtānām sarva loka namaskṛtaḥ udātta kula jātīyaḥ udātta abhijanaḥ sadā eṣa dharmaḥ mayā proktaḥ vidhātrā svayam īritaḥ hastābhyām yadi vā padbhyām rajjvā daṇḍena vā punar loṣṭaiḥ stambhaiḥ upāyaiḥ vā jantūn bādhati śobhane upakrāmati jantūn ca udvega jananaḥ sadā evaṃśīla samācāraḥ nirayam pratipadyate sa ced mānuṣa tām gacchet yadi kālasya paryayāt loka dveṣyaḥ adhamaḥ puṃsām svayam karma kṛtaiḥ phalaiḥ eṣa devi manuṣyeṣu boddhavyaḥ jñāti bandhuṣu aparaḥ sarva bhūtāni dayāvān anupaśyati na rajjvā na ca daṇḍena na loṣṭaiḥ na āyudhena ca udvejayati bhūtāni ślakṣṇa karmā dayā paraḥ evaṃśīla samācāraḥ svarge samupajāyate sa ced karma kṣayāt martyaḥ manuṣyeṣu upajāyate alpa ābādhaḥ nirītīkaḥ sa jātaḥ sukham edhate sukha bhāgī nirāyāsaḥ nirudvegaḥ sadā naraḥ eṣa devi satām mārgaḥ bādhā yatra na vidyate ime manuṣyāḥ dṛśyante ūha apoha viśāradāḥ jñāna vijñāna saṃpannāḥ prajñāvantaḥ artha kovidāḥ duṣprajñāḥ ca apare deva jñāna vijñāna varjitāḥ alpa prajñaḥ virūpākṣa katham bhavati mānavaḥ jāti andhāḥ ca apare deva roga ārtāḥ ca apare tathā narāḥ klībāḥ ca dṛśyante kāraṇam brūhi tatra vai brāhmaṇān veda viduṣaḥ siddhān dharma vidaḥ tathā paripṛcchanti ahar ahar kuśala akuśalam tathā varjayanti aśubham karma sevamānāḥ śubham tathā sa ced mānuṣa tām yāti medhāvī tatra jāyate śrutam prajñā anugam ca asya kalyāṇam upajāyate para dāreṣu ye mūḍhāḥ cakṣuḥ duṣṭam prayuñjate roga ārtāḥ te bhavanti iha narāḥ duṣkṛta karmiṇaḥ ye tu mūḍhāḥ durācārāḥ viyonau maithune ratāḥ puruṣeṣu su duṣprajñāḥ klība tvam upayānti te paśūn ca ye bandhayanti ye ca eva guru talpa gāḥ prakīrṇa maithunāḥ ye ca klībāḥ jāyanti te narāḥ śreyāṃsam mārgam ātiṣṭhan sadā yaḥ pṛcchate dvijān dharma anveṣī guṇa ākāṅkṣī sa svargam samupāśnute medhāvī dhāraṇā yuktaḥ prājñaḥ tatra abhijāyate eṣa devi satām dharmaḥ mantavyaḥ bhūti kārakaḥ nṛṇām hita arthāya tava mayā vai samudāhṛtaḥ apare su alpa vijñānāḥ dharma vidveṣiṇaḥ narāḥ vratavantaḥ narāḥ ke cit śraddhā dama parāyaṇāḥ avratāḥ bhraṣṭa niyamāḥ tathā anye rākṣasa upamāḥ yajvānaḥ ca tathā eva anye nirhomāḥ ca tathā apare āgamāt loka dharmāṇām maryādāḥ pūrva nirmitāḥ prāmāṇyena anuvartante dṛśyante hi dṛḍha vratāḥ adharmam dharmam iti āhuḥ ye ca moha vaśam gatāḥ avratāḥ naṣṭa maryādāḥ te proktāḥ brahmarākṣasāḥ te ced kāla kṛta udyogāt saṃbhavanti iha mānuṣāḥ nirhomāḥ nirvaṣaṭkārāḥ te bhavanti nara adhamāḥ eṣa devi mayā sarvaḥ saṃśaya chedanāya te kuśala akuśalaḥ nṝṇām vyākhyātaḥ dharma sāgaraḥ pṛcchāmi tvām varārohe pṛṣṭā vada mama īpsitam sāvitrī brahmaṇaḥ sādhvī kauśikasya śacī satī mārtaṇḍa jasya dhūmorṇā ṛddhiḥ vaiśravaṇasya ca rohiṇī śaśinaḥ sādhvī svāhā ca eva vibhāvasoḥ aditiḥ kaśyapasya atha sarvāḥ tāḥ pati devatāḥ pṛṣṭāḥ ca upāsitāḥ ca eva tāḥ tvayā devi nityaśas strī dharmam śrotum icchāmi tvayā udāhṛtam āditas sahadharma carī me tvam sama śīlā sama vratā samāna sāra vīryā ca tapaḥ tīvram kṛtam ca te tvayā hi uktaḥ viśeṣeṇa pramāṇa tvam upaiṣyati striyaḥ ca eva viśeṣeṇa strī janasya gatiḥ sadā gauḥ gām gacchati su śroṇi lokeṣu eṣā sthitiḥ sadā mama ca ardham śarīrasya mama ca ardhāt viniḥsṛtā sura kārya karī ca tvam loka saṃtāna kāriṇī tava sarvaḥ su viditaḥ strī dharmaḥ śāśvataḥ śubhe tasmāt aśeṣatas brūhi strī dharmam vistareṇa me etābhiḥ saha saṃmantrya pravakṣyāmi anupūrvaśas strī ca bhūteśa satatam striyam eva anudhāvati mayā saṃmānitāḥ ca eva bhaviṣyanti sarit varāḥ eṣā sarasvatī puṇyā nadīnām uttamā nadī prathamā sarva saritām nadī sāgara gāminī vipāśā ca vitastā ca candrabhāgā irāvatī śatadruḥ devikā sindhuḥ kauśikī gomatī tathā tathā devanadī ca iyam sarva tīrtha abhisaṃvṛtā gaganāt gām gatāḥ devī gaṅgā sarva sarit varā iti uktvā devadevasya patnī dharma bhṛtām varā smita pūrvam iva ābhāṣya sarvāḥ tāḥ saritaḥ tadā strī dharma kuśalāḥ tāḥ vai gaṅgā ādyāḥ saritām varāḥ ayam bhagavatā dattaḥ praśnaḥ strī dharma saṃśritaḥ tam tu saṃmantrya yuṣmābhiḥ vaktum icchāmi śaṃkare na ca eka sādhyam paśyāmi vijñānam bhuvi kasya cit bhīṣmaḥ uvāca evam sarvāḥ sarit śreṣṭhāḥ pṛṣṭāḥ puṇyatamāḥ śivāḥ tatas devanadī gaṅgā niyuktā pratipūjya tām bahvībhiḥ buddhibhiḥ sphītā strī dharma jñā śuci smitā śailarājasutām devīm puṇyā pāpa apahām śivām buddhyā vinaya saṃpannā sarva jñāna viśāradā sa smitam bahu buddhi āḍhyā gaṅgā vacanam abravīt dhanyāḥ smaḥ anugṛhītāḥ smaḥ devi dharma parāyaṇā yā tvam sarva jagat mānyā nadīḥ mānayase anaghe nūnam janam aduṣṭa ātmā paṇḍita ākhyām sa gacchati jñāna vijñāna saṃpannān ūha apoha viśāradān bhīṣmaḥ uvāca tatas sā ārādhitā devī gaṅgayā bahubhiḥ guṇaiḥ prāha sarvam aśeṣeṇa strī dharmam surasundarī strī dharmaḥ pūrvaḥ eva ayam vivāhe bandhubhiḥ kṛtaḥ su svabhāvā su vacanā su vṛttā sukha darśanā an anya cittā su mukhī bhartuḥ sā dharma cāriṇī deva vat satatam sādhvī yā bhartāram prapaśyati śuśrūṣām paricāram ca deva vat yā karoti ca na anya bhāvā hi avimanāḥ suvratā sukha darśanā putra vaktram iva abhīkṣṇam bhartuḥ vadanam īkṣate yā sādhvī niyata ācārā sā bhavet dharma cāriṇī śrutvā daṃpati dharmam vai sahadharma kṛtam śubham an anya cittā su mukhī bhartuḥ sā dharma cāriṇī paruṣāṇi api ca uktā yā dṛṣṭā vā krūra cakṣuṣā su prasanna mukhī bhartuḥ yā nārī sā pativratā na candra sūryau na tarum puṃnāmnaḥ yā nirīkṣate bhartṛ varjam vara ārohā sā bhavet dharma cāriṇī patim putram iva upāste sā nārī dharma bhāginī yā nārī prayatā dakṣā yā nārī putriṇī bhavet pati priyā pati prāṇā sā nārī dharma bhāginī śuśrūṣām paricaryām ca karoti avimanāḥ sadā su pratītā vinītā ca sā nārī dharma bhāginī spṛhā yasyāḥ yathā patyau sā nārī dharma bhāginī kalya utthāna ratā nityam guru śuśrūṣaṇe ratā su saṃmṛṣṭa kṣayā ca eva go śakṛt kṛta lepanā agni kārya parā nityam sadā puṣpa bali pradā devatā atithi bhṛtyānām nirupya patinā saha śeṣa annam upabhuñjānāḥ yathānyāyam yathāvidhi tuṣṭa puṣṭa janā nityam nārī dharmeṇa yujyate śvaśrū śvaśurayoḥ pādau toṣayantī guṇa anvitā mātā pitṛ parā nityam yā nārī sā tapodhanā brāhmaṇān durbala anāthān dīna andha kṛpaṇān tathā bibharti annena yā nārī sā pati vrata bhāginī yā nārī bhartṛ paramā bhavet bhartṛ vratā śivā patiḥ hi devaḥ nārīṇām patiḥ bandhuḥ patiḥ gatiḥ patyā samā gatiḥ na asti daivatam vā yathā patiḥ pati prasādaḥ svargaḥ vā tulyaḥ nāryāḥ na vā bhavet yadi akāryam adharmam vā yadi vā prāṇa nāśanam patiḥ brūyāt daridraḥ vā vyādhitaḥ vā katham cana āpannaḥ ripu saṃsthaḥ vā brahma śāpa arditaḥ api vā āpad dharmān anuprekṣya tat kāryam aviśaṅkayā yā tu evaṃbhāvinī nārī sā bhavet dharma bhāginī bhīṣmaḥ uvāca iti uktaḥ sa tu deveśaḥ pratipūjya gireḥ sutām tatas yayuḥ bhūta gaṇāḥ saritaḥ ca yathāgatam vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ uvāca śrutvā dharmān aśeṣeṇa pāvanāni ca sarvaśas yudhiṣṭhiraḥ śāṃtanavam punar eva abhyabhāṣata kim ekam daivatam loke kim vā api ekam parāyaṇam stuvantaḥ kam kam arcantaḥ prāpnuyuḥ mānavāḥ śubham kaḥ dharmaḥ sarva dharmāṇām bhavataḥ paramaḥ mataḥ bhīṣmaḥ uvāca an ādi nidhanam viṣṇum sarva loka mahā īśvaram brahmaṇyam sarva dharma jñam lokānām kīrti vardhanam eṣa me sarva dharmāṇām dharmaḥ adhikatamaḥ mataḥ yat bhaktyā puṇḍarīkākṣam stavaiḥ arcet naraḥ sadā pavitrāṇām pavitram yaḥ maṅgalānām ca maṅgalam daivatam devatānām ca bhūtānām yaḥ avyayaḥ pitā yatas sarvāṇi bhūtāni bhavanti ādi yuga āgame viṣṇoḥ nāma sahasram me śṛṇu pāpa bhaya apaham yāni nāmāni gauṇāni vikhyātāni mahātmanaḥ ṛṣibhiḥ parigītāni tāni vakṣyāmi bhūtaye viśvam viṣṇuḥ vaṣaṭkāraḥ bhūta bhavya bhavat prabhuḥ bhūta kṛt bhūta bhṛt bhāvaḥ bhūtātmā bhūtabhāvanaḥ pūta ātmā paramātmā ca muktānām paramā gatiḥ avyayaḥ puruṣaḥ sākṣī kṣetrajñaḥ akṣaraḥ eva ca yogaḥ yoga vidām netā pradhāna puruṣa īśvaraḥ nārasiṃha vapuḥ śrīmān keśavaḥ puruṣottamaḥ sarvaḥ śarvaḥ śivaḥ sthāṇuḥ bhūtādiḥ nidhiḥ avyayaḥ saṃbhavaḥ bhāvanaḥ bhartā prabhavaḥ prabhuḥ īśvaraḥ svayaṃbhūḥ śaṃbhuḥ ādityaḥ puṣkarākṣaḥ mahā svanaḥ an ādi nidhanaḥ dhātā vidhātā dhātuḥ uttamaḥ viśvakarmā manuḥ tvaṣṭā sthaviṣṭhaḥ sthaviraḥ dhruvaḥ agrāhyaḥ śāśvataḥ kṛṣṇaḥ lohita akṣaḥ pratardanaḥ īśānaḥ prāṇa daḥ prāṇaḥ jyeṣṭhaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ prajāpatiḥ īśvaraḥ vikramī dhanvī medhāvī vikramaḥ kramaḥ anuttamaḥ durādharṣaḥ kṛtajñaḥ kṛtiḥ ātmavān sureśaḥ śaraṇam śarma viśvaretāḥ prajā bhavaḥ ahar saṃvatsaraḥ vyālaḥ pratyayaḥ sarva darśanaḥ vṛṣākapiḥ ameya ātmā sarva yoga viniḥsṛtaḥ vasuḥ vasu manāḥ satyaḥ sama ātmā saṃmitaḥ samaḥ rudraḥ bahu śirāḥ babhruḥ viśva yoniḥ śuci śravāḥ amṛtaḥ śāśvataḥ sthāṇuḥ varārohaḥ mahātapāḥ loka adhyakṣaḥ surādhyakṣaḥ dharma adhyakṣaḥ kṛtākṛtaḥ catur ātmā catur vyūhaḥ caturdaṃṣṭraḥ caturbhujaḥ bhrājiṣṇuḥ bhojanam bhoktā sahiṣṇuḥ jagadādijaḥ upendraḥ vāmanaḥ prāṃśuḥ amoghaḥ śuciḥ ūrjitaḥ ati indraḥ saṃgrahaḥ sargaḥ dhṛta ātmā niyamaḥ yamaḥ vedyaḥ vaidyaḥ sadāyogī vīra hā mādhavaḥ madhuḥ anirdeśya vapuḥ śrīmān ameya ātmā mahā adri dhṛk hiraṇyanābhaḥ sutapāḥ padmanābhaḥ prajāpatiḥ amṛtyuḥ sarva dṛś siṃhaḥ saṃdhātā saṃdhimān sthiraḥ ajaḥ durmarṣaṇaḥ śāstā viśruta ātmā surāri hā nimiṣaḥ animiṣaḥ sragvī vācaspatiḥ udāra dhīḥ agraṇīḥ grāmaṇīḥ śrīmān nyāyaḥ netā samīraṇaḥ sahasra mūrdhā viśva ātmā sahasra akṣaḥ sahasra pād āvartanaḥ nivṛtta ātmā saṃvṛtaḥ saṃpramardanaḥ satkartā satkṛtaḥ sādhuḥ jahnuḥ nārāyaṇaḥ naraḥ asaṃkhyeyaḥ aprameyātmā viśiṣṭaḥ śiṣṭa kṛt śuciḥ vṛṣā ahī vṛṣabhaḥ viṣṇuḥ vṛṣa parvā vṛṣa udaraḥ na eka rūpaḥ bṛhat rūpaḥ śipiviṣṭaḥ prakāśanaḥ ojaḥ tejaḥ dyuti dharaḥ prakāśa ātmā pratāpanaḥ ṛddhaḥ spaṣṭa akṣaraḥ mantraḥ candra aṃśuḥ bhāskara dyutiḥ yuga ādi kṛt yuga āvartaḥ na eka māyaḥ mahā aśanaḥ iṣṭaḥ viśiṣṭaḥ śiṣṭeṣṭaḥ śikhaṇḍī nahuṣaḥ vṛṣaḥ apām nidhiḥ adhiṣṭhānam apramattaḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ aśokaḥ tāraṇaḥ tāraḥ śūraḥ śauriḥ janeśvaraḥ atulaḥ śarabhaḥ bhīmaḥ samayajñaḥ haviḥ hariḥ sarva lakṣaṇa lakṣaṇyaḥ lakṣmīvān samitiṃjayaḥ udbhavaḥ kṣobhaṇaḥ devaḥ śrīgarbhaḥ parameśvaraḥ karaṇam kāraṇam kartā vikartā gahanaḥ guhaḥ pararddhiḥ paramaḥ spaṣṭaḥ tuṣṭaḥ puṣṭaḥ śubha īkṣaṇaḥ vīraḥ śaktimatām śreṣṭhaḥ dharmaḥ dharma vid uttamaḥ hiraṇya garbhaḥ śatru ghnaḥ vyāptaḥ vāyuḥ adhokṣajaḥ ṛtuḥ sudarśanaḥ kālaḥ parameṣṭhī parigrahaḥ ugraḥ saṃvatsaraḥ dakṣaḥ viśrāmaḥ viśva dakṣiṇaḥ vistāraḥ sthāvaraḥ sthāṇuḥ pramāṇam bījam avyayam anirviṇṇaḥ sthaviṣṭhaḥ bhūḥ dharma yūpaḥ mahā makhaḥ yajñaḥ ijyaḥ mahā ijyaḥ ca kratuḥ satram satām gatiḥ sarva darśī vimukta ātmā sarvajñaḥ jñānam uttamam suvrataḥ sumukhaḥ sūkṣmaḥ su ghoṣaḥ sukha daḥ suhṛd svāpanaḥ svavaśaḥ vyāpī na eka ātmā na eka karma kṛt avijñātā sahasrāṃśuḥ vidhātā kṛtalakṣaṇaḥ uttaraḥ gopatiḥ goptā jñāna gamyaḥ purātanaḥ śarīra bhūta bhṛt bhoktā kapi indraḥ bhūri dakṣiṇaḥ vinayaḥ jayaḥ satya saṃdhaḥ dāśārhaḥ sātvatām patiḥ jīvaḥ vinayitā sākṣī mukundaḥ amita vikramaḥ mahā ṛṣiḥ kapila ācāryaḥ kṛtajñaḥ medinīpatiḥ tripadaḥ tridaśādhyakṣaḥ mahāśṛṅgaḥ kṛtānta kṛt vedhāḥ svāṅgaḥ ajitaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ dṛḍhaḥ saṃkarṣaṇaḥ acyutaḥ varuṇaḥ vāruṇaḥ vṛkṣaḥ puṣkara akṣaḥ mahā manāḥ ādityaḥ jyotiḥ ādityaḥ sahiṣṇuḥ gati sattamaḥ su dhanvā khaṇḍa paraśuḥ dāruṇaḥ draviṇa pradaḥ divaḥspṛś sarva dṛś vyāsaḥ vācaspatiḥ ayonijaḥ tri sāmā sāmagaḥ sāma nirvāṇam bheṣajam bhiṣak saṃnyāsa kṛt śamaḥ śāntaḥ niṣṭhā śāntiḥ parāyaṇam śubhāṅgaḥ śāntidaḥ sraṣṭā kumudaḥ kuvaleśayaḥ go hitaḥ go patiḥ goptā vṛṣabha akṣaḥ vṛṣa priyaḥ śrīdharaḥ śrīkaraḥ śreyaḥ śrīmān lokatraya āśrayaḥ vijita ātmā vidheya ātmā sat kīrtiḥ chinna saṃśayaḥ udīrṇaḥ sarvatas cakṣuḥ anīśaḥ śāśvataḥ sthiraḥ bhūśayaḥ bhūṣaṇaḥ bhūtiḥ viśokaḥ śokanāśanaḥ arciṣmān arcitaḥ kumbhaḥ viśuddha ātmā viśodhanaḥ anirdeśya vapuḥ viṣṇuḥ vīraḥ anantaḥ dhanaṃjayaḥ mahā kratuḥ mahā yajvā mahā yajñaḥ mahā haviḥ stavyaḥ stava priyaḥ stotram stutiḥ stotā raṇa priyaḥ pūrṇaḥ pūrayitā puṇyaḥ puṇya kīrtiḥ anāmayaḥ śūrasenaḥ yadu śreṣṭhaḥ sannivāsaḥ suyāmunaḥ bhūta āvāsaḥ sarva asu nilayaḥ analaḥ viśvamūrtiḥ mahā mūrtiḥ dīpta mūrtiḥ a mūrtimān aneka mūrtiḥ avyaktaḥ śata mūrtiḥ śata ānanaḥ suvarṇavarṇaḥ hemāṅgaḥ varāṅgaḥ candanāṅgadī vīra hā viṣamaḥ śūnyaḥ ghṛta āśīḥ acalaḥ calaḥ amānī mānadaḥ mānyaḥ lokasvāmī tejaḥ vṛṣaḥ dyuti dharaḥ sarva śastrabhṛtām varaḥ catur mūrtiḥ catur bāhuḥ catur vyūhaḥ catur gatiḥ śubhāṅgaḥ lokasāraṅgaḥ sutantuḥ tantuvardhanaḥ arkaḥ vāja sanaḥ śṛṅgī jayantaḥ sarva vid jayī suvarṇa binduḥ akṣobhyaḥ sarva vāc īśvara īśvaraḥ sahasra arciḥ sapta jihvaḥ sapta edhāḥ sapta vāhanaḥ aṇuḥ bṛhat kṛśaḥ sthūlaḥ guṇa bhṛt nirguṇaḥ mahān adhṛtaḥ sva dhṛtaḥ su āsyaḥ prāgvaṃśaḥ vaṃśa vardhanaḥ bhārabhṛt kathitaḥ yogī yogīśaḥ sarva kāma daḥ āśramaḥ śramaṇaḥ kṣāmaḥ suparṇaḥ vāyu vāhanaḥ sattvavān sāttvikaḥ satyaḥ satya dharma parāyaṇaḥ anirviṇṇaḥ sadā amarṣī loka adhiṣṭhānam adbhutam akrūraḥ peśalaḥ dakṣaḥ dakṣiṇaḥ kṣamiṇām varaḥ uttāraṇaḥ duṣkṛti hā puṇyaḥ duḥsvapna nāśanaḥ vīra hā rakṣaṇaḥ santaḥ jīvanaḥ paryavasthitaḥ caturasraḥ gabhīra ātmā vidiśaḥ vyādiśaḥ diśaḥ anādiḥ bhūḥ bhuvaḥ lakṣmīḥ suvīraḥ rucira aṅgadaḥ ūrdhvagaḥ sat patha ācāraḥ prāṇa daḥ praṇavaḥ paṇaḥ pramāṇam prāṇa nilayaḥ prāṇa kṛt prāṇa jīvanaḥ bhūḥ bhuvaḥ svar taruḥ tāraḥ savitā prapitāmahaḥ yajñaḥ yajñapatiḥ yajvā yajña aṅgaḥ yajña vāhanaḥ ātmayoniḥ svayaṃjātaḥ vaikhānaḥ sāma gāyanaḥ śaṅkhabhṛt nandakī cakrī śārṅgadhanvā gadā dharaḥ rathāṅga pāṇiḥ akṣobhyaḥ sarva praharaṇa āyudhaḥ iti idam kīrtanīyasya keśavasya mahātmanaḥ nāmnām sahasram divyānām aśeṣeṇa prakīrtitam yaḥ idam śṛṇuyāt nityam yaḥ ca api parikīrtayet na aśubham prāpnuyāt kim cit saḥ amutra iha ca mānavaḥ veda antagaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ syāt kṣatriyaḥ vijayī bhavet vaiśyaḥ dhana samṛddhaḥ syāt śūdraḥ sukham avāpnuyāt dharma arthī prāpnuyāt dharmam artha arthī ca artham āpnuyāt kāmān avāpnuyāt kāmī prajā arthī ca āpnuyāt prajāḥ yaśaḥ prāpnoti vipulam jñāti prādhānyam eva ca acalām śriyam āpnoti śreyaḥ ca āpnoti anuttamam bhayāt mucyeta bhītaḥ ca mucyeta āpannaḥ āpadaḥ durgāṇi atitarati āśu puruṣaḥ puruṣottamam vāsudeva āśrayaḥ martyaḥ vāsudeva parāyaṇaḥ sarva pāpa viśuddha ātmā yāti brahma sanātanam janma mṛtyu jarā vyādhi bhayam vā api upajāyate imam stavam adhīyānaḥ śraddhā bhakti samanvitaḥ yujyeta ātma sukha kṣānti śrī dhṛti smṛti kīrtibhiḥ na krodhaḥ na ca mātsaryam na lobhaḥ na aśubhā matiḥ bhavanti kṛta puṇyānām bhaktānām puruṣottame dyauḥ sa candra arka nakṣatrā kham diśaḥ bhūḥ mahodadhiḥ vāsudevasya vīryeṇa vidhṛtāni mahātmanaḥ jagat vaśe vartata idam kṛṣṇasya sacarācaram indriyāṇi manaḥ buddhiḥ sattvam tejaḥ balam dhṛtiḥ vāsudeva ātmakāni āhuḥ kṣetram kṣetrajñaḥ eva ca sarva āgamānām ācāraḥ prathamam parikalpyate ṛṣayaḥ pitaraḥ devāḥ mahābhūtāni dhātavaḥ jaṅgama ajaṅgamam ca idam jagat nārāyaṇa udbhavam yogaḥ jñānam tathā sāṃkhyam vidyāḥ śilpāni karma ca vedāḥ śāstrāṇi vijñānam etat sarvam janārdanāt ekaḥ viṣṇuḥ mahat bhūtam pṛthak bhūtāni anekaśas trīn lokān vyāpya bhūtātmā bhuṅkte viśva bhuj avyayaḥ imam stavam bhagavataḥ viṣṇoḥ vyāsena kīrtitam paṭhet yaḥ icchet puruṣaḥ śreyaḥ prāptum sukhāni ca bhajanti ye puṣkarākṣam na te yānti parābhavam yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca ke pūjyāḥ ke namaskāryāḥ katham varteta keṣu ca kimācāraḥ kīdṛśeṣu pitāmaha na riṣyate bhīṣmaḥ uvāca brāhmaṇānām paribhavaḥ sādayet api devatāḥ brāhmaṇānām namaskartā yudhiṣṭhira na riṣyate te hi lokān imān sarvān dhārayanti manīṣiṇaḥ brāhmaṇāḥ sarva lokānām mahāntaḥ dharma setavaḥ dhana tyāga abhirāmāḥ ca vāc saṃyama ratāḥ ca ye ramaṇīyāḥ ca bhūtānām nidhānam ca dhṛta vratāḥ praṇetāraḥ ca lokānām śāstrāṇām ca yaśasvinaḥ tapaḥ yeṣām dhanam nityam vāc ca eva vipulam balam prabhavaḥ ca api dharmāṇām dharma jñāḥ sūkṣma darśinaḥ yān upāśritya jīvanti prajāḥ sarvāḥ caturvidhāḥ panthānaḥ sarva netāraḥ yajña vāhāḥ sanātanāḥ pitṛpaitāmahīm gurvīm udvahanti dhuram sadā dīpāḥ sarvasya lokasya cakṣuḥ cakṣuṣmatām api sarva śilpa ādi nidhayaḥ nipuṇāḥ sūkṣma darśinaḥ gati jñāḥ sarva bhūtānām adhyātma gati cintakāḥ ādi madhya avasānānām jñātāraḥ chinna saṃśayāḥ parāvara viśeṣa jñāḥ gantāraḥ paramām gatim vimuktāḥ dhuta pāpmānaḥ nirdvaṃdvāḥ niṣparigrahāḥ māna arhāḥ mānitāḥ nityam jñāna vidbhiḥ mahātmabhiḥ samam yeṣām dukūlam ca śāṇa kṣauma ajināni ca tiṣṭheyuḥ api a bhuñjānāḥ bahūni divasāni api śoṣayeyuḥ ca gātrāṇi svādhyāyaiḥ saṃyata indriyāḥ lokān anyān sṛjeyuḥ ca lokapālān ca kopitāḥ apeyaḥ sāgaraḥ yeṣām abhiśāpāt mahātmanām yeṣām kopa agniḥ adyā api daṇḍake nā upaśāmyati devānām api ye devāḥ kāraṇam kāraṇasya ca pramāṇasya pramāṇam ca kaḥ tān abhibhavet budhaḥ yeṣām vṛddhaḥ ca bālaḥ ca sarvaḥ saṃmānam arhati a vidvān brāhmaṇaḥ devaḥ pātram vai pāvanam mahat vidvān bhūyastaraḥ devaḥ pūrṇa sāgara saṃnibhaḥ a vidvān ca eva vidvān ca brāhmaṇaḥ daivatam mahat praṇītaḥ ca apraṇītaḥ ca yathā agniḥ daivatam mahat śmaśāne hi api tejasvī pāvakaḥ nā eva duṣyati yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca kām tu brāhmaṇa pūjāyām vyuṣṭim dṛṣṭvā janādhipa kam vā karma udayam matvā tān arcasi mahāmate bhīṣmaḥ uvāca atrā api udāharanti imam itihāsam purātanam asya lokasya sarvasya māhiṣmatyām mahā balaḥ sa tu ratna ākaravatīm sa dvīpām sāgara ambarām śaśāsa sarvām pṛthivīm haihayaḥ satya vikramaḥ sva vittam tena dattam tu dattātreyāya kāraṇe ārādhayām āsa ca tam kṛtavīrya ātmajaḥ munim nyamantrayata saṃhṛṣṭaḥ sa dvijaḥ ca varaiḥ tribhiḥ sahasra bāhuḥ bhūyām vai camū madhye gṛhe anyathā mama bāhu sahasram tu paśyantām sainikāḥ raṇe vikrameṇa mahīm kṛtsnām jayeyam vipula vrata tām ca dharmeṇa saṃprāpya pālayeyam atandritaḥ anuśāsantu mām santaḥ mithyā vṛttam tad āśrayam abravīt vīrya saṃmohāt kaḥ nu asti sadṛśaḥ mayā vīrya dhairya yaśaḥ śaucaiḥ vikrameṇa ojasā api vā tad vākya ante ca antarikṣe vāc uvāca aśarīriṇī na tvam mūḍha vijānīṣe brāhmaṇam kṣatriyāt varam sahitaḥ brāhmaṇena iha kṣatriyaḥ rakṣati prajāḥ kuryām bhūtāni tuṣṭaḥ aham kruddhaḥ nāśam tathā naye karmaṇā manasā vācā na mattaḥ asti varaḥ dvijaḥ brāhmaṇāḥ saṃśritāḥ kṣatram na kṣatram brāhmaṇa āśritam śritān brahma upadhāḥ viprāḥ khādanti kṣatriyān bhuvi kṣatriyeṣu āśritaḥ dharmaḥ prajānām paripālanam kṣatrāt vṛttiḥ brāhmaṇānām taiḥ katham brāhmaṇaḥ varaḥ sarva bhūta pradhānān tān bhaikṣa vṛttīn aham sadā ātma saṃbhāvitān viprān sthāpayāmi ātmanaḥ vaśe kathitam hi anayā satyam gāyatryā kanyayā divi vijeṣyāmi avaśān sarvān brāhmaṇān carma vāsasaḥ na ca mām cyāvayet rāṣṭrāt triṣu lokeṣu kaḥ cana devaḥ vā mānuṣaḥ vā api tasmāt jyeṣṭhaḥ dvijāt aham arjunasya vacaḥ śrutvā vitrastā abhūt niśācarī tyaja enam kaluṣam bhāvam brāhmaṇebhyaḥ namaskuru eteṣām kurvataḥ pāpam rāṣṭra kṣobhaḥ hi te bhavet atha vā tvām mahīpāla śamayiṣyanti vai dvijāḥ nirasiṣyanti vā rāṣṭrāt hata utsāham mahā balāḥ tam rājā kaḥ tvam iti āha tatas tam prāha mārutaḥ aho tvayā adya vipreṣu bhakti rāgaḥ pradarśitaḥ yādṛśam pṛthivī bhūtam tādṛśam brūhi vai dvijam vāyoḥ vā sadṛśam kim cit brūhi tvam brāhmaṇa uttamam apām vai sadṛśam brūhi sūryasya nabhasaḥ api vā vāyuḥ uvāca śṛṇu mūḍha guṇān kān cit brāhmaṇānām mahātmanām ye tvayā kīrtitāḥ rājan tebhyaḥ atha brāhmaṇaḥ varaḥ tyaktvā mahī tvam bhūmiḥ tu spardhayā aṅga nṛpasya ha nāśam jagāma tām vipraḥ vyaṣṭambhayata kaśyapaḥ akṣayāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ rājan divi ca iha ca nityadā apibat tejasā hi āpaḥ svayam eva aṅgirāḥ purā sa tāḥ piban kṣīram iva na atṛpyata mahā tapāḥ apūrayat mahā oghena mahīm sarvām ca pārthiva ahalyām kāmayānaḥ vai dharma artham ca na hiṃsitaḥ tathā samudraḥ nṛpate pūrṇaḥ mṛṣṭena vāriṇā brāhmaṇaiḥ abhiśaptaḥ san lavaṇodaḥ kṛtaḥ vibho suvarṇa varṇaḥ nirdhūmaḥ saṃhata ūrdhva śikhaḥ kaviḥ suvarṇa dhāriṇā nityam avaśaptāḥ dvijātinā samaḥ na tvam dvijātibhyaḥ śreṣṭham viddhi narādhipa daṇḍakānām mahat rājyam brāhmaṇena vināśitam tālajaṅgham mahat kṣatram aurveṇa ekena nāśitam tvayā ca vipulam rājyam balam dharmaḥ śrutam tathā atha vā brāhmaṇa śreṣṭham anu bhūta anupālakam yena idam nikhilam viśvam janitam sthāvaram caram aṇḍa jātam tu brahmāṇam ke cid icchanti apaṇḍitāḥ aṇḍāt bhinnāt babhuḥ śailāḥ diśaḥ ambhaḥ pṛthivī divam draṣṭavyam nā etat evam hi katham jyāyastamaḥ hi saḥ smṛtam ākāśam aṇḍam tu tasmāt jātaḥ pitāmahaḥ na asti aṇḍam asti tu brahmā sa rājan loka bhāvanaḥ iti uktaḥ sa tadā tūṣṇīm abhūt vāyuḥ tam abravīt vāyuḥ uvāca imām bhūmim brāhmaṇebhyaḥ ditsuḥ vai dakṣiṇām purā aṅgaḥ nāma nṛpaḥ rājan tatas cintām mahī yayau dhāraṇīm sarva bhūtānām ayam prāpya varaḥ nṛpaḥ katham icchati mām dātum dvijebhyaḥ brahmaṇaḥ sutām sā aham tyaktvā gamiṣyāmi bhūmi tvam brahmaṇaḥ padam ayam sa rāṣṭraḥ nṛpatiḥ mā bhūt iti tatas agamat tatas tām kaśyapaḥ dṛṣṭvā vrajantīm pṛthivīm tadā praviveśa mahīm sadyas muktvā ātmānam samāhitaḥ ruddhā sā sarvatas jajñe tṛṇa oṣadhi samanvitā dharma uttarā naṣṭa bhayā bhūmiḥ āsīt tatas nṛpa evam varṣa sahasrāṇi divyāni vipula vrataḥ triṃśatam kaśyapaḥ rājan bhūmiḥ āsīt atandritaḥ pṛthivī kāśyapī jajñe sutā tasya mahātmanaḥ eṣa rājan īdṛśaḥ vai brāhmaṇaḥ kaśyapaḥ abhavat anyam prabrūhi vā api tvam kaśyapāt kṣatriyam varam tūṣṇīm babhūva nṛpatiḥ pavanaḥ tu abravīt punar śṛṇu rājan utathyasya jātasya āṅgirase kule bhadrā somasya duhitā rūpeṇa paramā matā sā ca tīvram tapaḥ tepe mahābhāgā yaśasvinī utathyam tu mahābhāgam tad kṛte avarayat tadā tatas āhūya sā utathyam dadau atra yaśasvinīm tām tu akāmayata śrīmān varuṇaḥ pūrvam eva ha sa ca āgamya vanaprastham yamunāyām jahāra tām parama adbhuta saṃkāśam ṣaṣ sahasra śatahradam prāsādaiḥ apsarobhiḥ ca divyaiḥ kāmaiḥ ca śobhitam tatra devaḥ tayā sārdham reme rājan jaleśvaraḥ provāca gaccha brūhi tvam varuṇam paruṣam vacaḥ mad vākyāt muñca me bhāryām kasmāt vā hṛtavān asi somena dattā bhāryā me tvayā ca apahṛtā adya vai mama eṣā su priyā bhāryā na enām utsraṣṭum utsahe iti uktaḥ varuṇena atha nāradaḥ prāpya tam munim utathyam abravīt vākyam na ati hṛṣṭa manāḥ iva gale gṛhītvā kṣiptaḥ asmi varuṇena mahā mune nāradasya vacaḥ śrutvā kruddhaḥ prājvalat aṅgirāḥ apibat tejasā vāri viṣṭabhya su mahā tapāḥ suhṛdbhiḥ kṣipyamāṇaḥ api na eva amuñcata tām tadā tatas tat iriṇam jātam samudraḥ ca apasarpitaḥ tasmāt deśāt nadīm ca eva provāca asau dvijottamaḥ adṛśyā gaccha bhīru tvam sarasvati marum prati tasmin saṃcūrṇite deśe bhadrām ādāya vāripaḥ adadāt śaraṇam gatvā bhāryām āṅgirasāya vai pratigṛhya tu tām bhāryām utathyaḥ su manāḥ bhavat tatas sa labdhvā tām bhāryām varuṇam prāha dharma vid utathyaḥ su mahā tejāḥ yat tat śṛṇu narādhipa mayā eṣā tapasā prāptā krośataḥ te jalādhipa eṣa rājan īdṛśaḥ vai utathyaḥ brāhmaṇa ṛṣabhaḥ bravīmi aham brūhi vā tvam utathyāt kṣatriyam varam bhīṣmaḥ uvāca iti uktaḥ sa tadā tūṣṇīm abhūt vāyuḥ tatas abravīt śṛṇu rājan agastyasya māhātmyam brāhmaṇasya ha asuraiḥ nirjitāḥ devāḥ nirutsāhāḥ ca te kṛtāḥ yajñāḥ ca eṣām hṛtāḥ sarve pitṛbhyaḥ ca svadhā tathā karma ijyāḥ mānavānām ca dānavaiḥ haihaya ṛṣabha bhraṣṭa aiśvaryāḥ tatas devāḥ ceruḥ pṛthvīm iti śrutiḥ abhivādya ca tam devāḥ dṛṣṭvā ca yaśasā vṛtam idam ūcuḥ mahātmānam vākyam kāle janādhipa dānavaiḥ yudhi bhagnāḥ sma tathā aiśvaryāt ca bhraṃśitāḥ tat asmān naḥ bhayāt tīvrāt trāhi tvam muni puṃgava prajajvāla ca tejasvī kālāgniḥ iva saṃkṣaye tena dīpta aṃśu jālena nirdagdhāḥ dānavāḥ tadā antarikṣāt mahā rāja nyapatanta sahasraśas ubhau lokau parityajya yayuḥ kāṣṭhām sma dakṣiṇām baliḥ tu yajate yajñam aśvamedham mahīm gataḥ ye anye svasthāḥ mahī sthāḥ ca te na dagdhāḥ mahā asurāḥ tatas lokāḥ punar prāptāḥ suraiḥ śāntam ca tat rajaḥ atha enam abruvan devāḥ bhūmiṣṭhān asurān jahi dagdhum tapaḥ hi kṣīyet me dhakṣyāmi iti ca pārthiva evam dagdhāḥ bhagavatā dānavāḥ svena tejasā agastyena tadā rājan tapasā bhāvitātmanā īdṛśaḥ ca api agastyaḥ hi kathitaḥ te mayā anagha bravīmi aham brūhi vā tvam agastyāt kṣatriyam varam iti uktaḥ sa tadā tūṣṇīm abhūt vāyuḥ tatas abravīt śṛṇu rājan vasiṣṭhasya mukhyam karma yaśasvinaḥ ādityāḥ satram āsanta saraḥ vai mānasam prati vasiṣṭham manasā gatvā śrutvā tatra asya gocaram yajamānān tu tān dṛṣṭvā vyagrān dīkṣā anukarśitān hantum icchanti śaila ābhāḥ khalinaḥ nāma dānavāḥ adūrāt tu tatas teṣām brahmadatta varam saraḥ hatāḥ hatāḥ vai te tatra jīvanti āplutya dānavāḥ tatas taiḥ arditāḥ devāḥ śaraṇam vāsavam yayuḥ sa ca taiḥ vyathitaḥ śakraḥ vasiṣṭham śaraṇam yayau tatas abhayam dadau tebhyaḥ vasiṣṭhaḥ bhagavān ṛṣiḥ tathā tān duḥkhitān jānan ānṛśaṃsya paraḥ muniḥ kailāsam prasthitām ca api nadīm gaṅgām mahā tapāḥ saraḥ bhinnam tayā nadyā sarayūḥ sā tatas abhavat evam sa indrāḥ vasiṣṭhena rakṣitāḥ tridivaukasaḥ brahma datta varāḥ ca eva hatāḥ daityāḥ mahātmanā bravīmi aham brūhi vā tvam vasiṣṭhāt kṣatriyam varam bhīṣmaḥ uvāca iti uktaḥ tu arjunaḥ tūṣṇīm abhūt vāyuḥ tam abravīt śṛṇu me haihaya śreṣṭha karma atreḥ su mahātmanaḥ devāḥ nṛpati śārdūla saha eva balibhiḥ tadā asuraiḥ vadhyamānāḥ te kṣīṇa prāṇāḥ divaukasaḥ vayam vadhyāmahe ca api śatrubhiḥ tamasā āvṛte na adhigacchāma śāntim ca bhayāt trāyasva naḥ prabho dṛṣṭvā na ati prabham somam tathā sūryam ca pārthiva vyajayat śatru saṃghān ca devānām svena tejasā atriṇā dahyamānān tān dṛṣṭvā devāḥ mahā asurān udbhāsitaḥ ca savitā devāḥ trātā hata asurāḥ advitīyena muninā japatā carma vāsasā phala bhakṣeṇa rāja ṛṣe paśya karma atriṇā kṛtam tasya api vistareṇa uktam karma atreḥ su mahātmanaḥ bravīmi aham brūhi vā tvam atritaḥ kṣatriyam varam iti uktaḥ tu arjunaḥ tūṣṇīm abhūt vāyuḥ tam abravīt śṛṇu rājan mahat karma cyavanasya mahātmanaḥ aśvinoḥ pratisaṃśrutya cyavanaḥ pākaśāsanam aśvibhyām saha na icchāmaḥ pātum somam mahā vrata pibantu anye yathākāmam na aham pātum iha utsahe tatas karma samārabdham hitāya sahasā aśvinoḥ tat tu karma samārabdham dṛṣṭvā indraḥ krodha mūrchitaḥ tathā vajreṇa bhagavān amarṣa ākula locanaḥ tam āpatantam dṛṣṭvā eva cyavanaḥ tapasā anvitaḥ madam mantra āhuti mayam vyādita āsyam mahā muniḥ dvi yojana śatāḥ tasya daṃṣṭrāḥ parama dāruṇāḥ hanuḥ tasya bhavat bhūmau ekaḥ ca asya aspṛśat divam jihvā mūle sthitāḥ tasya sarve devāḥ sa vāsavāḥ timeḥ āsyam anuprāptāḥ yathā matsyāḥ mahā arṇave abruvan sahitāḥ śakram praṇama asmai dvijātaye aśvibhyām saha somam ca pibāmaḥ vigata jvarāḥ tatas sa praṇataḥ śakraḥ cakāra cyavanasya tat cyavanaḥ kṛtavān tau ca api aśvinau soma pīthinau akṣeṣu mṛgayāyām ca pāne strīṣu ca vīryavān etaiḥ doṣaiḥ naraḥ rājan kṣayam yāti na saṃśayaḥ bravīmi aham brūhi vā tvam cyavanāt kṣatriyam varam bhīṣmaḥ uvāca tūṣṇīm āsīt arjunaḥ tu pavanaḥ tu abravīt punar śṛṇu me brāhmaṇeṣu eva mukhyam karma janādhipa madasya āsyam anuprāptāḥ yadā sa indrāḥ divaukasaḥ tadā iyam cyavanena iha hṛtā teṣām vasuṃdharā śoka ārtāḥ ca mahātmānam brahmāṇam śaraṇam yayuḥ devāḥ ūcuḥ mad āsya vyatiṣiktānām asmākam loka pūjita cyavanena hṛtā bhūmiḥ kapaiḥ ca api divam prabho gacchadhvam śaraṇam viprān āśu sa indrāḥ divaukasaḥ prasādya tān ubhau lokau avāpsyatha yathā purā te yayuḥ śaraṇam viprān te ūcuḥ kān jayāmahe tatas karma samārabdham brāhmaṇaiḥ kapanāśanam tat śrutvā preṣitaḥ dūtaḥ brāhmaṇebhyaḥ dhanī kapaiḥ sa ca tān brāhmaṇān āha dhanī kapavacaḥ yathā bhavadbhiḥ sadṛśāḥ sarve kapāḥ kim iha vartate sarve veda vidaḥ prājñāḥ sarve ca kratu yājinaḥ śrīḥ ca eva ramate teṣu dhārayanti śriyam ca te vṛthā dārān na gacchanti vṛthāmāṃsam na bhuñjate dīptam agnim juhvati ca gurūṇām vacane sthitāḥ sarve ca niyata ātmānaḥ bālānām saṃvibhāginaḥ etaiḥ ca anyaiḥ ca bahubhiḥ guṇaiḥ yuktān katham kapān vijeṣyatha nivartadhvam nivṛttānām śubham hi vaḥ brāhmaṇāḥ ūcuḥ kapān vayam vijeṣyāmaḥ ye devāḥ te vayam smṛtāḥ tasmāt vadhyāḥ kapā asmākam dhanin yāhi yathāgatam dhanī gatvā kapān āha na vaḥ viprāḥ priyaṃkarāḥ gṛhītvā astrāṇi atho viprān kapāḥ sarve samādravan samudagra dhvajān dṛṣṭvā kapān sarve dvijātayaḥ vyasṛjan jvalitān agnīn kapānām prāṇa nāśanān brahma sṛṣṭāḥ havyabhujaḥ bhuktvā sanātanāḥ nabhasi iva yathā abhrāṇi vyarājanta narādhipa praśaśaṃsuḥ dvijān ca eva brahmāṇam ca yaśasvinam teṣām tejaḥ tathā vīryam devānām vavṛdhe tatas avāpnuvan ca amara tvam triṣu lokeṣu pūjitam pratipūjya mahā bāho yat tat śṛṇu narādhipa jīvāmi aham brāhmaṇa arthe sarvathā satatam prabho brahmaṇe brāhmaṇebhyaḥ ca praṇamāmi ca nityaśas dattātreya prasādāt ca mayā prāptam idam yaśaḥ aho brāhmaṇa karmāṇi yathā māruta tattvataḥ vāyuḥ uvāca brāhmaṇān kṣatra dharmeṇa pālayasva indriyāṇi ca yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca brāhmaṇān arcase rājan satatam saṃśita vratān kam tu karma udayam dṛṣṭvā tān arcasi narādhipa kām vā brāhmaṇa pūjāyām vyuṣṭim dṛṣṭvā mahāvrata bhīṣmaḥ uvāca eṣa te keśavaḥ sarvam ākhyāsyati mahāmatiḥ vyuṣṭim brāhmaṇa pūjāyām dṛṣṭa vyuṣṭiḥ mahā vrataḥ balam śrotre vāc manaḥ cakṣuṣī ca jñānam tathā na viśuddham mama adya deha nyāsaḥ na ati cirāt mataḥ me na ca ati tūrṇam savitā adya yāti uktāḥ dharmāḥ ye purāṇe mahāntaḥ brāhmaṇānām kṣatriyāṇām viśām ca paurāṇam ye daṇḍam upāsate ca śeṣam kṛṣṇāt upaśikṣasva pārtha aham hi enam vedmi tattvena kṛṣṇam yaḥ ayam hi yat ca asya balam purāṇam ameya ātmā keśavaḥ kaurava indra saḥ ayam dharmam vakṣyati saṃśayeṣu kṛṣṇaḥ pṛthvīm asṛjat kham divam ca varāhaḥ ayam bhīma balaḥ purāṇaḥ asya ca adhas atha antarikṣam divam ca diśaḥ catasraḥ pradiśaḥ catasraḥ sṛṣṭiḥ tathā eva iyam anuprasūtā sa nirmame viśvam idam purāṇam asya nābhyām puṣkaram saṃprasūtam yatra utpannaḥ svayam eva amita ojāḥ yena ācchinnam tat tamaḥ pārtha ghoram yat tat tiṣṭhati arṇavam tarjayānam kṛte yuge dharmaḥ āsīt samagraḥ tretā kāle jñānam anuprapannaḥ balam tu āsīt dvāpare pārtha kṛṣṇaḥ kalau adharmaḥ kṣitim ājagāma sa bhūtānām bhāvanaḥ bhūta bhavyaḥ sa viśvasya asya jagataḥ ca api goptā yadā dharmaḥ glāyati vai surāṇām tadā kṛṣṇaḥ jāyate mānuṣeṣu dharme sthitvā sa tu vai bhāvitātmā parān ca lokān aparān ca yāti tyājyān tyaktvā atha asurāṇām vadhāya kārya akārye kāraṇam ca eva pārtha sa viśva karmā sa ca viśva rūpaḥ sa viśva bhṛt viśva sṛj viśva jit ca tam gandharvāḥ apsarasaḥ ca nityam upatiṣṭhante vibudhānām śatāni tam rākṣasāḥ ca parisaṃvahante rāyaspoṣaḥ sa vijigīṣuḥ ekaḥ sa paurāṇīm brahma guhām praviṣṭaḥ mahī satram bhārata agre dadarśa sa ca eva gām uddadhāra agrya karmā vikṣobhya daityān uragān dānavān ca tasya antarikṣam pṛthivī divam ca sarvam vaśe tiṣṭhati śāśvatasya sa kumbharetāḥ sasṛje purāṇam yatra utpannam ṛṣim āhuḥ vasiṣṭham sa mātariśvā vibhuḥ aśva vājī sa raśmimān savitā ca ādidevaḥ tena asurāḥ vijitāḥ sarve eva tasya vikrāntaiḥ vijitāni iha trīṇi sa devānām mānuṣāṇām pitṝṇām tam eva āhuḥ yajña vidām vitānam tam brāhmaṇāḥ veda vidaḥ juṣanti tasya ādityaḥ bhām upayujya bhāti mahā tejāḥ sarva gaḥ sarva siṃhaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ lokān dhārayate tathā ekaḥ aśnan an aśnan ca tathā eva dhīraḥ kṛṣṇam sadā pārtha kartāram ehi saḥ ekadā kakṣa gataḥ mahātmā tṛptaḥ vibhuḥ khāṇḍave dhūmaketuḥ saḥ eva aśvaḥ śvetam aśvam prayacchat saḥ eva aśvān atha sarvān cakāra evam ramyān asṛjat parvatān ca hṛṣīkeśaḥ amita dīpta agni tejāḥ durvāsāḥ vai tena na anyena śakyaḥ gṛhe rājan vāsayitum mahā ojāḥ tam eva āhuḥ ṛṣim ekam purāṇam sa viśva kṛt vidadhāti ātma bhāvān vedān ca yaḥ vedayate adhidevaḥ vidhīn ca yaḥ ca āśrayate purāṇān jyotīṃṣi śuklāni ca sarva loke trayaḥ lokāḥ lokapālāḥ trayaḥ ca saṃvatsaraḥ saḥ ṛtuḥ saḥ ardha māsaḥ saḥ ahorātraḥ sa kalā vai sa kāṣṭhāḥ mātrāḥ muhūrtāḥ ca lavāḥ kṣaṇāḥ ca viṣvaksene sarvam etat pratīhi candra ādityau graha nakṣatra tārāḥ sarvāṇi darśāni atha paurṇamāsyaḥ rudra ādityāḥ vasavaḥ atha aśvinau ca sādhyāḥ viśve marutām ṣaṭ gaṇāḥ ca prajāpatiḥ deva mātā aditiḥ ca sarve kṛṣṇāt ṛṣayaḥ ca eva sapta vāyuḥ bhūtvā vikṣipate ca viśvam agniḥ bhūtvā dahate viśva rūpaḥ āpaḥ bhūtvā majjayate ca sarvam brahmā bhūtvā sṛjate viśva saṃghān jyotiḥ bhūtaḥ paramaḥ asau purastāt prakāśayan prabhayā viśva rūpaḥ apaḥ sṛṣṭvā hi ātmabhūḥ ātmayoniḥ purā akarot sarvam eva atha viśvam ṛtūn utpātān vividhāni adbhutāni meghān vidyut sarvam airāvatam ca sarvam kṛṣṇāt sthāvaram jaṅgamam ca viśva ākhyātāt viṣṇum enam pratīhi viśvāvāsam nirguṇam vāsudevam saṃkarṣaṇam jīva bhūtam vadanti sa pañcadhā pañca jana upapannam saṃcodayan viśvam idam sisṛkṣuḥ tatas bhūmim vyadadhāt pañca bījām dyauḥ pṛthivyām dhāsyati bhūri vāri tatas devān asurān mānuṣān ca lokān ṛṣīn ca atha pitṝn prajāḥ ca samāsena vividhān prāṇi lokān sarvān sadā bhūtapatiḥ sisṛkṣuḥ śubha aśubham sthāvaram jaṅgamam ca mṛtyuḥ ca eva prāṇinām antakāle sākṣāt kṛṣṇaḥ śāśvataḥ dharma vāhaḥ yat praśastam ca lokeṣu puṇyam yat ca śubha aśubham etādṛśaḥ keśavaḥ ayam svayaṃbhūḥ nārāyaṇaḥ paramaḥ ca avyayaḥ ca madhyam ca asya jagataḥ tasthuṣaḥ ca sarveṣām bhūtānām prabhavaḥ ca apyayaḥ ca yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca brūhi brāhmaṇa pūjāyām vyuṣṭim tvam madhusūdana vāsudevaḥ uvāca śṛṇuṣva avahitaḥ rājan dvijānām bharata ṛṣabha kim phalam brāhmaṇeṣu asti pūjāyām madhusūdana sadā dvijātīn saṃpūjya kim phalam tatra mānada etat brūhi pitar sarvam su mahān saṃśayaḥ atra me pratyabruvam mahā rāja yat tat śṛṇu samāhitaḥ vyuṣṭim brāhmaṇa pūjāyām raukmiṇeya nibodha me ete hi soma rājānaḥ īśvarāḥ sukha duḥkhayoḥ brāhmaṇa pramukham saukhyam na me atra asti vicāraṇā brāhmaṇa pramukham vīryam āyuḥ kīrtiḥ yaśaḥ balam lokāḥ loka īśvarāḥ ca eva sarve brāhmaṇa pūrvakāḥ tat katham na ādriyeyam vai īśvaraḥ asmi iti putraka anyān api sṛjeyuḥ ca lokān loka īśvarān tathā katham teṣu na varteya samyak jñānāt su tejasaḥ avasat mad gṛhe tāta brāhmaṇaḥ hari piṅgalaḥ cīra vāsāḥ bilva daṇḍī dīrgha śmaśru nakha ādimān dīrghebhyaḥ ca manuṣyebhyaḥ pramāṇāt adhikaḥ bhuvi sa sma saṃcarate lokān ye divyāḥ ye ca mānuṣāḥ imāḥ gāthāḥ gāyamānaḥ catvareṣu sabhāsu ca durvāsasam vāsayet kaḥ brāhmaṇam satkṛtam gṛhe paribhāṣām ca me śrutvā kaḥ nu dadyāt pratiśrayam yaḥ mām kaḥ cit vāsayeta na sa mām kopayet iha sa sma bhuṅkte sahasrāṇām bahūnām annam ekadā ekadā sma alpakam bhuṅkte na vā eti ca punar gṛhān na ca asya vayasā tulyaḥ pṛthivyām abhavat tadā saḥ asmad āvasatham gatvā śayyāḥ ca āstaraṇāni ca kanyāḥ ca alaṃkṛtāḥ dagdhvā tatas vyapagataḥ svayam atha mām abravīt bhūyas sa muniḥ saṃśita vrataḥ kṛṣṇa pāyasam icchāmi bhoktum iti eva sa tvaraḥ sarvāṇi eva anna pānāni bhakṣyāḥ ca uccāvacāḥ tathā a vimṛśya eva ca tatas kṛtavān asmi tat tathā tena ucchiṣṭena gātrāṇi śiraḥ ca eva abhyamṛkṣayam sa dadarśa tadā abhyāśe mātaram te śubha ānanām muniḥ pāyasa digdha aṅgīm rathe tūrṇam ayojayat pratodena ātudat bālām rukmiṇīm mama paśyataḥ na ca me stokam api āsīt duḥkham īrṣyā kṛtam tadā tatas sa rājamārgeṇa mahatā niryayau bahis tat dṛṣṭvā mahat āścaryam dāśārhāḥ jāta manyavaḥ brāhmaṇāḥ eva jāyeran na anyaḥ varṇaḥ katham cana kaḥ hi enam ratham āsthāya jīvet anyaḥ pumān iha āśīviṣa viṣam tīkṣṇam tatas tīkṣṇataram viṣam brahma āśīviṣa dagdhasya na asti kaḥ cit cikitsakaḥ tām nā amarṣayata śrīmān tatas tūrṇam acodayat padātiḥ utpathena eva prādhāvat dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ jitaḥ krodhaḥ tvayā kṛṣṇa prakṛtyā eva mahā bhuja prītaḥ asmi tava govinda vṛṇu kāmān yathā īpsitān yāvat eva manuṣyāṇām anne bhāvaḥ bhaviṣyati yathā eva anne tathā teṣām tvayi bhāvaḥ bhaviṣyati yāvat ca puṇyā lokeṣu tvayi kīrtiḥ bhaviṣyati triṣu lokeṣu tāvat ca vaiśiṣṭyam pratipatsyase sarvam tathā eva draṣṭāsi viśiṣṭam vā janārdana atas mṛtyu bhayam nā asti yāvat icchā tava acyuta iti uktaḥ aham śarīram svam apaśyam śrī samāyutam rukmiṇīm ca abravīt prītaḥ sarva strīṇām varam yaśaḥ kīrtim ca anuttamām loke samavāpsyasi śobhane na tvām jarā vā rogaḥ vā vaivarṇyam ca api bhāmini sprakṣyanti puṇya gandhā ca kṛṣṇam ārādhayiṣyasi ṣoḍaśānām sahasrāṇām vadhūnām keśavasya ha variṣṭhā saha lokyā ca keśavasya bhaviṣyasi tasmin antarhite ca aham upāṃśu vratam ādiśam yat kim cit brāhmaṇaḥ brūyāt sarvam kuryām iti prabho tatas parama hṛṣṭa ātmā prāviśam gṛham eva ca praviṣṭa mātraḥ ca gṛhe sarvam paśyāmi tat navam tatas aham vismayam prāptaḥ sarvam dṛṣṭvā navam dṛḍham apūjayam ca manasā raukmiṇeya dvijam tadā māhātmyam dvijamukhyasya sarvam ākhyātavān tadā pūjayasva mahābhāgān vāgbhiḥ dānaiḥ ca nityadā evam vyuṣṭim aham prāptaḥ brāhmaṇānām prasāda jām yat ca mām āha bhīṣmaḥ ayam tat satyam bharata ṛṣabha yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca durvāsasaḥ prasādāt te yat tadā madhusūdana avāptam iha vijñānam tat me vyākhyātum arhasi mahābhāgyam ca yat tasya nāmāni ca mahātmanaḥ tattvataḥ jñātum icchāmi sarvam matimatām vara vāsudevaḥ uvāca yat avāptam mahā rāja śreyaḥ yat ca arjitam yaśaḥ prayataḥ prātar utthāya yat adhīye viśām pate prāñjaliḥ śatarudrīyam tat me nigadataḥ śṛṇu śaṃkaraḥ tu asṛjat tāta prajāḥ sthāvara jaṅgamāḥ na asti kim cit param bhūtam mahādevāt viśām pate iha triṣu api lokeṣu bhūtānām prabhavaḥ hi saḥ visaṃjñāḥ hata bhūyiṣṭhāḥ vepanti ca patanti ca śrutvā vidīryet hṛdayam devānām api saṃyuge yān ca ghoreṇa rūpeṇa paśyet kruddhaḥ pinākadhṛk na surāḥ na asurāḥ loke na gandharvāḥ na pannagāḥ dhanuṣā bāṇam utsṛjya sa ghoṣam vinanāda ca te na śarma kutas śāntim viṣādam lebhire surāḥ tena jyā tala ghoṣeṇa sarve lokāḥ samākulāḥ babhūvuḥ avaśāḥ pārtha viṣeduḥ ca sura asurāḥ andhena tamasā lokāḥ prāvṛtāḥ na cakāśire pranaṣṭā jyotiṣām bhās ca saha sūryeṇa bhārata bhṛśam bhītāḥ tatas śāntim cakruḥ svastyayanāni ca ṛṣayaḥ sarva bhūtānām ātmanaḥ ca hita eṣiṇaḥ pūṣāṇam ca abhidudrāva pareṇa vapuṣā anvitaḥ puroḍāśam bhakṣayataḥ daśanān vai vyaśātayat tatas praṇemuḥ devāḥ te vepamānāḥ sma śaṃkaram punar ca saṃdadhe rudraḥ dīptam su niśitam śaram rudrasya vikramam dṛṣṭvā bhītāḥ devāḥ saha ṛṣibhiḥ tatas prasādayām āsuḥ śarvam te vibudha uttamāḥ jepuḥ ca śatarudrīyam devāḥ kṛtvā añjalim tatas saṃstūyamānaḥ tridaśaiḥ prasasāda maheśvaraḥ rudrasya bhāgam yajñe ca viśiṣṭam te tu akalpayan bhayena tridaśāḥ rājan śaraṇam ca prapedire asurāṇām purāṇi āsan trīṇi vīryavatām divi āyasam rājatam ca eva sauvarṇam aparam tathā nā aśakat tāni maghavā bhettum sarva āyudhaiḥ api atha sarve amarāḥ rudram jagmuḥ śaraṇam arditāḥ tatas ūcuḥ mahātmānaḥ devāḥ sarve samāgatāḥ sa tathā uktaḥ tathā iti uktvā viṣṇum kṛtvā śara uttamam śalyam agnim tathā kṛtvā puṅkham vaivasvatam yamam vedān kṛtvā dhanuḥ sarvān jyām ca sāvitrim uttamām devān ratha varam kṛtvā viniyujya ca sarvaśas śareṇa āditya varṇena kālāgni sama tejasā te asurāḥ sa purāḥ tatra dagdhāḥ rudreṇa bhārata tam ca eva aṅka gatam dṛṣṭvā bālam pañcaśikham punar umā jijñāsamānā vai kaḥ ayam iti abravīt tadā asūyataḥ ca śakrasya vajreṇa prahariṣyataḥ ayam śreṣṭhaḥ iti jñātvā vavande tam umāpatim tatas prasādayām āsuḥ umām rudram ca te surāḥ sa ca api brāhmaṇaḥ bhūtvā durvāsāḥ nāma vīryavān dvāravatyām mama gṛhe ciram kālam upāvasat tān udāra tayā ca aham akṣamam tasya duḥsaham sa candramāḥ sa ca īśānaḥ sa sūryaḥ varuṇaḥ ca saḥ sa kālaḥ saḥ antakaḥ mṛtyuḥ sa tamaḥ rātri ahāni ca māsa ardha māsāḥ ṛtavaḥ saṃdhye saṃvatsaraḥ ca saḥ sa dhātā sa vidhātā ca viśva karmā sa sarva vid nakṣatrāṇi diśaḥ ca eva pradiśaḥ atha grahāḥ tathā īdṛśaḥ sa mahādevaḥ bhūyas ca bhagavān atas na hi śakyāḥ guṇāḥ vaktum api varṣa śataiḥ api vāsudevaḥ uvāca yudhiṣṭhira mahā bāho mahā bhāgyam mahātmanaḥ vadanti agnim mahādevam tathā sthāṇum maheśvaram eka akṣam tryambakam ca eva viśvarūpam śivam tathā dve tanū tasya devasya veda jñāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ viduḥ ghorām anyām śivām anyām te tanū bahudhā punar śivā saumyā ca yā tasya dharmaḥ tu āpaḥ atha candramāḥ brahmacaryam carati eṣa śivā yā asya tanuḥ tathā īśvara tvāt mahat tvāt ca maheśvaraḥ iti smṛtaḥ devānām su mahān yat ca yat ca asya viṣayaḥ mahān yat ca viśvam mahat pāti mahādevaḥ tatas smṛtaḥ śivam icchan manuṣyāṇām tasmāt eṣa śivaḥ smṛtaḥ sthira liṅgaḥ ca yat nityam tasmāt sthāṇuḥ iti smṛtaḥ yat asya bahudhā rūpam bhūtam bhavyam bhavat tathā sthāvaram jaṅgamam ca eva bahurūpaḥ tatas smṛtaḥ dhūmram rūpam ca yat tasya dhūrjaṭī iti atas ucyate viśve devāḥ ca yat tasmin viśvarūpaḥ tatas smṛtaḥ sahasrākṣaḥ ayuta akṣaḥ vā sarvata ukṣi mayaḥ api vā cakṣuṣaḥ prabhavaḥ tejaḥ na asti antaḥ atha asya cakṣuṣām sarvathā yat paśūn pāti taiḥ ca yat ramate punar teṣām adhipatiḥ yat ca tasmāt paśupatiḥ smṛtaḥ vigraham pūjayet yaḥ vai liṅgam vā api mahātmanaḥ liṅgam pūjayitā nityam mahatīm śriyam aśnute ṛṣayaḥ ca api devāḥ ca gandharva apsarasaḥ tathā sukham dadāti prīta ātmā bhaktānām bhakta vatsalaḥ eṣaḥ eva śmaśāneṣu devaḥ vasati nityaśas yajante tam janāḥ tatra vīrasthāna niṣeviṇam viṣama sthaḥ śarīreṣu sa mṛtyuḥ prāṇinām iha sa ca vāyuḥ śarīreṣu prāṇaḥ apānaḥ śarīriṇām tasya ghorāṇi rūpāṇi dīptāni ca bahūni ca nāmadheyāni vedeṣu bahūni asya yathārthataḥ vyāsāt anantaram yat ca api upasthānam mahātmanaḥ pradātā sarva lokānām viśvam ca api ucyate mahat jyeṣṭha bhūtam vadanti enam brāhmaṇāḥ ṛṣayaḥ apare prathamaḥ hi eṣa devānām mukhāt agniḥ ajāyata grahaiḥ bahuvidhaiḥ prāṇān saṃruddhān utsṛjati api sa mocayati puṇya ātmā śaraṇyaḥ śaraṇa āgatān āyuḥ ārogyam aiśvaryam vittam kāmān ca puṣkalān sa dadāti manuṣyebhyaḥ saḥ eva ākṣipate punar aiśvaryāt ca eva kāmānām īśvaraḥ punar ucyate maheśvaraḥ ca lokānām mahatām īśvaraḥ ca saḥ vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ uvāca bhīṣmam śāṃtanavam bhūyas paryapṛcchat yudhiṣṭhiraḥ nirṇaye vā mahābuddhe sarva dharma bhṛtām vara pratyakṣam āgamaḥ vā iti kim tayoḥ kāraṇam bhavet bhīṣmaḥ uvāca na asti atra saṃśayaḥ kaḥ cit iti me vartate matiḥ śṛṇu vakṣyāmi te prājña samyak tvam anupṛcchasi dṛṣṭam śrutam anantam hi yatra saṃśaya darśanam pratyakṣam kāraṇam dṛṣṭam hetukāḥ prājña māninaḥ tat ayuktam vyavasyanti bālāḥ paṇḍita māninaḥ śakyam dīrgheṇa kālena yuktena atandritena ca prāṇayātrām anekām ca kalpayānena bhārata tatpareṇa eva na anyena śakyam hi etat tu kāraṇam hetūnām antam āsādya vipulam jñānam uttamam yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca pratyakṣam lokataḥ siddham lokāḥ ca āgama pūrvakāḥ śiṣṭa ācāraḥ bahuvidhaḥ brūhi tat me pitāmaha bhīṣmaḥ uvāca adharmāḥ dharma rūpeṇa tṛṇaiḥ kūpāḥ iva āvṛtāḥ tatas taiḥ bhidyate vṛttam śṛṇu ca eva yudhiṣṭhira avṛttyā ye ca bhindanti śruta tyāga parāyaṇāḥ dharma vidveṣiṇaḥ mandāḥ iti uktaḥ teṣu saṃśayaḥ atṛpyantaḥ tu sādhūnām ye eva āgama buddhayaḥ param iti eva saṃtuṣṭāḥ tān upāssva ca pṛccha ca kāma arthau pṛṣṭhatas kṛtvā lobha moha anusāriṇau na teṣām bhidyate vṛttam yajña svādhyāya karmabhiḥ ācāraḥ kāraṇam ca eva dharmaḥ ca eva trayam punar yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca apāre mārgamāṇasya param tīram a paśyataḥ vedāḥ pratyakṣam ācāraḥ pramāṇam tat trayam yadi bhīṣmaḥ uvāca yadi evam manyase rājan tridhā dharma vicāraṇā uktaḥ mārgaḥ trayāṇām ca tat tathā eva samācara jijñāsā tu na kartavyā dharmasya paritarkaṇāt sadā eva bharata śreṣṭha mā te bhūt atra saṃśayaḥ andhaḥ jaḍaḥ iva āśaṅkaḥ yat bravīmi tat ācara brāhmaṇeṣu ca vṛttiḥ yā pitṛpaitāmaha ucitā tām anvehi mahā bāho svargasya ete hi deśikāḥ pramāṇam apramāṇam vai yaḥ kuryāt abudhaḥ naraḥ eteṣu eva tu ime lokāḥ kṛtsnāḥ iti nibodha tān yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca bravītu bhagavān etat kva te gacchanti tādṛśāḥ bhīṣmaḥ uvāca dharme eva ratiḥ teṣām ācārya upāsanāt bhavet manuṣyāḥ yadi vā devāḥ śarīram upatāpya vai prathamam brahmaṇaḥ putram dharmam āhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ dharmiṇaḥ paryupāsante phalam pakvam iva āśayaḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca asatām kīdṛśam rūpam sādhavaḥ kim ca kurvate bravītu me bhavān etat santaḥ asantaḥ ca kīdṛśāḥ bhīṣmaḥ uvāca durācārāḥ ca durdharṣāḥ durmukhāḥ ca api asādhavaḥ sādhavaḥ śīla saṃpannāḥ śiṣṭa ācārasya lakṣaṇam rājamārge gavām madhye goṣṭha madhye ca dharmiṇaḥ na upasevanti rāja indra sargam mūtra purīṣayoḥ pañcānām aśanam dattvā śeṣam aśnanti sādhavaḥ na jalpanti ca bhuñjānāḥ na nidrānti ārdra pāṇayaḥ citra bhānum anaḍvāham devam goṣṭham catuṣpatham brāhmaṇam dhārmikam caityam te kurvanti pradakṣiṇam vṛddhānām bhāra taptānām strīṇām bāla āturasya ca brāhmaṇānām gavām rājñām panthānam dadate ca te atithīnām ca sarveṣām preṣyāṇām sva janasya ca tathā śaraṇa kāmānām goptā syāt svāgata pradaḥ sāyam prātar manuṣyāṇām aśanam deva nirmitam na antarā bhojanam dṛṣṭam upavāsa vidhiḥ hi saḥ homa kāle yathā vahniḥ kālam eva pratīkṣate ṛtu kāle tathā nārī ṛtum eva pratīkṣate amṛtam brāhmaṇāḥ gāvaḥ iti etat trayam ekatas yajuṣā saṃskṛtam māṃsam upabhuñjan na duṣyati pṛṣṭha māṃsam vṛthāmāṃsam putra māṃsam ca tat samam karma vai saphalam kṛtvā gurūṇām pratipādayet gurūn abhyarcya vardhante āyuṣā yaśasā śriyā vṛddhān na ativadet jātu na ca saṃpreṣayet api na āsīnaḥ syāt sthiteṣu evam āyuḥ asya na riṣyate na nagnām īkṣate nārīm na vidvān puruṣān api maithunam satatam guptam āhāram ca samācaret tīrthānām guravaḥ tīrtham śucīnām hṛdayam śuci darśanānām param jñānam saṃtoṣaḥ paramam sukham sāyam prātar ca vṛddhānām śṛṇuyāt puṣkalāḥ giraḥ śrutam āpnoti hi naraḥ satatam vṛddha sevayā svādhyāye bhojane ca eva dakṣiṇam pāṇim uddharet yacchet vāc manasī nityam indriyāṇām ca vibhramam saṃskṛtam pāyasam nityam yavāgūm kṛsaram haviḥ aṣṭakāḥ pitṛ daivatyāḥ vṛddhānām abhipūjanam śmaśrukarmaṇi maṅgalyam kṣutānām abhinandanam vyādhitānām ca sarveṣām āyuṣaḥ pratinandanam avarāṇām samānānām śiṣyāṇām ca samācaret pāpam ācakṣate nityam hṛdayam pāpa karmiṇām jñāna pūrvam vinaśyanti gūhamānāḥ mahājane jñāna pūrvam kṛtam karma chādayante hi asādhavaḥ na mām manuṣyāḥ paśyanti na mām paśyanti devatāḥ pāpena abhihataḥ pāpaḥ pāpam eva abhijāyate yathā vārdhuṣikaḥ vṛddhim dehabhede pratīkṣate prāyaścitta hatam pāpam tathā sadyas praṇaśyati tasmāt pāpam na gūheta gūhamānam vivardhate kṛtvā tu sādhuṣu ākhyeyam te tat praśamayanti uta āśayā saṃcitam dravyam yat kāle na upabhujyate mānasam sarva bhūtānām dharmam āhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ tasmāt sarvāṇi bhūtāni dharmam eva samāsate nidhim nidadhyāt pāratryam yātrā artham dāna śabditam yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca na abhāgadheyaḥ prāpnoti dhanam su balavān api bhāgadheya anvitaḥ tu arthān kṛśaḥ bālaḥ ca vindati kṛta yatna aphalāḥ ca eva dṛśyante śataśas narāḥ na a labhyam ca upalabhyeta nṛṇām bharata sattama yadā prayatnam kṛtavān dṛśyate hi aphalaḥ naraḥ mārgan naya śataiḥ arthān a mārgan ca aparaḥ sukhī akāryam asakṛt kṛtvā dṛśyante hi adhanāḥ narāḥ dhana yuktāḥ tu adharma sthāḥ dṛśyante ca apare janāḥ adhītya nītim yasmāt ca nīti yuktaḥ na dṛśyate anabhijñaḥ ca sācivyam gamitaḥ kena hetunā yadi vidyām upāśritya naraḥ sukham avāpnuyāt na vidvān vidyayā hīnam vṛtti artham upasaṃśrayet yathā pipāsām jayati puruṣaḥ prāpya vai jalam dṛṣṭa arthaḥ vidyayā api evam avidyām prajahet naraḥ na aprāpta kālaḥ mriyate viddhaḥ śara śataiḥ api tṛṇa agreṇa api saṃspṛṣṭaḥ prāpta kālaḥ na jīvati bhīṣmaḥ uvāca īhamānaḥ samārambhān yadi na āsādayet dhanam dānena bhogī bhavati medhāvī vṛddha sevayā ahiṃsayā ca dīrgha āyuḥ iti prāhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ tasmāt dadyāt na yāceta pūjayet dhārmikān api su ābhāṣī priya kṛt śuddhaḥ sarva sattva a vihiṃsakaḥ yadā pramāṇa prabhavaḥ svabhāvaḥ ca sukha asukhe maśa kīṭa pipīlānām sthiraḥ bhava yudhiṣṭhira bhīṣmaḥ uvāca tatra āśvasīta satkṛtvā a satkṛtvā na viśvaset buddhim āviśya bhūtānām dharma artheṣu pravartate tadā āśvasīta dharma ātma adṛḍha buddhiḥ na viśvaset etāvat mātram etat hi bhūtānām prājña lakṣaṇam yathā hi upasthita aiśvaryāḥ pūjayante narāḥ narān evam eva ātmanā ātmānam pūjayanti iha dhārmikāḥ tasmāt viśuddham ātmānam jānīyāt dharma cāriṇam trayāṇām api lokānām āloka karaṇaḥ bhavet yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca vipāpmā ca bhavet kena kim vā kalmaṣa nāśanam bhīṣmaḥ uvāca ayam daivata vaṃśaḥ vai ṛṣi vaṃśa samanvitaḥ dvi saṃdhyam paṭhitaḥ putra kalmaṣa apaharaḥ paraḥ pitāmahaḥ jagannāthaḥ sāvitrī brahmaṇaḥ satī veda bhūḥ atha kartā ca viṣṇuḥ nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ umāpatiḥ virūpākṣaḥ skandaḥ senāpatiḥ tathā śakraḥ śacīpatiḥ devaḥ yamaḥ dhūmorṇayā saha varuṇaḥ saha gauryā ca saha ṛddhyā dhaneśvaraḥ saumyā gauḥ surabhiḥ devī viśravāḥ ca mahān ṛṣiḥ ṣaṣ kālaḥ sāgaraḥ gaṅgā sravantyaḥ atha marut gaṇāḥ vālakhilyāḥ tapaḥsiddhāḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ tathā nāradaḥ parvataḥ ca eva viśvāvasuḥ hahā huhūḥ tumbaruḥ citrasenaḥ ca deva dūtaḥ ca viśrutaḥ deva kanyāḥ mahābhāgāḥ divyāḥ ca apsarasām gaṇāḥ urvaśī menakā rambhā miśrakeśī alambuṣā viśvācī ca ghṛtācī ca pañcacūḍā tilottamā ādityāḥ vasavaḥ rudrāḥ sa aśvinaḥ pitaraḥ api ca dharmaḥ satyam tapaḥ dīkṣā vyavasāyaḥ pitāmahaḥ śarvaryaḥ divasāḥ ca eva mārīcaḥ kaśyapaḥ tathā śukraḥ bṛhaspatiḥ bhaumaḥ budhaḥ rāhuḥ śanaiścaraḥ nakṣatrāṇi ṛtavaḥ ca eva māsāḥ saṃdhyāḥ sa vatsarāḥ vainateyāḥ samudrāḥ ca kadru jāḥ pannagāḥ tathā śatadrūḥ ca vipāśā ca candrabhāgā sarasvatī gaṅgā mahānadī ca eva kapilā narmadā tathā kampunā ca viśalyā ca karatoyā ambuvāhinī sarayūḥ gaṇḍakī ca eva lohityaḥ ca mahā nadaḥ godāvarī ca veṇṇā ca kṛṣṇaveṇā tathā adrijā dṛṣadvatī ca kāverī vaṃkṣuḥ mandākinī tathā prayāgam ca prabhāsam ca puṇyam naimiṣam eva ca puṇya tīrthaiḥ ca kalilam kurukṣetram prakīrtitam sindhūttamam tapodānam jambūmārgam atha api ca hiraṇvatī vitastā ca tathā evā ikṣumatī nadī bhūmi bhāgāḥ tathā puṇyāḥ gaṅgādvāram atha api ca ṛṣikulyāḥ tathā medhyā nadī citrapathā tathā kauśikī yamunā sītā tathā carmaṇvatī nadī nadī bhīmarathī ca eva bāhudā ca mahā nadī mahendravāṇī tridivā nīlikā ca sarasvatī nandā ca aparanandā ca tathā tīrtham mahāhradam gayā atha phalgutīrtham ca dharmāraṇyam suraiḥ vṛtam puṇyam triloka vikhyātam sarva pāpa haram śivam vindhyaḥ dhātu vicitra aṅgaḥ tīrthavān auṣadha anvitaḥ śṛṅgavān mandaraḥ nīlaḥ niṣadhaḥ darduraḥ tathā citrakūṭaḥ añjana ābhaḥ ca parvataḥ gandhamādanaḥ puṇyaḥ somagiriḥ ca eva tathā eva anye mahīdharāḥ diśaḥ ca vidiśaḥ ca eva kṣitiḥ sarve mahīruhāḥ viśvedevāḥ nabhaḥ ca eva nakṣatrāṇi grahāḥ tathā pāntu vaḥ satatam devāḥ kīrtitā a kīrtitā mayā devatā anantaram viprān tapaḥ siddhān tapaḥ dhikān kīrtitān kīrtayiṣyāmi sarva pāpa pramocanān yavakrītaḥ atha raibhyaḥ ca kakṣīvān auśijaḥ tathā bhṛgvaṅgirāḥ tathā kaṇvaḥ medhātithiḥ atha prabhuḥ barhī ca guṇa saṃpannaḥ prācīm diśam upāśritāḥ bhadrām diśam mahābhāgāḥ ulmucuḥ pramucuḥ tathā mumucuḥ ca mahābhāgaḥ svastyātreyaḥ ca vīryavān mitrāvaruṇayoḥ putraḥ tathā agastyaḥ pratāpavān dṛḍhāyuḥ ca ūrdhvabāhuḥ ca viśrutau ṛṣi sattamau paścimām diśam āśritya ye edhante nibodha tān uṣadguḥ saha sodaryaiḥ parivyādhaḥ ca vīryavān ṛṣiḥ dīrghatamāḥ ca eva gautamaḥ kaśyapaḥ tathā atreḥ putraḥ ca dharma ātmā tathā sārasvataḥ prabhuḥ uttarām diśam āśritya ye edhante nibodha tān atriḥ vasiṣṭhaḥ śaktiḥ ca pārāśaryaḥ ca vīryavān ṛcīka pautraḥ rāmaḥ ca ṛṣiḥ auddālakiḥ tathā lomaśaḥ nāciketaḥ ca lomaharṣaṇaḥ eva ca ṛṣiḥ ugraśravāḥ ca eva bhārgavaḥ cyavanaḥ tathā ādyaḥ prakīrtitaḥ rājan sarva pāpa pramocanaḥ nṛgaḥ yayātiḥ nahuṣaḥ yaduḥ pūruḥ ca vīryavān dhundhumāraḥ dilīpaḥ ca sagaraḥ ca pratāpavān kṛśāśvaḥ yauvanāśvaḥ ca citrāśvaḥ satyavān tathā duḥṣantaḥ bharataḥ ca eva cakravartī mahā yaśāḥ yavanaḥ janakaḥ ca eva tathā dṛḍharathaḥ nṛpaḥ rāmaḥ rākṣasa hā vīraḥ śaśabinduḥ bhagīrathaḥ karaṃdhamaḥ nara śreṣṭhaḥ kadhmoraḥ ca nara adhipaḥ dakṣaḥ ambarīṣaḥ kukuraḥ ravataḥ ca mahā yaśāḥ mucukundaḥ ca rājarṣiḥ mitrabhānuḥ priyaṃkaraḥ trasadasyuḥ tathā rājā śvetaḥ rāja ṛṣi sattamaḥ mahābhiṣaḥ ca vikhyātaḥ nimi rājaḥ tathā aṣṭakaḥ āyuḥ kṣupaḥ ca rājarṣiḥ kakṣeyuḥ ca nara adhipaḥ śibiḥ auśīnaraḥ ca eva gayaḥ ca eva nara adhipaḥ pratardanaḥ divodāsaḥ saudāsaḥ kosala īśvaraḥ ailaḥ nalaḥ ca rājarṣiḥ manuḥ ca eva prajāpatiḥ havidhraḥ ca pṛṣadhraḥ ca pratīpaḥ śaṃtanuḥ tathā kakṣasenaḥ ca rājarṣiḥ ye ca anye na anukīrtitāḥ mā vighnam mā ca me pāpam mā ca me paripanthinaḥ vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ uvāca tūṣṇīṃbhūte tadā bhīṣme paṭe citram iva arpitam muhūrtam iva ca dhyātvā vyāsaḥ satyavatī sutaḥ nṛpam śayānam gāṅgeyam idam āha vacaḥ tadā rājan prakṛtim āpannaḥ kururājaḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ sahitaḥ bhrātṛbhiḥ sarvaiḥ pārthivaiḥ ca anuyāyibhiḥ upāste tvām nara vyāghra saha kṛṣṇena dhīmatā yudhiṣṭhiram saha amātyam anujajñe nadī sutaḥ uvāca ca enam madhuram tatas śāṃtanavaḥ nṛpaḥ yayātiḥ iva rāja indra śraddhā dama puraḥsaraḥ kṣatra dharma rataḥ pārtha pitṝn devān ca tarpaya rañjayasva prajāḥ sarvāḥ prakṛtīḥ parisāntvaya anu tvām tāta jīvantu mitrāṇi suhṛdaḥ tathā caitya sthāne sthitam vṛkṣam phalavantam iva dvijāḥ dhṛtarāṣṭram puraskṛtya gāndhārīm ca pativratām saha taiḥ ṛṣibhiḥ sarvaiḥ bhrātṛbhiḥ keśavena ca praviveśa kuruśreṣṭha puram vāraṇasāhvayam vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ uvāca tatas kuntī sutaḥ rājā paura jānapadam janam pūjayitvā yathānyāyam anujajñe gṛhān prati sāntvayām āsa nārīḥ ca hata vīrāḥ hata īśvarāḥ vipulaiḥ artha dānaiḥ ca tadā pāṇḍu sutaḥ nṛpaḥ saḥ abhiṣiktaḥ mahā prājñaḥ prāpya rājyam yudhiṣṭhiraḥ avasthāpya nara śreṣṭhaḥ sarvāḥ sva prakṛtīḥ tadā pratigṛhya āśiṣaḥ mukhyāḥ tadā dharma bhṛtām varaḥ uṣitvā śarvarīḥ śrīmān pañcāśat nagara uttame dṛṣṭvā nivṛttam ādityam pravṛttam ca uttarāyaṇam ghṛtam mālyam ca gandhān ca kṣaumāṇi ca yudhiṣṭhiraḥ candana agaru mukhyāni tathā kāla agarūṇi ca prasthāpya pūrvam kaunteyaḥ bhīṣma saṃsādhanāya vai mālyāni ca mahārhāṇi ratnāni vividhāni ca dhṛtarāṣṭram puraskṛtya gāndhārīm ca yaśasvinīm mātaram ca pṛthām dhīmān bhrātṝn ca puruṣa ṛṣabhaḥ mahatā rāja bhogyena paribarheṇa saṃvṛtaḥ stūyamānaḥ mahā rāja bhīṣmasya agnīn anuvrajan niścakrāma purāt tasmāt yathā devapatiḥ tathā āsasāda kurukṣetre tatas śāṃtanavam nṛpam upāsyamānam vyāsena pārāśaryeṇa dhīmatā hata śiṣṭaiḥ nṛpaiḥ ca anyaiḥ nānā deśa samāgataiḥ rakṣibhiḥ ca mahātmānam rakṣyamāṇam samantataḥ śayānam vīra śayane dadarśa nṛpatiḥ tatas tatas rathāt avārohat bhrātṛbhiḥ saha dharmarāj dvaipāyana ādīn viprān ca taiḥ ca pratyabhinanditaḥ ṛtvigbhiḥ brahma kalpaiḥ ca bhrātṛbhiḥ ca saha acyutaḥ āsādya śara talpa stham ṛṣibhiḥ parivāritam abravīt bharata śreṣṭham dharmarājaḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ bhrātṛbhiḥ saha kauravya śayānam nimnagā sutam yudhiṣṭhiraḥ aham nṛpate namaḥ te jāhnavī suta śṛṇoṣi ced mahā bāho brūhi kim karavāṇi te ācāryāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ ca eva ṛtvijaḥ bhrātaraḥ ca me putraḥ ca te mahā tejāḥ dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ janeśvaraḥ upasthitaḥ saha amātyaḥ vāsudevaḥ ca vīryavān hata śiṣṭāḥ ca rājānaḥ sarve ca kurujāṅgalāḥ tān paśya kuru śārdūla samunmīlaya locane evam uktaḥ tu gāṅgeyaḥ kuntī putreṇa dhīmatā dadarśa bhāratān sarvān sthitān saṃparivārya tam diṣṭyā prāptaḥ asi kaunteya saha amātyaḥ yudhiṣṭhira parivṛttaḥ hi bhagavān sahasrāṃśuḥ divākaraḥ aṣṭa pañcāśatam rātryaḥ śayānasya adya me gatāḥ śareṣu niśita agreṣu yathā varṣa śatam tathā māghaḥ ayam samanuprāptaḥ māsaḥ puṇyaḥ yudhiṣṭhira tri bhāga śeṣaḥ pakṣaḥ ayam śuklaḥ bhavitum arhati dhṛtarāṣṭram atha āmantrya kāle vacanam abravīt rājan vidita dharmaḥ asi su nirṇīta artha saṃśayaḥ bahu śrutāḥ hi te viprāḥ bahavaḥ paryupāsitāḥ veda śāstrāṇi sarvāṇi dharmān ca manuja īśvara vedān ca caturaḥ sa aṅgān nikhilena avabudhyase śrutam deva rahasyam te kṛṣṇadvaipāyanāt api yathā pāṇḍoḥ sutāḥ rājan tathā eva tava dharmataḥ tān pālaya sthitaḥ dharme guru śuśrūṣaṇe ratān dharmarājaḥ hi śuddha ātmā nideśe sthāsyate tava ānṛśaṃsya param hi enam jānāmi guru vatsalam tava putrāḥ durātmānaḥ krodha lobha parāyaṇāḥ īrṣyā abhibhūtāḥ durvṛttāḥ tān na śocitum arhasi vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ uvāca etāvat uktvā vacanam dhṛtarāṣṭram manīṣiṇam vāsudevam mahā bāhum abhyabhāṣata kauravaḥ anujānīhi mām kṛṣṇa vaikuṇṭha puruṣottama rakṣyāḥ ca te pāṇḍaveyāḥ bhavān hi eṣām parāyaṇam vāsudevena tīrthena putra saṃśāmya pāṇḍavaiḥ saṃdhānasya paraḥ kālaḥ tava iti ca punar punar na ca me tat vacaḥ mūḍhaḥ kṛtavān sa su manda dhīḥ ghātayitvā iha pṛthivīm tatas sa nidhanam gataḥ tvām ca jānāmi aham vīra purāṇam ṛṣi sattamam nareṇa sahitam devam badaryām su cira uṣitam tathā me nāradaḥ prāha vyāsaḥ ca su mahā tapāḥ nara nārāyaṇau etau saṃbhūtau manujeṣu iti vāsudevaḥ uvāca anujānāmi bhīṣma tvām vasūn āpnuhi pārthiva na te asti vṛjinam kim cit mayā dṛṣṭam mahā dyute pitṛ bhaktaḥ asi rājarṣe mārkaṇḍeyaḥ iva aparaḥ vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ uvāca evam uktaḥ tu gāṅgeyaḥ pāṇḍavān idam abravīt dhṛtarāṣṭra mukhān ca api sarvān sa suhṛdaḥ tathā prāṇān utsraṣṭum icchāmi tat mā anujñātum arhatha ānṛśaṃsya paraiḥ bhāvyam sadā eva niyata ātmabhiḥ brahmaṇyaiḥ dharma śīlaiḥ ca ca bhārata punar evā bravīt dhīmān yudhiṣṭhiram idam vacaḥ brāhmaṇāḥ ca eva te nityam prājñāḥ ca eva viśeṣataḥ ācāryāḥ ṛtvijaḥ ca eva pūjanīyāḥ narādhipa vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ uvāca evam uktvā kurūn sarvān bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavaḥ tadā tūṣṇīm babhūva kauravyaḥ sa muhūrtam ariṃdama dhārayām āsa ca ātmānam dhāraṇāsu yathākramam tasya ūrdhvam agaman prāṇāḥ saṃniruddhāḥ mahātmanaḥ idam āścaryam āsīt ca madhye teṣām mahātmanām yat yat muñcati gātrāṇām sa śaṃtanu sutaḥ tadā kṣaṇena prekṣatām teṣām viśalyaḥ saḥ abhavat tadā tam dṛṣṭvā vismitāḥ sarve vāsudeva purogamāḥ saṃniruddhaḥ tu tena ātmā sarveṣu āyataneṣu vai mahā ulkā iva ca bhīṣmasya mūrdha deśāt janādhipa niḥsṛtya ākāśam āviśya kṣaṇena antaradhīyata evam sa nṛpa śārdūla nṛpaḥ śāṃtanavaḥ tadā tatas tu ādāya dārūṇi gandhān ca vividhān bahūn citām cakruḥ mahātmānaḥ pāṇḍavāḥ viduraḥ tathā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ tu gāṅgeyam viduraḥ ca mahāmatiḥ uṣṇīṣe paryagṛhṇītām mādrī putrau ubhau tadā tālavṛntāni upādāya paryavījan samantataḥ yājakāḥ juhuvuḥ ca agnim jaguḥ sāmāni sāmagāḥ tatas candana kāṣṭhaiḥ ca tathā kāleyakaiḥ api samavacchādya gāṅgeyam prajvālya ca hutāśanam apasavyam akurvanta dhṛtarāṣṭra mukhāḥ nṛpāḥ saṃskṛtya ca kuru śreṣṭham gāṅgeyam kuru sattamāḥ jagmuḥ bhāgīrathī tīram ṛṣi juṣṭam kuru udvahāḥ kṛṣṇena bharata strībhiḥ ye ca paurāḥ samāgatāḥ vidhivat kṣatriya śreṣṭhāḥ sa ca sarvaḥ janaḥ tadā utthāya salilāt tasmāt rudatī śoka lālasā nibodhata yathāvṛttam ucyamānam mayā anaghāḥ rāja vṛttena saṃpannaḥ prajñayā abhijanena ca satkartā kuru vṛddhānām pitṛ bhaktaḥ dṛḍha vrataḥ jāmadagnyena rāmeṇa purā yaḥ na parājitaḥ divyaiḥ astraiḥ mahā vīryaḥ sa hataḥ adya śikhaṇḍinā aśmasāra mayam nūnam hṛdayam mama pārthivāḥ sametam pārthivam kṣatram kāśi puryām svayaṃvare hatam śikhaṇḍinā śrutvā yat na dīryati me manaḥ pīḍitaḥ na ati yatnena nihataḥ sa śikhaṇḍinā evaṃvidham bahu tadā vilapantīm mahā nadīm āśvāsayām āsa tadā sāmnā dāmodaraḥ vibhuḥ samāśvasihi bhadre tvam mā śucaḥ śubha darśane gataḥ sa paramām siddhim tava putraḥ na saṃśayaḥ vasuḥ eṣa mahā tejāḥ śāpa doṣeṇa śobhane saḥ eṣa kṣatra dharmeṇa yudhyamānaḥ raṇa ajire dhanaṃjayena nihataḥ na eṣa nunnaḥ śikhaṇḍinā bhīṣmam hi kuru śārdūlam udyata iṣum mahā raṇe na śaktaḥ saṃyuge hantum sākṣāt api śatakratuḥ na śaktāḥ syuḥ nihantum hi raṇe tam sarva devatāḥ iti uktā sā tu kṛṣṇena vyāsena ca saridvarā tyaktvā śokam mahā rāja svam vāri avatatāra ha satkṛtya te tām saritam tatas kṛṣṇa mukhāḥ nṛpāḥ anujñātāḥ tayā sarve nyavartanta janādhipāḥ
